Brezila: Mba afaka hitondra fiara raitra ve ny mainty hoditra? ||| Brazil: Can black people drive luxury cars?
Tany amin'ny faran'ny volana Aogositra tany, nipongatra indray noho ny tranga iray nanaitra ny sain'ny maro manerana ny firenena mihitsy ny resaka fanavakavahana sy fitsarana ivelany eo anivon'ny fiarahamonina Breziliana. ||| Towards the end of August the simmering debate about racism and prejudice in Brazilian society was stirred up by a case that has provoked outrage throughout the country.
Januário Alves de Santana, lehilahy mainty hoditra iray eo amin'ny faha-telopolon'ny taonany eo, no voadaroky ny mpiambina roalahy raha iny izy niandry ny vady aman-janany teo amin'ny faritra fametrahana fiara tamina iray amin'irony toeram-pivarotana lehibe iraisampirenena any Brezila irony. ||| Januário Alves de Santana, a black man in his late thirties, was beaten by a couple of security guards as he waited for his wife and children in the car park of one of the largest international retailers in Brazil.
Nampangaina izy ho nikasa hangalatra ny fiara izay azy ihany. ||| He was accused of trying to steal his own car.
Ireo mpanafika azy dia nihevitra mazava fa hoe satria mainty izy dia tsy tokony ho afaka hanjifa Ford EcoSport (karazana iray raisina ho isan'ny lafo vidy any Brezila). ||| The attackers clearly thought that because he was black he wouldn't be able to afford a Ford EcoSport (a model of car considered upmarket in Brazil).
Sary avy amin'i Juarez Silva Jr. ||| Picture by Juarez Silva Jr.
Rachel Glickhouse, avy amin'ny Adventures of a Gringa, dia mamaritra ny fizotry ny zava-nitranga tamin'ny 7 Aogositra amin'ny antsipirihany, araka izay nambaran'i Januário. ||| Rachel Glickhouse, from Adventures of a Gringa, describes the course of events of August 7th in detail, as told by Januário.
Izy dia miblaogy amin'ny teny Anglisy: ||| She blogs in English:
Nijoro teo anilan'ny fiarany izy, voamariny fa nisy lehilahy roa mampiahiahy tamy nanatona azy. ||| Standing outside of the car, he noticed more suspicious men approaching him.
Avy eo ny iray izay mpiandraikitra ny fiambenana ihany nanatona azy sady namoaka fitaovam-piadiana. ||| Then one who was actually a security guard approached him and took out a gun.
Tonga ilehio dia namely an'i Januário tsy nisy alaharo alaharo, ary Januário tsy nahalala akory na jiolahy io na mpitandro filaminana. ||| He attacked Januário without identifying himself, and Januário didn't know if it was a mugger or a cop.
Nandritra ny fifampitoloman'izy ireo, nianjo vonjy ireo mpandalo, ary i Januário dia nihevitra fa avotra izy. ||| While they struggled, passersby called for help, and Januário thought he was saved.
Mpiambina marobe avy ao amin'ny Carrefour no tonga nanatona, ary nazavainy fa resaka tsy mifankahazo izy ity tsy nieritreritra izay hangalatra ilay kodiarandroa teo anila teo izy. ||| Several security guards from Carrefour approached, and he explained that it was a misunderstanding he was not in fact trying to steal the motorcycle nearby.
Nosamborin'ireo mpiambina izy ary nentina niditra tanaty efitrano kely iray hanazava hoe inona no nitranga. ||| The security guards grabbed him and took him inside to a small room to work out what had happened.
Raha izany, hoy izy ireo,  nangalatra EcoSport iray ianao ary avy eo mbola nihevitra ny haka kodiarandroa iray koa? ||| So, they said, you stole an EcoSport and were trying to take a motorcycle, too?
Dia niditra tamin'ny fidarohana tsy ampieritreretana an'i Januário ireo mpiambina dimy, izay nambaran'ny tatitra voalohany ho ampaham-potoana fampijaliana, tehamaina, totohondry, ary vodibasy, daroka amin'ny nifiny ka nahatonga azy ho boba-rà. ||| The five security guards then proceeded to beat Januário senseless, in what the original report called a torture session, hitting, punching, headbutting, and pistol-whipping him, knocking out his teeth and leaving him bleeding heavily.
Januário nilaza fa niezaka ny hanazava ihany ny maha azy ny fiara izy, ary tao anatiny tao ny zanany vavikely raha niantsena ny ankohonany. ||| Januário says he tried to explain that the car was his, and that his baby daughter was inside while his family was shopping.
Tsy niraharaha azy ireo mpanafika azy. ||| His attackers ignored him.
Rehefa tsy hangina ianao, hotapatapahako daholo ny taolam-batanao rehetra hoy ny iray tamin'izy ireo nandrahona. ||| If you don't shut up, I'll break every bone in your body, one of them yelled.
Nikakakaka izy ireo rehefa nisisika izy nilaza fa azy ny fiara. ||| They laughed when he insisted it was his car.
Naharitra roapolo minitra teo ny faharetan'ny daroka talohan'ny nahatongavan'ny pôlisy. ||| The beating lasted around twenty minutes, before the police arrived.
Ary mbola nampiany fa tsy nitsahatra hatreo akory ny fampijaliana, fa na dia taorian'ny nahatongavan'ny pôlisy aza: ||| And she adds that the torture wasn't over yet, even after the arrival of the police:
Iray tamin'ireo pôlisy, antsoina amin'ny anarana hoe Pina, no tsy nino ny tantaran'i Januário. ||| One of the military policemen, by the name of Pina, didn't buy Januário's story.
Sahala amin'ny olona efa nifonja matetika ianao e!. ||| You look like you've been in jail a couple of times.
Alefa moa e, mba miaiky, ao izay an, hoy ilay manamboninahitry ny pôlisy. ||| Come on, fess up, it's ok, the police officer said.
Pôlisy iray hafa no tsy nino ny maha-olona mpisahana fiambenana azy teo aloha, ka dia nanomboka nanadina azy momba ny fitsipika fisahanana fiambenana. ||| Another police officer didn't believe he was a security guard, and started quizzing him about security rules.
Farany, nandeha nankeny amin'ny fiaran'i Januário ilay pôlisy ary nanamarina fa azy sy ny vadiny tokoa ny fiara. ||| Finally, the police went to Januário's car and confirmed it did in fact belong to him and his wife.
Teo ny ankohonany, tohina mafy nahita azy vonton-drà sy vaky nify, ary ilay zanany vavikely mbola resin-tory tao anaty fiara. ||| His family was there, shocked to see him bleeding with cracked teeth, and his daughter was still asleep in the car.
Dia lasa fotsiny tsy niantso fiara mpamonjy voina na nanampy azy ny pôlisy. ||| The police left without offering to send an ambulance or helping him.
Nentin'ny ankohonany tany amin'ny hôpitaly, notsaboina noho ny dona sy ireo ratrany i Januário. ||| Taken to hospital by his family, Januário was treated for shock and lacerations.
Very 8 kilao izy hatreo, misedra tsy fahitan-tory ary tsy mbola afaka miverina mamonjy ny asany. ||| He has since lost 8 kilos, has been suffering from insomnia and has not been able to return to work.
Tamin'ny Alakamisy lasa teo, niatrika fandidiana ho fanitsiana ny taolana tapaka tao amin'ny karandohany izy. ||| Last Thursday, he underwent an operation to correct a bone fracture in his skull.
Nametraka fitoriana ny pôlisy ao an-toerana ny fianakaviany, saingy araka ny filazan'ny pôlisy, ny daroka nahazo azy dia vokatry ny korontana sy  fifanjevoan'ny samy mpividy vitsivitsy. ||| The family has logged a complaint with the local police, but according to the police version, his beating was a result of a disturbance and a fight between a few shoppers.
Carrefour dia namoaka ny fialantsininy noho ilay resaka tsy nifankahazo ary nanambara fa vonona handray anjara amin'ny fanadihadiana. ||| Carrefour has issued a statement expressing its regret at the misunderstanding and saying it will cooperate with the investigations.
Na izany aza, i Januário dia mihevitra ny hitory eo anatrehan'ny fitsarana ilay vondron'orinasam-barotra sy ny Fanjakan'i São Paulo, sy hivarotra ilay fiara, izay mbola aloany R$789 isam-bolana (eo amin'ny $419 eo ho eo), mandritra ny 72 volana. ||| Meanwhile, Januário plans to take both the retail chain and the State of São Paulo to court, and to sell the car, which he is still paying off in R$789 (approximately $419) instalments, spread over a set of 72 instalments.
Nanako nanerana ny firenena ilay tranga, ary maro ny olona naneho firaisankina tamin'i Januário, saingy tsy vao voalohany no nitrangan-javatra toy izao. ||| The case has had repercussions all over the country, with most people sympathizing with Januário, but this is not the first time that something like this has happened.
Araka ny anasongadinan'ny blaogy Censurado, fihetsika maro hafa manohintohina ny mainty hoditra no efa nataon'ireto olona mpiandraikitra fiambenana an'ity vondron'orinasam-barotra ity. ||| As the Censurado blog points out, many other acts of prejudice against black people have been committed by the security personnel of this same retail chain.
Teny maneso no entin'ny mpitoraka blaogy manontany ireo mpamaky: ||| The blogger ironically asks the readers:
Te-hahazo toro-hevitra vitsivitsy avy aminareo mpamaky ahy aho. ||| I want some advice from my readers.
Raha mba te-hividy zavatra aho, shampoo, ambarao, ao amin'ny Carrefour, tokony hitondra namana fotsy hoditra ve aho hiaraka amiko? ||| If I happen to need to buy something, some shampoo, say, in Carrefour, should I take a white friend with me?
Maria Frô mamerina mamoaka ny lahatsoratra momba ilay tantara navoakan'ny AfroPress, sady manampy lohateny lehibe iray miventy ilay bestseller BrezilianaNão Somos Racistas (tsy mpanavakava-bolon-koditra isika) an'ilay mpanao gazety Ali Kamel. ||| Maria Frô replicates the original news story by AfroPress, adding a different headline that paraphrases the Brazilian bestseller Não Somos Racistas (We Are Not Racists) by journalist Ali Kamel.
Ny lohatenin'ny lahatsorany ao amin'ny blaogy dia: ||| The title of her blog post is:
Eny, raha ny lazain'i Kamel, tsy mpanavakava-bolon-koditra isika. ||| Indeed, according to Kamel, we're not racists.
Mpamono olona fotsiny ihany isika. ||| We're just almost murderers.
Ny blaogy Pão e Rosas dia manakiana mafy tokoa ilay tranga. ||| The Pão e Rosas blog vehemently repudiated the case.
Manaraka ny lalan-kevitra iraisana izy ity, miresaka ny anganongano manao hoe ny kolontsain'ny "melting pot" Breziliana dia demokrasia narindra ara-poko: ||| It follows the same line of argument, disputing the myth that cultural "melting pot: Brazil is a harmonious racial democracy:
Raha mbola ny intelligentsia, ireo mpanao pôlitika bevozona sy ny media taka-bahoaka no misisika miteny hoe tsy mpanavakava-bolon-koditra isika, hipongatra foana ny zava-doza toy ity ary haneho amintsika ny fomba fisehon'ny fanavakavahana amin'ny endrika maherisetra sy mampahonena. ||| Whilst the intelligentsia, bourgeois politicians and mass media insist that we are not racists, scandals like this surface and show us how racism manifests itself in many violent and repugnant ways.
Ny fifanoheran-kevitry faratampon'ny demokrasia ara-poko dia mifototra amin'ireo tranga toy ity, ary azontsika tanisaina ireo maro hafa nanohina tamin'ny fotoan'androny nefa dia adino mora foana avy eo, izay maro no tsy nahazo sazy akory. ||| The complete fallacy of racial democracy collapses in cases like this, and we could list many others that caused outrage at the time but were soon forgotten, mostly remaining unpunished.
Juarez Silva Jr., avy amin'ny Blog do Juarez, dia manontany tena raha marina tokoa fa ny fanavakavahana mahazo ny mainty hoditra ao Brezila dia olana ara-tsosialy fa tsy ara-poko: ||| Juarez Silva Jr., from Blog do Juarez, wonders if it is indeed true that discrimination against black people in Brazil is a social, not racial, problem:
rehefa tsy mifanitsy amina lasitra stereotype iray sy toerana ara-tsosialy iray ny mainty hoditra dia manefa  izany eo ihany, raha toa (ilay zalahy ity) tsy nanana fiara raitra, angamba tsy nisy na inona na inona nitranga, sa tsy izany? ||| when black people don't fit a certain stereotype and social place they pay the price  after all, if (this guy) didn't have a fancy car, maybe nothing would have happened, right?
Trotraky ny antsojay satria ny toerany eo anivon'ny fiarahamonina tsy mifanandrify amin'izay andrasan'ny fiarahamonina aminy, ilay niharam-boina eto dia mihevitra sahady ny hivarotra ilay fiara nampidi-kizo ||| Tired of getting hassled because his social status doesn't fit what society expects of him, the victim has already considered selling the problematic car
 Carrefour mpanavakava-bolon-koditra, fanehoan-kery iray fanoherana ny fanavakavaham-bolon-koditra natao amin'ny fitaratry ny fiara teo amin'ny toeram-piantsonan'ny fiara ao amin'ny Carrefour. ||| "Racist Carrefour", a demonstration against racism on car windows in Carrefour's car park.
Ao amin'ny vohikala Geledés Instituto da Mulher Negra (Ivontoerana Geledés ho an'ny vehivavy mainty hoditra, pt), maro ireo olona sorena amin'ity vaovao ity ary niloa-bava namoaka ny alahelon'izy ireo ao amin'ny boaty fametrahana fanamarihana. ||| On the Geledés Instituto da Mulher Negra (Geledés Black Woman Institute, pt) website, many people lamented this news and voiced their indignation in the comment box.
Ohatra, milaza i Ayraon: ||| For instance, Ayraon says:
Aty Brezila irery ihany no heverin'ny olona ho miafina ny fanavakavaham-bolon-koditra. ||| It's only in Brazil that people think racism is hidden.
Hagaigena! ||| Bullshit!
Miafina fotsiny ho an'ireo tsy te-hijery azy izany. ||| It's only hidden for those who don't want to see it.
Amin'ny teny hafa, diso hevitra tamin'ny fomba fijeriny mivilana momba ny tenany ihany ny Breziliana. ||| In other words, Brazilians are deluded by a distorted perception of themselves.
Foko mifangaro isika! ||| We're a mixed race !
hoy ny iray, Tsy misy mainty na fotsy izany, hoy ny iray hafa miteny, raha sendra misy olona mainty hoditra milaza fa nizaka fanavakavaham-bolon-koditra izy. ||| someone says, There is neither black nor white, someone else declares, should the unacknowledged black person say that he/she has experienced racism.
Any ivelany any, ho an'ireo mahafatantra hoe toy inona moa i Brezila dia tsy afaka hahatakatra hoe fomba ahoana no nanafenan'ity firenena ity nandritry ny fotoana elabe ny fanavakavaham-bolon-koditra tao aminy. ||| Overseas, those who know what Brazil is like cannot understand how this country has managed to hide its sickly racism for so long.
Eto an-toerana, miara-miaina hadalana itambaram-be isika: ny fotsy hoditra mihevitra fa tsy misy zavatra toy izany hoe fanavakavahana izany fa zavatra foronin'ny mainty hoditra any an-tsainy any izany (dia ireo mainty' izay heverin'ny sasany ho toy ny tsy misy), ary ny mainty hoditra indray milaza fa ny fanavakavaham-bolon-koditra breziliana dia misarom-boaly; Maro no manaiky an'io teo-javatra io (ary dia maro mihitsy ireo milaza fa tsy mbola niharan'izany fanavakavahana izany ry zareo, na dia lasibatr'izany isan'andro vaky izao aza). ||| Over here, we live in collective insanity: white people think that there's no such a thing as racism and that it is merely imagined by black people (the same blacks' that other people say don't exist), and black people say that Brazilian racism is covert; Many accept this situation (and some even say they have never suffered racism, despite being the target of it on a daily basis).
Ny tantaran'ity lehilahy avy any Bahia ity no tena nankarary saina ahy, satria dia hiverimberina ny toy io rehefa tsy misy fandraisana andraikitra avy amintsika. ||| The story of this man from Bahia makes me sad, because it is going to repeat itself over and over without any reaction from us.
Sa mba hanao zavatra isika momba azy ity? ||| Or are we going to do something about it?
Ho valin'ny fanontaniana'ilay mpitoraka blaogy, nanomboka ireo hetsika fanoherana. ||| To answer the blogger's question, the protests have begun.
Nisy fanehoankery natao ny 22 Aogositra, ary raha ny nambaran'ny Geledés dia hetsi-panoherana lehibe iray hanoherana ilay vondron'orinasam-barotra no hatao ny 5 Septambra. ||| There was a demonstration on August 22nd, and according to Geledés a bigger protest against the retail chain will take place on September 5th.
Olana saro-bahana ny fanavakavaham-bolon-koditra ho an'ireo firenena nozanahan'ireo tany mandroso sy niaina teo ambany vahohon'ny fanandevozana; mbola betsaka ny antsojay mipoitra any anatin'ny fiarahamonina maoderina any. ||| Race is a very complex issue for countries that once were colonies of developed states and overshadowed by slavery; a lot of prejudice remains in modern society.
Nanamarika an'i Brezila ny fanandevozana mahery setra natao ireo Afrikana mainty hoditra, izay naharitra efa ho 300 taona ary, hatramina dingana iray voafaritra, dia kitro nifaharan'ny toekarena nandritry ny vanim-potoanan'ny fanjanahantany. ||| Brazil is marked by the violent slavery of black Africans, which lasted for over 300 years and was, to a certain degree, the linchpin of the economic framework during the colonial era.
Nandova izany holatra ara-tsosialy izany ireo mainty hoditra aty amin'izao fotoana izao ary miaritra amin'ny endrika samihafa ny fanavakavaham-bolon-koditra amin'ny andavanandrom-piainan'izy ireo. ||| Black people here today have inherited this social stigma and suffer from racism in many aspects of their daily life.
Nefa sakafom-panahy ho an'ny saina, ary ventiny ho an'ny hafatra hafa io. ||| But this is all food for thought, and material for another post.

Maraoka: Tetikasa Zotran-dalamby TGV Vita Frantsay Miteraka Resabe ||| Morocco: French Made TGV Rail Project Causes Controversy
Ny Alakamisy 29 Septambra 2011, nitsidika an'i Maraoka ny Filoha Frantsay Sarkozy mba hanotrona ny fanombohana ny asa fanorenana zotram-piarandalamby TGV mampitohy ireo tanàna ao Tangier sy Casablanca. ||| On Thursday 29 September, 2011, President Sarkozy of France visited Morocco to oversee the launch of construction work on a new TGV rail link between the cities of Tangier and Casablanca.
Ity fiarandalamby haingam-pandeha vita frantsay ity dia tokony hanomboka hisosa amin'ny Desambra 2015 ary mitontaly 20 lavitrisa dirhams (US$2.4 lavitrisa) ny vivavinam-pandaniana aminy. ||| The French made high-velocity train is due to start operating by December 2015 and is worth an estimated 20 billion dirhams (US$2.4 billion).
Ny masoivohom-baovaom-panjakana Maraokana M.A.P. dia nidehaka hoe i Maraoka no firenena voalohany indrindra aty Afrika sy amin'ny tany Arabo hanana fitaterana an-dalamby raitra sy araka ny haitao avo lenta toy izany ||| Moroccan state-run news agency M.A.P. boasts that Morocco is the first country of Africa and the Arab world to have such a technologically advanced rail transport grid
Nandritra ny lanonana, teo ambany fiahian'ny mpanjakan'i Maraoka Mohammed VI sy ny Filoha Sarkozy, ny Minisitry ny Fitaterana Maraokana, Karim Ghellab dia nanazava fa ny TGV dia andrasana hiteraka asa vaovao sy ho seha-piofanana momba ny asa amin'ny fitaterana an-dalamby ho an'ireo Maraokana mitady asa. ||| At a ceremony chaired by King Mohammed VI of Morocco and President Sarkozy, the Moroccan Minister of Transport Karim Ghellab explained that the TGV is expected to generate new jobs and offer training opportunities in rail professions for Moroccan jobseekers.
Na izany aza, dia miteraka resabe ihany ity tetikasa ity eny anivon'ny tontolon'ny bilaogy Maraokana. ||| The project is, however, causing a stir in the Moroccan blogosphere.
Mametra-panontaniana ireo bilaogera Maraokana mikasika izay antony ao ambadik'izao, ary manontany raha tena ilain'ny fireneny tokoa ny tetikasa lafo vidy be toy izao. ||| Bloggers are raising questions about the motives behind the scheme and asking whether their country needs a project that costly.
Fiarandalamby TGV any ambanivohitra frantsay. ||| TGV train in the French countryside.
Ilay bilaogera Maraokana anti-panahy, Larbi, dia mihetsika manohitra ilay heloka bevava ara-toekarena. ||| Veteran Moroccan blogger Larbi protests against a project he deems an economic crime.
Azavainy fa ilay fifanarahana dia tampi-maso nomena an'i Sarkozy tany amin'ny faramparan'ny taona 2007 tany mba ho fanambatambazana ny Frantsay noho ny tsy nahazoan-dry zareo ny fifanarahana varotra fitaovam-piadiana, nitentina volabe, nanoloana ny Amerikana. ||| He explains the contract was offered to Sarkozy back in 2007 as a reward to the French after they lost a lucrative arms deal against the Americans.
Tamin'izany fotoana, ny governemanta Maraokana dia nifidy ny fiaramanidina mpiady Lockheed Martin F-16 avy any Etazonia nanoloana ny fiaramanidina mpiady frantsay Dassault Rafales. ||| Back then, the Moroccan government preferred the United States' Lockheed Martin F-16 fighter jets to the French Dassault Rafales.
Nisafidy ny hividy ny TGV frantsay i Maraoka mba hampiononana an'i Sarkozy, hoy ilay bilaogera manazava. ||| Morocco offered to purchase the French TGV system to console Sarkozy, the blogger explains.
Manoratra i Larbi, mitodika amin'ny filoha Sarkozy: ||| Larbi writes, addressing President Sarkozy:
Dia teo no teraka ity hadalàna ara-toekarena ity: miainga avy aminà fifangaroana fandrebireben-tsaina nataonao tamin'ireo mpitondra Maraokana, ny finiavan'ireto farany hanome fahafaham-po anao, ary ny finiavana, na va re holazaintsika hoe, ny di-dohan'ny mpanjaka Mohammed VI. ||| Thus was born this economic insanity: from a mixture of psychological ascendance you have over Moroccan leaders, the latter's will to please you, and the will, or shall we say the whim, of King Mohammed VI.
Indray maraina, tsy nasiam-pandinihana mialoha akory, tsy nisy fifampiresahana na fijerena izay mba hahazoana tombony, dia notapahanay fa homenay valisoa ianareo, dia ny TGV, mba tsy ho tezitra. ||| One morning, without preliminary study, without any consultation or business case, we decided to award you a TGV so that you didn't get angry.
Ho setriny dia nanao kabary mampandry adrisa ianao tao amin'ny Parlemanta Maraokana hilazana izay tsara rehetra azonao sainina momba ny mpanjaka Mohammed VI sy ny demaokrasia Maraokana. ||| In return you kindly made a beautiful speech in the Moroccan parliament to say all the good you think of King Mohammed VI and the Moroccan democracy.
Tamin'ny 2007 izany. ||| It was in 2007.
Arivo taona lasa izany. ||| It was a thousand years ago.
Ny zavatra tokana azo antoka anefa, tsy niova ianaona ho lohataona Arabo io na tsia. ||| One thing is for sure though, you have not changed Arab spring or not.
Ny fitsidihan'i Sarkozy tao Maraoka dia nitranga indrindra tao anatin'ny fotoana izay isian'ny adihevitra lehibe ao amin'ny firenena, momba ny fanavaozana demoakratika nentin'ny Lohataona Arabo, natosik'ireo hetsi-panoherana am-pilaminana teny an-dalambe notarihan'ny hetsiky ny tanora 20 Febroary mpandàla ny demaokrasia. ||| Sarkozy's visit to Morocco comes at a time when the country is having an important debate on democratic reforms inspired by the Arab spring, punctuated by peaceful street demonstrations led by the pro-democracy youth movement February 20.
Ho an'ny maro, ilay fitsidihana dia manamarika fanohanana midanadana ataon'i Frantsa ny fanavaozana maha-be resaka tarihan'ny Mpanjaka Mohammed VI. ||| For many, the visit marks the open support of France to the controversial reforms lead by King Mohammed VI.
Ho an'ilay mafàna fo Rachid Droit, io dia miteraka fitsabahana amin'ny raharaha anatin'i Maraoka. ||| For activist Rachid Droit this constitutes an interference in the internal affairs of Morocco.
Tsy miolankolaka ny hafany ho an'i Sarkozy: ||| His message to Sarkozy is unambiguous:
"Sarkozy, 'ndeha mandeha any! ||| "Sarkozy, get out!
Tsy amidy akory i Maraoka". ||| Morocco is not for sale".
Saribe avy amin'i Rachid Droit, nakarina tao amin'ny Facebook. ||| Poster by Rachid Droit, posted on Facebook.
Ny tambajotra Alstom ||| Alstom connection
Ny orinasa frantsay Alstom, izay nahazo ilay fifanarahana hametraka ilay TGV Maraokana, dia tafiditra anaty lisitra maintin'ny BDS campaign (Boycott, Divestment and Sanctions) hatramin'izy io nipongatra, tany amin'ny Janoary 2010 tany, hoe tafiditra tamin'ny tetikasa fanorenana zotran-dalamby tram tao Jerosalema ilay orinasa, nosainina hampitohy an'i Jerosalema Andrefana amin'ireo fibodoana tsy ara-dalàna ao anatiny sy manodidina an'i Palestina Atsinanana. ||| The French company Alstom, which won the contract to build the Moroccan TGV, is blacklisted by the BDS campaign (Boycott, Divestment and Sanctions) since it emerged, back in January 2010, that the company was involved in the construction of a light rail project in Jerusalem designed to connect West Jerusalem to illegal settlements in and surrounding occupied Palestinian East Jerusalem.
Mamfakinch!, tranonkala iray tantaninà andianà mafàna fo Maraokana, no miresaka ilay olana sady manontany tena hoe: ||| Mamfakinch!, a website run by a group of Moroccan activists, raises the issue and wonders:
Fony nanome io tetikasa io ho an'ny Alstom, noraisina tao anatin'ny kajikajy ve ny efa fandraisan'io orinasa io anjara amin'ny fametrahana zotranà tram iray hampitohy ny Andrefan'i Jerosalema amin'ny Atsinanan'i Jerosalema sy faritra roa bodoiny? ||| When the project was assigned to Alstom, had the company's participation in the construction of a tramway connecting West Jerusalem to East Jerusalem and to two West Bank settlements been considered at all?
Ho fampahatsiahivana, ny ligy Arabo, izay mpikambana feno ao anatiny i Maraoka, dia nandany fanapahan-kevitra iray manameloka ilay tetikasa zotran-dalamby tram ao Jerosalema (tany am-piandohan'ny 2010 tany). ||| As a reminder, the Arab league, of which Morocco is a full member, passed a resolution condemning the light rail project of Jerusalem (in early 2010).
Lafo vidy ny hafainganam-pandeha ||| The high cost of high speed
Betsaka amin'ireo resabe manodidina ilay tetikasa TGV no mikasika ny tombam-bidiny. ||| Much of the controversy surrounding the TGV project stems from its estimated cost.
Manoratra ilay bilaogera Omar El Hyani: ||| Blogger Omar El Hyani writes:
Ny tombam-bidin'ilay tetikasa tany ampiandohana dia teo amin'ny 20 lavitrisa dirhams Maraokana teo, latsaka kely monja ny 2 lavitrisa euros. ||| The project's initial cost was estimated at 20 billion Moroccan dirhams, just under 2 billion euros.
Saingy tany am-piandohan'ity volana ity, fahagagàna iray no nitsena ireo Maraokana mpandoa hetra: tsy 20 lavitrisa intsony ny tombam-bidin'ilay tetikasa fa 33 lavitrisa dirhams (manodidina ny 3 lavitrisa euros)! ||| But earlier this month, a surprise awaited Moroccan taxpayers: the estimated cost of the project is no longer 20 billion but 33 billion dirhams (about 3 billion euros)!
Eny, tsy diso famaky akory ianao. ||| Yes, you read that right.
Fiakarana 13 lavitrisa dirhams (iray lavitrisa euros). ||| An increase of 13 billion dirhams (over one billion euros).
Ary dia tsy nisy na dia fanazavàna iray aza naroso hatreto! ||| And not a single explanation provided so far!
Tohizan'i Omar amin'ny fanazavàny ny antony eritreretiny ho tsy nanaovana fakàn-kevitra tamin'ny fomba demaokratika mikasika ny vidin'ilay tetikasa: ||| Omar goes on explaining why he thinks the cost of the project has not been subject to democratic scrutiny:
Aoka tsy ho vendrana isika. ||| Let's not be naive.
Misy sokajinà tetikasa izay tsy ananan'ireo parlemantera sy minisitra fahefana: ireo tetikasa milatsaka avy any ambony, tarihana, vatsiana vola ary atolotra eo ambony karipetra mena midorehitra, ary manoloana kamera maro raha mbola azo atao. ||| There is a category of projects that parliamentarians and ministers have no control over: projects that fall from above, conducted, funded, and presented on a red carpet, preferably in front of many cameras.
Ary ahoana ny amin'ireo fepetra footra momba ny fitantanana mangarahara ny toekarena? ||| What about the basic rules of economic governance?
Ny fijerena izay mba tombony ho azo? ||| Business cases?
Ny fanadihadiana ny fiantraikany ara-toekarena sy sosialy? ||| Economic and socio-economic impact studies?
Ahoana ny toe-bolam-panjakana? ||| What about the state of public finances?
Hadalàna mihoampampana! ||| What an insanity!
TGV - hatao inona? ||| A TGV - what for?
Ilay bilaogera Kingstoune dia velom-panahiana ny amin'ilay fiheverana hoe ny TGV dia ho vahaolana sahaza an'ireo olan'ny fitateram-bahoaka ao Maraoka satria, milaza izy, efa voaporofo fa vahaolana tsy sahaza ary lafo vidy izany tany Frantsa. ||| Blogger Kingstoune doubts the TGV is the right answer to the problems of public transport in Morocco since, he argues, it has proved to be an inadequate and costly solution in France itself.
Ho azy, ny TGV dia endrika isehoan'ny di-dohan'ny mpanjaka fotsiny fa tsy tena filàna marina. ||| For him, the TGV is more an expression of a royal whim than it is of a true demand.
Hoy izy manoratra: ||| He writes:
Manontany tena aho raha mba efa nandinika lalina sy niady hevitra momba ity tetikasa ity ireo politisiana sy teknisiana. ||| I wonder if politicians and technocrats have studied or discussed this project critically.
Thailandy: Voatsiny Noho Ny Tahan'ny Fitondrana Vohoky ny Tanora Ny Facebook ||| Thailand: Facebook Blamed for Teen Pregnancies
I Thailandy no manana taha ambony indrindra eo amin'ny tanora bevohoka erantany. ||| Thailand has one of the highest rate of teenage pregnancies in the world.
Tombatombanana ho 120.000 isan-taona ireo tanora mitondra vohoka tsy nirina, ary toa hoe anisan'ny tompon'andraikitra mahatonga izany vohoka tsy niriana izany ny Facebook izay tambajotra sosialy fanta-daza, raha mino ny famintinana naroson'ny Foibem-pirenena misahana ny fampandrosoana ara-toe-karena sy sosialy (NESDB) isika: ||| It's estimated that 120,000 unplanned teen pregnancies happen each year, and it seems popular social networking site Facebook is partly to blame for the unwanted pregnancies, if we are to believe the conclusion of the National Economic and Social Development Board (NESDB):
Nilaza ny NESDB fa olona eo amin'ny 18-24 no tena mpisera facebook indrindra, mahatratra 40% amin'ireo mpisare facebook rehetra. ||| The NESDB has revealed that people in the age group of 18-24 are the biggest group of facebook users, accounting for 40% of all users.
Nilaza io birao io fa ny firongatry ny tambajotra sosialy no tena fositra mahatonga ny vohoky ny tanora satria manoratra zavatra manaitaitra na rakikira an-tsary eo amin'ny aterineto ireo tanora ireo. ||| The Board said that the social media growth is partly to blame for the teen pregnancy problems as some youngsters post seducing messages or video clips online.
Amin'ny lafiny iray, manazava ny tsy fetezan'ny fanabeazana ara-pananahana ao Thailandy i Saksith Saiyasombut ||| Saksith Saiyasombut, on the other hand, highlights the inadequacies of Thailand's sexual education program:
Mazava ho azy fa mahazo tsiny ny tambazotra sosialy lehibe indrindra noho ireo zavatra mahatsiravina hita ao izay misarika ny tanora hanao firaisana ara-nofo tsy vaaaro. ||| Of course the largest social network is to be blamed for the all the steamy content that drive teenagers to have unprotected sex.
Na izao koa ny fanazavana tsotra indrindra – Manana olana goavana i Thailandy eo amin'ny resaka fampianarana ara-pananahana. ||| Or it could be the much more simple explanation – Thailand has a severe problem with sexual education.
Raha toa ka te handresy ny hakiviana, dia tokony ho tonga saina ny mpitondra fanjakana fa ny hany vahaolana lojika indrindra ialana amin'ny vohoky ny tanora dia ny fampianarana azy ireo tsara ny momba ny fananahana ary ny fampisehoana azy ireo ny marina mikasika ny fisian'izany fa tsy ny fanafenana izany velively akory. ||| If the moral outrage could be put to one side, the powers that be might be able to see that the only reasonable solution to avoid teen pregnancies is to have proper sexual education and face the naked truth about the existence of sexuality instead of tucking it away.
Nilaza ny Ricefieldradio fa tsy misy idiran'ny tambajotra sosialy mihitsy ny fitondrana vohoka eo amin'ny tanora: ||| Ricefieldradio comments that social media has nothing to do with teen pregnancies:
Tsy misy idiran'ny Facebook sy haino aman-jery sosialy hafa ny vohoky ny tanora sy ny firaisana ara-nofo. ||| Facebook and other Social media has nothing to do with teen pregnancies or sex.
Resaka retsika io. ||| It's hormones.
Efa mitady fanaovana firaisana ara-nofo ny tanora na dia mbola tsy notorontoronina akory aza ny loharanon'ny tambazotra sosialy. ||| Young people managed to have sex way before any of the social network founders mothers was even inseminated.
Mbola nanamafy ny amin'ny nanafoanana ny fianarana fananahana ao Thailandy ihany koa ny Tasty Thailand: ||| Tasty Thailand also points out the reduced sex education classes in Thailand:
Sady ny faha 18 taona dia taonan'ny 'hatanorana' raha ny fahafantarantsika nefa, raha araka ny lalàna, dia efa azo lazaina ho olon-dehibe ireo mahatratra izany taona izany. ||| After all, 18 may be technically a 'teen' but, by law, it's actually the age of an adult.
Noho izany dia tsy mitombona mihitsy ny 'fanomezana tsiny ny ny Facebook' ho antony mahatonga ny vohoky ny tanora ||| So that doesn't fit the 'blame Facebook' camp for teen pregnancies at all
Satria rehefa natao ny fandinihana, dia tsy miankina amin'ny fanafoanana ny fampianarana ny firaisana ara-nofo any an-tsekolin'ny Thailandy nandritra ny taona maro teo aloha ny fiakaran'ny tahan'ireo tanora bevohoka ao Thailandy, na koa hoe tsy mampianatra ny zanany mikasika ny fanabeazana aizana ny Ray aman-dReny ao Thailandy. ||| Because, after all, Thailand's growing teen pregnancy rate can't be because sex education classes in Thai schools have been drastically reduced in recent years, or because Thai parents don't teach their kids about contraception now can it?
NY MARINA - Niaiky ny andraikitry ny Ray aman-dReny ny Fahafahana Manohitra Sivana ao Thailandy: ||| FACT - Freedom Against Censorship Thailand recognizes the role of parenting:
Marina fa mora voasarika amin'ny Facebook ny zanatsika. ||| Sure, Facebook may make it easier for our kids to hook up.
Nefa tsy fahaizana manabe ny zanaka ny tsy fanaraha-maso azy ireo eo anoloan'ny solosaina. ||| But it's bad parenting which fails to supervise your kid on a computer.
Mety ny ilain'ny ankizy angamba dia ny milalao baolina kitra miaraka amin'ny namany fotsiny...baolina kitra foana! ||| Maybe kids just need to play football with friends...a lot of football!
Ireto misy fanehoan-kevitra tao amin'ny Twitter. ||| Here are some reactions on Twitter.
Facebook no nahatonga izany ary manana ny hadisoany izy eo amin'ny vohoky ny tanora ao Thailandy. ||| Facebook did it and shares the blame for Thailand's teen pregnancies.
Mampanontany tena hoe iza no diso folo taona lasa izay... Prem? ||| Wondering who was to blame ten years ago... Prem?
Isika mieritreritra fa ny fanaovana firaisana ara-nofo tsy voaaro ihany no miteraka vohoka eo amin'ny tanora. ||| To think, we always thought unprotected sex causes teen pregnancies.
Nefa ankehitriny dia toa hoe tompon'andraikitra amin'izany koa ny Facebook! ||| Apparently Facebook does actually!
Tsy voalohany izao no lazaina fa manana ny fahadisoany ny Facebook eo amin'ny firongatry ny tahan'ny fitondrana vohoka eo amin'ny tanora. ||| This is not the first time that Facebook was blamed for rising teen pregnancies.
Tamin'ny taona lasa, dia nanome tsiny ny tambazotra sosialy lehibe indrindra ilay mpitondra fivavahana iray tao Central Java, Indonezia ho tompon'andraikitra amin'ny fahabetsahan'ny isan'ny tanora manambady aloha loatra sy amin'ny fiakaran'ny tahan'ny vohoka tsy niriana teo amin'ny tanora teo amin'ny firenena. ||| Last year, a religious leader in Central Java, Indonesia also blamed the giant social network for the rise of underage marriages and unwanted teen pregnancies in the country.
Tonizia: Krizin'ny mpitsoa-ponenana ao an-tsisintanin'i Libya ||| Tunisia: Refugee Crisis at the Libya Border
Ny sisintany misy eo amin'i Tonizia sy i Libya dia nahatazanana ny firohotry ny mpitsoa-ponenana maro be hatramin' ny nisian'ny fitroarana tao Lybia. ||| The border between Tunisia and Libya has seen a massive influx of refugees since the uprising in Libya began.
Sady lava no sarotra ny dia mamonjy sisintany, ary ho ny ankamaroany dia tsy mbola tsy mifarana eo ny fahasarotana. ||| The journey to the border is long and tough, and for most it doesn't end there.
Vahoaka marobe aman-jatony no niandry sady niaritra ny andro mangatsiaka mba hiampita hankao Tonizia. ||| Huge crowds of thousands have been waiting for days in freezing cold weather to cross in to Tunisia.
Maherin'ny 75000 ny olona nandositra ny herisetra tao Lybia mba ho any Tonizia, nanomboka ny 20 febroary, ary mbola maro ireo ho avy. ||| Up to 75,000 people have fled the violence in Libya to Tunisia, since February 20, and even more people are expected.
Ny toe-draharaha ao amin'ny sisintany Libya-Tonizia dia miditra ao anatin'ny krizy miantraika lalina amin'ny mahaolona, hoy ny UNHCR. ||| The situation at the Libya-Tunisia border is at crisis point, says the UNHCR.
Nalefan'i IFRC ao Ras Jdir ity horonan-tsary ity tamin'ny 1 martsa. ||| The IFRC have posted this video from Ras Jdir on March 1.
Maro tamin'ny mpitsoa-ponenana tafahitsoka eo amin'ny amin'ny toeram-piampitàna Ras Jdir any Tonizia no Ejypsiana nipetraka tao Libya. ||| Many of the refugees who are trapped at the crossing point of Ras Jdir in Tunisia are Egyptians who lived in Libya.
Manaramaso akaiky ny zava-nitranga any an-tsisintany ny mpiray tanindrazana ao Ejipta. ||| Their compatriots in Egypt have been following the events at the border closely.
Nampirisika ireo Ejipsiana mba hanery ny governemantany hamerina ireo izay mbola tafahitsoka eo am-piampitàna ao Ras Jedir i Hani Mohammed: ||| Hani Mohammed urges Egyptians to put pressure on the government to bring back home those who are still trapped at the Ras Jedir crossing point:
Ejipsiana an'arivony tao amin'ny sisintany fiampitàna Ras Jdir, tao Ben Guerden, ao Tonizia, no miantsoantso vonjy. ||| Thousands of Egyptians at the border crossing of Ras Jdir, in Ben Guerden, in Tunisia, are screaming for help.
Azafady, alefaso ity hafatra ity ho an'ny governemanta Egypsiana. ||| Please, send this message to the Egyptian government.
Miharatsy ny toedraharaha aty ary atahorana ny hisian'ny krizy ara-tsakafo. ||| The situation there is deteriorating and there is fear that a humanitarian crisis may occur.
Niresaka momba ny fandosiran'ny Ejipsiana an'i Gadhafi ny namana Toniziana, noho ny krizy ara-tsakafo ao Ras Jdir... ary nihoatra amin'ny tokony izy ny hamaroany. ||| Tunisian friends are talking about Egyptians fleeing from Gaddafi, facing a humanitarian crisis in Ras Jdir... and the numbers have gone beyond their capabilities
Misaotra ry rahalahy sy ranabavy Toniziana noho ny fandraisanareo ny namana Ejipsiana. ||| Thanks Tunisian brothers and sisters for hosting your fellow Egyptians.
Nampiseho firaisan-kina taminy ianareo noho ny tsy firarahian'ny governemanta! ||| You showed them more solidarity than our careless government!
Ny fiantsona hamonjy ireo mpitsoa-ponenana ao Ras Jdir dia niparitaka tamin'ny fampitam-baovao,sy ny fampielezan-kevitra amin'ny fanangonana fanampiana. ||| Calls to come to the rescue of refugees in Ras Jdir have been spreading via social media, and campaigns to collect humanitarian aid have also been organised.

Antso ho amin'ny fanampiana! ||| Help!

Gabon: Kandidà mampiasa media sosialy amin'ity fifidianana filoham-pirenena manan-tantara ity ||| Gabon: Presidential Candidate Uses Social Media in Historic Election
Mampiasa ny media vaovao mba hampitàna ny hafany i Bruno Ben Moubamba, kandidà amin'ny fifidianana filoham-pirenena any Gabon. ||| Bruno Ben Moubamba, presidential candidate in Gabon, uses new media to spread his message.
Raha eo am-piomanana ny fifidianana voalohany taorian'ny nahafatesan'i Omar Bongo i Gabon dia indro misy kandidà iray miezaka ny mampiditra ny tenany ho ao anatin'ny tantara amin'ny alalan'ny fampiasana ny media sosialy. ||| As Gabon prepares for its first election since the death of Omar Bongo, one candidate is trying to make history with the aid of social media.

Tsy vitan'ny mampiasa blaogy ny fampielezan-kevitr'i Ben Moubamba fa nampiasa betsaka ireo sehatra sosialy (an-tserasera) hafa koa toy ny Twitter, Flickr, Facebook, YouTube, ary hi5. ||| The Ben Moubamba campaign not only has a blog, but has made extensive use of other social media platforms, including Twitter, Flickr, Facebook, YouTube, and hi5.
Mazava ho azy fa tsy fantatra loatra hoe Gaboney firy no mety ho tafiditra amin'ny alalan'ireo sehatra ireo; folo isan-jaton'ireo olom-pirenena ihany no manana aterineto, na azy manokana na any amin'ny cybercafe. ||| Of course, it is unclear how many Gabonese can be reached through these platforms; only an estimated ten percent of citizens have internet access, whether privately or via public cafes.
Talohan'ny nahafatesany tamin'ny 8 Jona nandritra ny faha-73 taonany, i Bongo no filoham-pirenena nitondra ela indrindra tany Afrika naharitra 41 taona teo amin'ny fitondrana. ||| Before his death on June 8th at the age of 73, Bongo was Africa's longest-serving ruler, having spent 41 years in power.
Ho henjana ny raharaha ho an'i Moubamba miatrika ny filatsahan'ny zanakalahin'i Bongo tahaka ny kandidà ofisialin'ny antoko mpitondra, ny tsy fahampin'ny fomba amam-panao demokratika any Gabon ary ny fifidianana amin'ny 30 Aogositra izay manakaiky haingana dia haingana. ||| With Bongo's son as the ruling party's official candidate, Gabon's lack of a democratic tradition, and with the August 30th election fast approaching, Moubamba faces an uphill battle.
Teraka tamin'ny 1967, taona nahazoan'i Bongo fahefana, taranaka vaovao ana mpitarika Afrikana i Moubamba. ||| Born in 1967, the year that Bongo came to power, Moubamba represents a younger generation of African leaders.

Eo am-pametrapetrahana ny ekipako avy amin'ny fiomanana hiditra ho ao anatin'ny fampielezan-kevitra aho izao. ||| At this moment, I am reorganizing my team to transition from the pre-campaign to the campaign.

Atoa. Haiti: Iharan'ny herisetra ireo vehivavy sy zazavavy nafindra toerana ||| Haiti: Displaced Women and Girls Victims of Gender Violence
Vokatr'ilay horohoron-tany nandringana tany Haiti, mbola iharan'ny herisetra ihany ireo vehivavy sy zazavavy, ary ny sasany amin'izy ireo dia tsy hoe voaolana fotsiny ihany, fa mbola mizaka ny tsy fisian'ny rafi-pitsarana sy ny tsy fahampian'ny fitsaboana ihany koa. ||| In the aftermath of the devastating Haiti earthquake, women and girls are still facing gender violence, as some of them not only experience rape, but then have to face an absent judicial system and less than adequate medical care.
Ao amin'ny blaogy Ms. Magazine Blog, Gina Ulysse nanoratra hoe ao anatin'ny fiainana andavanandron'ireo vehivavy miaina any amin'ireo toby Haitiana ny fanolanana, izay hanondroany ny Ivon-toerana misahana ny Fitsarana sy ny Demokrasia any Haiti (Institute for Justice and Democracy in Haiti (IJDH) sy ny Tatitr' i Madre mikasika ny Fanolanana any amin'ny Tobin'ireo Olona tsy Manan-kialofana (IDP) toy ny loharanon' antontan'isa mampihorohoron'ny fanaovana herisetra. ||| In the Ms. Magazine Blog, Gina Ulysse wrote Rape a Part of Daily Life for Women in Haitian Relief Camps, where she points towards the Institute for Justice and Democracy in Haiti (IJDH) and Madre 's Report on Rape in the Internally Displaced Persons (IDP) Camps as the source of terrifying statistics on gender violence.
Maro ireo vehivavy sy zazavavy no very tambajotra mpanohana azy ireny na very ray, rahalahy ary vady na sipa izay mety ho afaka niaro azy ireny. ||| Many women and girls have lost their support network as well as fathers, brothers and husbands or boyfriends who might've been able to protect them.
Noho izany dia manimba ny fiainany manokana ny fiarahany miaina amin'ny daholobe any amin'ny toby, maro ireo voatery mandro eny imasom-bahoaka sy matory eo akaikin'olona tsy fantany akory na any amin'ireo toerana izay mety hahavoan'ny herisetra azy ireo. ||| So being in cramped quarters in the camps really cuts down on their privacy, many have to shower in public and sleep next to strangers or in locations where they are vulnerable to attacks.
Rehefa mitranga ny herisetra, maro amin'ny tranga no fanolanana itambaram-be, tsy maintsy mbola hiatrika dingana hafa izy ireo: ny ankamarony tsy manana fomba ahafahana mahazo fanampiana ara-pitsaboana avy any amin'ireo vehivavy mpitsabo ary tsy mbola misy izany rafi-pitsarana izany, mamela azy ireo hiditra amin'ny kolikoly amin'ny polisy sy ny taimbavan"ireo manam-pahefana ho fanampin'ny fijalian'izy ireo tamin'ny daroka sy ny fahafantarany fa mbola mirenireny any ireo nidaroka azy. ||| Once the attacks take place, many of the cases being gang rapes, they have yet to face more ordeals: most have no way to receive medical aid from female practitioners and the justice system is almost non-existent, leaving them to deal with corruption in the police and revictimization from authorities in addition to the stigma from being attacked and the knowledge that their attackers are still at large.
Mbola tena ratsy ny fahazoan'ireo vehivavy ny rariny. ||| Women's access to jus­tice has been even worse.
Ireo vehivavy izay niharan'ny fanolanana–ary amin'izao dia miady amin'ny fijaliana sy ny vokatra ara-tsain'ireo fanolanana ireo– dia matetika no hesoina na nodin'ireo polisy tsy hita. ||| Women who reported rapes–and were already strug­gling with stigma­ti­za­tion and the psy­cho­log­i­cal effects of sex­ual assault–were often mocked or ignored by police.
Ohatra sasany, tsy maintsy nijoro nanoloana ny kolikoly ataon'ireo mpitandro filaminana ihany koa ireo vehivavy ireo. ||| In some instances, these women have had to deal with police cor­rup­tion as well.
Ary koa, mbola tsy notsarain'ny fitsarana Haitiana nysasany amin'ireo tranga ireo. ||| More­over, cases have not been pros­e­cuted by the Hait­ian judicial sys­tem.
Ireo sisa velona tamin'izany dia marefo satria mbola miaina eo amin'ny manodidina ny toby izay nidarohana azy ireo izy ireo ary dia tsy mbola voaasazy ireo nanolana azy ireo. ||| Sur­vivors remain vul­ner­a­ble since they con­tinue to live in the same areas of the camps where they were attacked and their rapists remain at large.
Vehivavy maro no nitatitra fa voaolana tamina fotoana samihafa nanomboka tamin'iny horohorontany iny. ||| Sev­eral women reported that they've been raped on dif­fer­ent occa­sions since the quake.
Ny IJDH, Mpiara-miasa ao amin'ny Tetikasa mikasika ny Fahasalamana sy ny Tetikasa vaovao Media Mpisolovava dia namoaka horonantsarin'ny fijoroana vavolombelona avy amin'ireo niharam-boina volana vitsy lasa izay. ||| The IJDH, Partners in Health and New Media Advocacy Program released a video a few months ago with testimonies from the victims.
Sandy Berkowitz no naka ny horonantsary ary i Harriet Hirshorn no namoaka izany. ||| The footage was recorded by Sandy Berkowitz and edited by Harriet Hirshorn.
Na dia miady ny hiverina amin'ny fiainana andavanandro aza ireo vehivavy ireo, toa tsy mampino loatra ny hivoaran'ny fiainan-dry zareo satria toa lasa hivadika ho toerana fipetrahana raikitra ireo toby vonjimaika. ||| Even though women struggle to return to normalcy, it is unlikely their situation will improve as the temporary camps seem to be turning into permanent accomodations.
Tamin'ny volana Janoary, C ARE USA nanadihady an'i Dr. Franck Geneus izay mandrindra ny tetikasan'ny Fahasalamana CARE any Haiti ary nanontany azy mikasika ireo antony mahatonga ny firongatry ny fanolanana marobe any amin'ireo toby ireo, ary nilaza ireo toetoetra mahatonga ny tobin'ny IDP ho tany lonaka ho an'ny herisetra izy: ny tsy fahampian'ny herinaratra izay mahatonga ny toby ho maizina amin'ny alina, ny haratsian'ny fandrindràna ireo toby ary ny tsy fanasarahana ireo toeram-pandroana sy ireo fanaovana maloto ka mba ho samy manana ny azy manokana ny lahy sy ny vavy. ||| Back in January, C ARE USA interviewed Dr. Franck Geneus who coordinates CARE's health program in Haiti and asked him about the reasons why there is higher risk of rape in these camps, and he mentioned the characteristics that make the IDP camps a fertile ground for attacks: the lack of electricity that makes camps absolutely dark at night, badly organized camps and non-segregated bathing facilities and latrines so that males and females have their own.
Janet Meyers, mpanome toro-hevitra ao amin'ny CARE dia nanome ny tolo-tànany manokana momba ny fomba tokony hanamboarana ireo toby ireo hiarovana ireo vehivavy sisam-paty vokatr'iny horohorontany iny, miresaka mikasika ireo tranga maro niseho tamin'ny volana Febroary. ||| Janet Meyers, Gender Advisor from CARE also put in her own 2 cents regarding how the camps would be established to make women safer in the earthquake aftermath, pointing out many of the same issues last February.
Manontany tena aho hoe firy amin'ireo olana ireo no mbola tsy voavaha ary rahatoa ka izany, satria toa ho lasa toerana raikitra ireo toby ireo, dia hanokatra lalàna mankany amina famonoana mihoatra noho ny efa misy fotsiny izany. ||| I wonder how many of these issues remain unresolved and if, as these camps turn into more permanent facilities, it will just pave the way for more assaults to take place.
Ejypta: Ny Karapanondronao, Ny Zonao Ry Vehivavy ||| Egypt: Your ID, Your Rights Targets Women
Karapanondro 2 tapitrisa ho an'ny vehivavy 2 tapitrisa Araka ny tarehimarika avy any amin'ny Ministeran'ny Atitany Ejypsianina, mahatratra 4 tapitrisa ireo vehivavy eto amin'ny firenena no tsy manana kara-panondro. ||| According to figures coming from the Egyptian Ministry of Interior, as many as 4 million women in the country do not have national identity cards.
Ny vehivavy tsy manana kara-panondro dia tsy manan-jo hanan-tany, tsy afaka mividy na mivarotra tapakilan-drenivola ary tsy afaka mandova raha misy ny fahafatesana eo amin'ny fianakaviana. ||| A woman without a national ID is not able to own land, she cannot buy or sell assets and she cannot even inherit from her deceased family members.
Mandrara ny vehivavy tsy hiditra amina karazana raharaham-panjakana ihany koa ny tsy fananana karapanondro, anisan'izany ny fampianarana, ny fahasalamana, ny zo hifidy sy ireo zo fototra ara-tsosialy hafa. ||| The lack of IDs also prevent women the access to various of public services, including education, healthcare, the right to vote and other basic social rights.
Ary noho izany indrindra no nanombohana ny fanentanana izay mikendry ny hampanana karampanondrom-pirenena ho an'ny vehivavy rehetra. ||| And that's why a new campaign has been launched aiming to provide all women with national ID cards.
Antsoina hoe "Ny karapanondronao, Ny Zonao" "Your ID, Your Rights" ny fanentanana ary ny tanjona dia ny hanatontosana karapanandro 2 tapitrisa maimaimpoana ho an'ny vehivavy Ejyptiana. ||| The campaign is called "Your ID, Your Rights" and their goal is to issue IDs to 2 million Egyptian women for free.
Hatomboka amin'ny tetikasa fitaratra mandritra ny telo volana ||| It will start with a pilot for three months. 2 Million IDs to 2 Million Women
Araka ny fanentanana ao amim'ny pejy Facebook: ||| According to the campaign's Facebook page:
Mandritra ny telo volana ny tetikasa fitaratra, ka manomboka amin'ny volana Martsa, ary ao amin'ny governorà Qaliobeya no hanatanterahana izany, izay manana distrika 14, ny tanjon'ny tetikasa fitaratra voalohany dia ny hanomezana karapanondro ho an'ny vehivavy 40.000. ||| The pilot will be for three months, starting from March, and it will take place in the Qaliobeya governorate, which has 14 districts, and the target of the pilot period are 40,000 women with no ID cards.
Nofidiana tao Qaliobeya ireo distrika manaraka ireto mandritra ny tetikasa fitaratra voalohany: Benha, Qalioub, Shebin El Kanater ary ny distrikan'i El-Kanater El-Khayreya. Ilene Perlman. ||| The following districts have been chosen in the Qaliobeya for the pilot period: Benha, Qalioub, Shebin El Kanater and El-Kanater El-Khayreya districts.
Araka ny filazan'ny tatitra avy amin'ny Firenena Mikambana tamin'ny taona 2006, tsy mahay mamaky teny sy manoratra ny 41% ny vehivavy efa lehibe ao Ejypta. ||| According to UN report in 2006, 41% of the adult females in Egypt are illiterate. Photo courtesy of Ilene Perlman.
Tsy ity no fanentanana voalohany hiezahana hanatrarana ny tanjona mitovy amin'izao fotoana, na dia izany aza, ity indray mitoraka ity dia nahazo fanohanana avy amina ONG isan-karazany, anisan'izany ny UN Women (United Nations Entity for Gender Equality sy ny Empowerment of Women) (Sampan'ny Firenena Mikambana Misahana ny Miralenta sy ny Fahaleovantenan'ny Vavy), UNDP (United Nations Development Program (Fandaharan'asan'ny Firenena Mikambana misahana ny Fampandrosoana), MSAD (Ministry of State for Administrative Development (Ministeram-panjakana ho amin'ny Fampandrosoana ny Fitantanana), SFD (Social Fund for Development (Fanampiana ara-tsosialy ho amin'ny Fampandrosoana), MoFA (Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Ministeran'ny Raharaham-bahiny), sy ny sisa hafa. ||| This isn't the first campaign of try to achieve the same goal, however this one is supported by various NGOs, including UN Women (United Nations Entity for Gender Equality and the Empowerment of Women), UNDP (United Nations Development Program), MSAD (Ministry of State for Administrative Development), SFD (Social Fund for Development), MoFA (Ministry of Foreign Affairs), and others.
Nampiasa ny fifampitam-baovao sosialy ihany koa ny mpikarakara ny fanentanana mba hampahafantarana bebe kokoa momba ny tetikasa. ||| The campaign organisers are also making use of social media to spread awareness about the project.
Nanangana kaonty tao amin'ny Twitter Facebook izy ireo ho fanentanana momba ny olana misahana ny miralenta. ||| They have launched accounts on Twitter and Facebook to raise awareness about the campaign as well as gender inequality issues in the country.
Eo amin'ny laharana faha-120 amin'ny firenena 128 no misy an'i Ejypta mikasika ny tsy fitovian'ny lehilahy sy ny vehivavy. ||| Egypt is ranked number 120 among 128 countries when it comes to gender inequality.

Ny tanjontsika amin'ny fidirana aterineto dia ny tsy mampahafantatra ny vehivavy ao an-tanàna, fa manentana ireo sokajin'olona eo no eo sy ny ambony. ||| The goal of our presence online is not the reach the women in villages, but to raise awareness about the campaign among middle and upper class.

Nicu Popescu, bilaogera, dia tonga amin'ny fanomezana tohankevitra hanoherana ny "filazana diso be" izay naely tao anatin'ity fifamalian-dresaka ity. ||| Blogger Nicu Popescu has come up with arguments combating the "main false statements" that have been circulated within this debate.
Tohankevitra diso 1: "Mba misy fiangonana firy moa any Arabia Saodita koa nahoana isika no tsy tsy maintsy hanome alalana ny maoske aty Moldavia" ||| False argument 1: "How many churches are in Saudi Arabia and why do we have to allow mosques in Moldova"
Tsy tiako mihitsy hianatra an'i Arabia Saodita na amin'ny lafiny inona na lafiny inona i Moldavia. ||| I do not want Moldova to imitate in any way Saudi Arabia.
Ny tadiaviko dia ny mba hahafahan'ny vehivavy eto Moldavia mamily fiara, mivoaka ny trano, ary ny fanjakana tsy hifangaro amin'ny fiangonana. ||| I want the women in Moldova to be able to drive cars, go out, and the state to be separate from the church.
Izay olona rehetra te-haka tahaka an'i Arabia Saodita dia olona tsy mikatsaka velively izay tsara ho an'ity firenena ity. ||| Whoever wants to imitate Saudi Arabia are the people who do not desire good for this country.
Ireo vondrom-piarahamonina Kristianina ao Siria sy Ejipta no nataony ho ohatra, izay eo amin'ny 10% eo amin'ny mponina any no Kristianina ary miasa tsy misy sakana ny fiangonana: ||| He brings up the example of the Christian communities in Syria and Egypt, where approximately 10 percent of the population are Christian and churches are fully functioning:
Mampalahelko fa tafakatra avo ny tsy fahaiza-mandefitra ara-pinoana ananan'ny vahoaka Moldavy mitaha amin'ny manampahefana Siriana sy Ejiptiana – fanjakana tsy refesi-mandidy, izay tato anatin'ny volana vitsy dia namono ny vahoakany ihany, saingy andanin'izay dia mankato ihany koa ny finoana kristianina ary niaro ny fiangonana tamin'ny vanimpotoana samihafa nanoloana ireo fanafihan'ireo Silamo mahery fihetsika. ||| It is regrettable that some Moldovan citizens have a higher degree of religious intolerance than the Syrian or Egyptian authorities – authoritarian states, which in the last months have killed their own citizens, but which at the same time recognize the Christian religion and have on many occasions protected the churches from attacks by radical Muslims.
Tohankevitra diso 2: "Tsy mifanaraka amin'ny tantara sy ny fomban-drazana eto amin'ity firenena ity mihitsy ny fivavahana Silamo, ary ny ankamaroan'ny Kristiana dia manohitra ny fankatoavana azy io" ||| False argument 2: "Islam does not correspond to the history and traditions of this land and the Christian majority is against its recognition"
Tsy iombonako hevitra izany. ||| I disagree.
Inoako fa tokony hanaja ny vitsy an'isa ara-pinoana i Moldavia, tafiditra anatin'izany ny Silamo; ary ny fanjakana tsy Kristiana toa an'i Siria na Sina dia tokony hanaja ny zon'ireo Kristiana vitsy an'isa. ||| I believe Moldova has to respect the religious minorities, including the Muslim one; and the non-Christian states like Syria or China have to respect the rights of the Christian minorities.
Tohankevitra diso 3: "Silamo sy Fampihorohoroana" ||| False argument 3: "Muslims and terrorism"
Aoka isika tsy hivazivazy. ||| Let's be serious.
Tena misy olona mihevitra ve fa ny mpifikitra fatratra amin'ny fivavahana Silamo dia mila fanoratana ara-panjakana mba hahafahany manao asa fampihorohoroana? ||| Does anyone really believe that fundamentalist Muslims need to be legally registered in order to commit terrorist attacks?
Sahala amin'ny hoe nanandrana ny hanoratra ara-panjakana ny trano fivavahany tany Etazonia ery i Bin Laden talohan'ny 11 Septambra. ||| As if Bin Laden tried to register his prayer house in the U.S. before September 11.
Ary ny fifandraisan'ny finoana sy ny asa fampihorohoroana/tsy fandeferana dia tena zava-tsarotra. ||| And the connection between religion and terrorism/radicalism is a bit more complex.
Ny any Afovoany Atsinanana dia faritra sarotra tokoa izay ahitàna ny vondrom-piarahamonina rehetra izay samy nanao zava-doza avokoa– Silamo, Jiosy, Kristiana. ||| The Middle East is a complex region where all communities have committed a number of crimes – Muslims, Jews, Christians.
Tohankevitra diso 4 "Stefan cel Mare sy ireo razambentsika dia niady nanohitra ny Silamo/Tiorka, ary tsy ho isika ankehitriny no hamela azy ireo hanao izay haha-ara-dalàna ny finoan-dry zareo" ||| False argument 4 "Stefan cel Mare and our ancestors fought Muslims/Turks, and we cannot allow them to now legalize their religion"
Ary raha niady tamin'i Rosia i Moldavia, dia ho nandràra ny fiangonana Rosiana koa ve isika? ||| And if Moldova had fought against Russia, do we have to interdict the Russian church?
Mila miady amin'ireo hevitra voizin'ny finoana hafa ny fiangonana ao Moldavia hanaporofoany fa izy no mendrika, akaiky indrindra ny vahoaka, manana pretra manam-pahaizana, nahita fianarana kokoa sy lavitry ny kolikoly, sns., ary tsy amin'ny fanaovana tsindry be fahatany amin'ny fanjakana Moldavy, izay tokony hitoetra ho tsy miandany amin'ny resaka finoana. ||| The church of Moldova has to combat the ideas promoted by other religions by demonstrating that it is better, closer to the citizens, has smarter, more educated and less corrupted priests, etc., and not through hysterical pressures on the Moldovan state, which has to be neutral in religious affairs.
Bilaogera iray hafa, i Vlad Cubreacov, no mitondra ho ao anatin'ny fifanakalozan-dresaka ny hevitra hoe ny fanosehana ny Silamo ho ivelan'ny lalàna dia mitondra mankany amin'ny fifanenjanana ara-pinoana eto amin'ny firenena, nefa koa mety hitarika any amin'ny fifanolanana amin'ireo mpiara-miasa avy any ivelany: ||| Another blogger, Vlad Cubreacov, brings into the debate the idea that putting Muslims outside the law would only degrade the religious climate in the country, but also could lead to some tensions with external partners:
Efa fantatra amin'ny ankapobeny fa ny firenena toa an'i Israely, ny Federasiona Rosiana, Armenia na Azerbaidjan dia mora tohina amin'ny fomba fitondràna an'ireo vitsy an'isa avy any aminy tonga any amin'ny firenen-kafa. ||| It is a generally-known fact that states like Israel, the Russian Federation, Armenia or Azerbaijan are sensitive to the way their minorities are treated in other countries.
Azontsika eritreretina fa ny fanafoanana ny fanoratana araka ny lalàna ny Ligy Islamika ao Moldavia dia hiteraka olana eo amin'ny fifandraisan'i Chisinau sy Baku na Mosko. ||| We can assume that cancelling the registration of the Islamic League in Moldova can raise problems in the relations between Chisinau and Baku or Moscow.
Resy lahatra izahay fa ny vondrom-piarahamonina Silamo iray voafehy anaty faritry ny lalàna sy ampidirina ho ao anaty fiaraha-monina dia tsara kokoa raha ampitahaina amin'ny iray hafa atosika ho any ivelany hanao ny ataony fotsiny any, lasibatra marefo ho an'ireo Silamo mahery fihetsika. ||| We believe that a Muslim community maintained within the legal system and integrated into the society is preferred to one that is left on its own account, an easy target to all kinds of integralists and Islamic fundamentalists.
Tsy arak'i Vlada Ciobanu ||| Vlada Ciobanu does not understand
Nahoana no feno Moldavy maro any ivelany, ary fiangonana sy pretra Ortodoksa maro afaka manao ny asany manerana izao tontolo izao, inona no ilàntsika manao diabe hilanja sary sy hazofijaliana ka tsy hamela ny olona hafa hisitraka ny fahalalahany. ||| Why when there are so many Moldovans abroad, and many churches and Orthodox priests can hold their services around the world, do we have to go out with icons, crosses and not let other people enjoy freedom.
Yemen: Saritaka ao Sanaa amin'ny vaovao mifanohitra momba an'i Saleh ||| Yemen: Confusion in Sanaa Amid Conflicting News on Saleh
Tafalatsaka anaty korontana tanteraka ny renivohitra Yemenita Sanaa nandritra ity folakandro ity, noho ny fisian'ny vaovao mifanohitra momba ny filoha Yemenita Ali Abdullah Saleh. ||| The Yemeni capital Sanaa plunged into chaos this afternoon, with conflicting reports circulating about Yemeni president Ali Abdullah Saleh.
Raha milaza ny sasany fa nandao ny lapam-panjakana ao Sanaa izy, ny hafa kosa nitatitra fa naratra izy nandritra ny fifandonana nitranga. ||| While some reports say he had fled the presidential palace in Sanaa, others are reporting that he was injured in clashes.

Ho fehiny, ny filoha Yemenita Saleh dia/tsy dia/mety/angamba/heverina/araka ny Twitter/ Araka ny Reuters/karazany/iza no mahalala hoe maty. ||| SoNiteraka fanantenana eto amin'ny tontolon'ny siokantsera, ny vaovao nampaharatra an'i Saleh, sy ny mety ho fahafatesany, ka iray sisa ny mpanao didijadona tavela any amin'ny tontolo Arabo. ||| News of Saleh's injuries, and possible death, raised hope in the Twittersphere, that the Arab world will soon have one less dictator.
Efa hatry ny elaela isika no niaina fialan'ny mpanao Didijadona andro Zoma. ||| We are long overdue a Friday of Departure of Despised Dictator.

Porto Riko: Diabe Hanoherana Ny Fantsom-pitaterana Solika ||| Puerto Rico: March Against the Pipeline
An-jatony ireo olona manerana ny nosy iray manontolo no nandray anjara tamin'ilay "Diabe Nasionaly: Mijoro manohitra mafy ny Fantsom-pitaterana Solika i Porto Riko" izay notanterahana ny Alahady 19 Febroary 2012, tany an-tanànan'i San Juan, renivohitri' Porto Riko. ||| Hundreds of people across the whole island joined the "National March: Puerto Rico stands firm against the Pipeline" that took place on Sunday 19 February, 2012, in the city of San Juan, the capital of Puerto Rico.
Nizotra avy any amin'ny Capitol (Mpanao lalàna) ka hatrany amin'ny Lapan'ireo Governora (La Fortaleza) ireo mpanao fihetsiketsehana ho fandàvana ilay antsoina hoe "Fomba Maitso," tetikasa natolotry ny fitantanan'ny governora Luis Fortuño, izay mikasa hanangana fantsona manana halàva 92 miles mba hitaterana solika avy any amin'ny morontsiraka atsimon'ny nosy mankany San Juan, any amin'ny morontsiraka avaratra, mamakivaky ireo tangoron-tendrombohitra ao afovoany. ||| The demonstrators marched from the Capitol (the Legislature) to the Governors Mansion (La Fortaleza) in rejection of the so-called "Green Way," a project proposed by the administration of the governor Luis Fortuño, which is looking to build a 92-mile-long tube to carry natural gas from the south coast of the island to San Juan, on the north coast, through the central mountain range.
Nokarakarain'ilay fikambanambe Casa Pueblo mipetraka any amin'ny vohitr'i Adjuntas io diabe io. ||| The march was organized by the community organization Casa Pueblo based in the town of Adjuntas.
Nitarika ireo fikasàna hanakana ilay antsoina hoe "Fomba Maitso" ny Casa Pueblo. ||| Casa Pueblo has led the attempts to put a stop to the so-called "Green Way".
Niteny ireo mpiaro ny tontolo iainana fa, raha mitohy io tetikasa io, hanana fiantraikany ratsy eo amin'ireo rano any ambanin'ny tany sy ireo ala misy azy izany, hitarika fahasimbana tsy azo amboarina intsony eo amin'ny firindran'ny zavaboarin'ny nosy. ||| Environmentalists have argued that, if the project goes ahead, it would have a negative impact on the aquifers and rain forests on its path, causing irreparable damage to the island's ecosystem.
Ireo fikambanana malaza eny ifotony sy ny vahoaka manohitra ny fanamboarana io fantsom-pitaterana solika io dia niantso izany ho "Fantson'ny Fahafatesana." ||| Grassroots organizations and people against the construction of the pipeline have called it the "Pipeline of Death".
Mizara sary vitsivitsy izay nalainy nandritra io fihetsiketsehana io ny mpanao gazety amin'ny alalan'ny sary Ricardo Alcaraz. ||| Photojournalist Ricardo Alcaraz shares some of the images he shot of the demonstration.
Nandray anjara tamin'io fihetsiketsehana io ny vahoaka avy any amin'ireo sehatry ny fiaraha-monina sivily rehetra. ||| People from all sectors of civil society joined the demonstration.
Nandeha avy any amin'ny Capitol ka nankany amin'ny Fortaleza ireo mpanao fihetsiketsehana. ||| The protesters marched from the Capitol to the Fortaleza.
Mahita ny lafiny andrefan'ny Trano Olaimpika ianao ao aoriana, foiben-toeran'ny komity ny Olaimpika nasionaly. ||| In the background you can see the west side of Olympic House, the headquarters of the national Olympic committee.
Nitaraina ireo sehatra samihafa fa mety hitarika fahasimbana goavana eo amin'ny zavaboahary ao amin'ny nosy io tetikasa io. ||| Various sectors have complained that the project would cause serious damage to the flora and fauna of the island.
Karazana zavaboahary maro tandindomin-doza no miaina ao amin'ny làlan'io fantsom-pitaterana solika natolotra io. ||| Several endangered species live on the proposed pipeline route.
Nandray anjara tamin'io fihetsiketsehana io ihany koa ilay mpikambana ao amin'ny Kongresy Luis Gutiérrez. ||| Congressman Luis Gutiérrez also joined the demonstration.
Nisy hetsika maro natao nandritra io diabe io. ||| There were a number of performances along the march.
Rakotry ny sainam-pirenenan'i Porto Riko ||| Wrapped with the Puerto Rican flag

Egypta: Miketrika valifaty ny Minisitry ny atitany ||| Egypt: The Ministry of Interior Seeks Revenge
Amin'ny fampiasana ny blaogin'izy ireo, ny finday, ary ireo media vaovao, dia nitatitra tranga fampijaliana maro nataon'ireo mpitandro filaminana tato anatin'ny taona vitsivitsy lasa ireo mafana fo Ejiptiana. ||| Using their blogs, mobile phones, and new media, Egyptian activists have exposed numerous torture incidents by police officers over the past few years.
Ny tranga teny nalaza indrindra dia ny an'i Emad El Kebir, izay nampijaliana sy novetavetain'i Islam Nabih sy Reda Fathi - mpitandro filaminana roa niatrika fitsaràna taorian'ny niparitahan'ny horonantsarin'ilay fampijaliana. ||| The most famous incident is that of Emad El Kebir, who was tortured and sodomized by Islam Nabih and Reda Fathi - the police officers who were brought to justice after the torture video went viral.
Ary ny vao haingana indrindra dia ny fampijaliana mahery vaika sy famonoana mahatsiravina an'i Khaled Said - Ejiptiana 28 taona avy any amin'ny tanàna amorontsirak'i Alexandria izay maty noho ny fangatahana ny taratasy fiantsoana azy. ||| And the most recent of which is the severe torture and brutal murder of Khaled Said - a 28-year-old Egyptian from the coastal city of Alexandria who died for asking for a search warrant.
Ny lahatsoratra farany indrindra navoakan'i Amr Gharbeia dia mitondra ny lohateny hoe: ||| Amr Gharbeia 's most recent post is entitled:
Mijoro manoloana ny fampijaliana. ||| Standing in the face of torture.
Izy ity dia mikasika ny tetikadin'ny olona sivily mba hanoherana ny fampijaliana. ||| It is about the civil society's most recent anti-torture initiative.
Ny tranga fampijaliana niseho farany indrindra, izay nanala ny ain'i Khaled Said dia nanamafy ny hafanam-po enti-manohitra ny fampijaliana, ka mametraka izany ho anisan'ireo antony mampihemotra ny olona amin'ny fitakiana ny zon'izy ireo hanana fiainana tsaratsara kokoa. ||| The most recent torture incident that took the life of Khaled Said rekindled activism against torture, placing it among the leading factors that discourage people from claiming their rights to a better life.
Osa loatra ireo olona eo ambany fanaraha-maso ka tsy afaka hiaro ny tenany; sady andraikitry ny fiaraha-monin'izy ireo ny mitandro ny fandriampahalemany sy ny filaminany. ||| People in custody are too weak to defend themselves; thus their safety and security is the responsibility of their society.
Androany, dia nisy tranonkala iray vaovao miady amin'ny fampijaliana nisokatra. ||| Today, a new site combating torture is activated.
Maro ireo fikambanana mpiaro ny zon'olombelona sy ireo olon-tokana mpiaro avy amina foto-kevitra samihafa no ao ambadik'ity tranonkala ity, izay iarahan-dry zareo miasa amin'ny fanoroana ireo niharan'ny fampijaliana toro-hevitra ara-psikolojika sy araka ny lalàna, amin'ny fitantaràna tranga hafa, amin'ny fifandraisana amin'ireo vondrona media mahazatra, ary amin'ny fanairana ny olona ho tonga saina amin'ny antony sy ny vokatr'izany. ||| Several human rights organizations and individual defenders from different paths of life are behind this site where they work together in offering torture victims psychological and legal counselling, exposing more incidents, reaching out to mainstream media organizations, and creating public awareness about the cause and its repercussions.
Ity tranonkala ity dia tohanan'ny The International Rehabilitation Council for Torture Victims (Filan-kevitra Iraisam-pirenena ho an'ny Famerenana ireo niharan'ny Fampijaliana ho aoa anaty fiarahamonina) any Copenhagen. ||| The new site is supported by The International Rehabilitation Council for Torture Victims in Copenhagen.
Ny vokatra voalohany vitan 'ity sehatra iraha-miasa ity dia " Ramy: Tantaran'ny tanànan'i Tamy El Amadeed " - sarimihetsika mikasika tovolahy iray avy amin'ny tanàna iray any Egypta izay nampijalian'ny mpitandro filaminana tamin'ny 2008 mba hiaiky famonoana izay tsy nataony velivaly. ||| The first fruits of this workforce is " Ramy: a Story from Tamy El Amadeed Village " - a movie about a young man from a village in Egypt who was tortured by the police in 2008 to confess to a murder he did not commit.
Raha ny voalazan'i Wael Abbas,toa miketrika valifaty avy amin'ireo namoaka ireo trangana kolikoly ataon'ny mpitandro filaminana sy ny fampijaliana mifanesy ny Ministeran'ny Atitany Ejiptiana. ||| According to Wael Abbas, it seems that the Egyptian Ministry of Interior is seeking revenge from those who exposed internal police force corruption and recurrent torture cases.
Wael dia nahazo hafatra avy amin'i Sameh El Aroosy izay nizara horonantsary maro mikasika ireo fampijaliana any amin'ireo tobin'ny mpitandro ny filaminana ilazany fa voasambotra tany Libya izy. ||| Wael received a message from Sameh El Aroosy who shared many video clips of torture in police stations saying that he has been arrested in Libya.
Nanapa-kevitra ny hanenjika ireo izay namoaka ireto fampijaliana manafintohina nataony ireto ny Minisiteran'ny atitany. ||| The Ministry if Interior has decided to settle accounts with those who have exposed its torture scandals.
Raha ny hita mazava dia mandingana ny sisintany Ejiptiana ny tànany mitady valifaty. ||| Obviously its vindictive arm reaches beyond the Egyptian borders.
Hiangaviana ianao hanampy ireo "mpanohitra ny fampijaliana". ||| Please help rescue "torture-busters".

Nizeria: Misaritaka, Miandry Ny Fahatongavanà Vehivavy Iray? ||| Nigeria: Adrift, Awaiting the Arrival of a Woman?
Atolotro an'i TJ, namako ao amin'ny vohikala Facebook, ny lohatenin'ity lahatsoratra ity-: ||| I owe the title of this post to my Facebook friend - TJ:
Maro ireo Nizeriana no tsy mahalala fa misavoritaka i Nizeria iray manontolo miandry ny fahatongavan'ilay vehivavy iray... ||| Most Nigerians don't know, that all of Nigeria is adrift, awaiting the arrival of a woman...

naniry aho ny hahalala ny nahatonga zainy zavatra rehetra izao. ||| I wish I could say why all this happened.

Firaisan-kina sy fiaretana no lakilen'ny fandresentsika hatramin'izao. ||| Solidarity and resistance have been the secret of our victory so far.

Nitsahatra ny rivotra be tamin'ny 30 may kanefa vokatry ny fahalehibeazan'ny fahavoazana, dia naato ny fianarana any an-tsekoly hatramin'ny 04 jona ary ao anatin'ny fampitandremana loza ny firenena manontolo. ||| The storm dissipated on May 30 but due to the large amount of damages, School classes have been suspended until June 4th and the entire country is on alert.

Nambara ny fiantsoana firenena ho anaty hamehana tany Goatemala satria namely mafy ny faritra afovoan'i Amerika ny rivo-doza niaraka tamin'ny orambe. ||| A state of emergency has been declared in Guatemala as the storms heavy rain thrashes through Central America.
Niteraka fikorianan'ny atsanga (fotaka be) i Agatha ary namotika trano maro sy fananana maro, nanapaka lalana ary niteraka tahotra sy horohoro manerana ny faritra rehetra sady ao koa ny mety hipoahan'ny volokano. ||| 'Agatha's' heavy rain has caused mud-slides which are destroying houses and businesses alike, cutting off roads and causing fear and panic throughout the region and there is a risk of a volcanic eruption.
