Syria: Ny lahatsoratra tsara indrindra sa ny faran'izay ratsy e? ||| Syria: The Best or the Worst Article Ever?
Iray amin'ireo takela-by any Syria maneho ny Filoha Bashar al-Assad ||| One of many billboards in Syria featuring President Bashar al-Assad
Matetika ireo mpitoraka blaogy Siriana no manakiana lahatsoratry ny mpivahiny momba ny firenen-dry zareo - mazàna izy ireny no "stereotypical" loatra, indraindray moa dia diso tanteraka. ||| Syrian bloggers frequently decry travel writing about their country - often it's too stereotypical, sometimes downright false.
Ary ho an'ny firenena izay tondroina ho "nitoka-monina" ela, fara-faharatsiny avy any Etazonia, tena mankarary manokana ny saina ny mahita ny lahatsoratra toy izany ka asandratra ho toy ny zava-marina. ||| And for a country considered long "isolated" at least from the United States, it can be particularly frustrating to see such writing promoted as accurate.
Kanefa, nony nahatsikaritra lahatsoratra iray nivoaka tamin'ny National Geographic noheveriny fa "ny tsara indrindra amin'ny lahatsoratra miresaka an'i Syria tanatin'ireo folotaona farany," i Sasa, Siriana mpitoraka blaogy be mpahalala, mpamahana ny blaogy Syria News Wire zavatra tsotra no azony nolazaina: ||| Therefore, when popular Syrian blogger Sasa, who pens the blog Syria News Wire spotted a recent piece in National Geographic that he deemed "the best article on Syria in a decade," he just had to say something:
Ny tena Syria marina no lazain'ity lahatsoratra ity. ||| This article is the real Syria.
Mampibaribary ireo teboka maro efa fantatry ny Siriana mikasika ny fireneny, saingy hodian'ireo mpanao gazety vahiny tsy hita (na dinganina), noho ny fahamaizan'izy ireny hanamafy fotsiny ny stereotypes-ny. ||| It is a checklist of points which Syrians know about their country, but which foreign journalists skip over, in the rush to confirm their own stereotypes.
Tsy atao mahagaga, matetika ao anaty firenena voasamatsamaka, tsy ny olona rehetra no homba ny fandalinan'i Sasa ilay lahatsoratra. ||| Unsurprisingly, in a country often divided, not everyone agreed with Sasa's interpretation of the article.
Imad Moustapha, Masoivoho Siriana any Etazonia (sady mpitoraka blaogy rahateo) dia nandefa taratasy ho an'ny tonian-dahatsoratry ny National Geographic izay nivoaka koa tao amin'ny blaogy Syria Comment, miantso ny lahatsoratry ny National Geographic ho "fanehoana diso momba an'i Syria izay tany niaviako." ||| Syrian Ambassador to the United States Imad Moustapha (himself a blogger) penned a letter to the editor of National Geographic that was republished on the blog Syria Comment, calling the National Geographic article a "misrepresentation of the Syria that I belong to".
Ny mpametraka fanamarihana, Alex avy amin'ny Creative Syria dia nanakiana ilay lahatsoratry ny National Geographic, amin'ny filazana hoe: ||| Commenter Alex of Creative Syria was critical of the National Geographic article, stating:
Tsy dia asiako olana loatra ny ankabeazan'izay voasoratra.. fa manana olana aho amin'ny fananako fahatsapana fa ny 90% amin'ilay lahatsoratra dia ny zavatra miiba no resahany ... Tsy mieritreritra aho hoe Amerikana mpamaky iray no hanisy fisalasalàna hanafoana ny fialantsasatra efa nomaniny mialoha hatao any Syria. ||| I have no problem with most of what was written.. but I have an issue with the obvious impression the article leaves through its 90% emphasis on negativity ... I don't think an American reading it will hesitate to cancel his planned first vacation in Syria.
Iza no hahalatsa-kanina ao Bab Touma raha misy Siriana mahantra mitolona ho an'ny demaokrasia ampijaliana ao ambadiky ny varavaran'i Bab Touma ao? ||| Who wants to enjoy lunch in Bab Touma if poor brave Syrian people fighting for democracy are being tortured next door in Bab Touma?
Mpametraka fanamarihana hafa indray, Ghassan, nankafia ilay lahatsoratra: ||| Another commenter, Ghassan, liked the article:
tena mifototra amin'ny zava-misy ilay lahatsoratra, araka ny tokony ho izy, ary tsy iadian-kevitra. ||| the articale is rational, reasonable, and accurate.
Manohana ny NG aho, ary ny fampitam-baovao sy fitenenana malalaka izay tsy misy ao Syria. ||| my support to NG, and to the free press and speach which do not exist in syria.
Norman, dia nametraka fanamarihana ihany koa tamin'ny lahatsoratr'i Landis, ka nanamarika fa: ||| Norman, also commenting on Landis's post, aptly remarked:
Mahaliana ny hoe ahoana no tsy hiombon-kevitra amin'ity lahatsoratra ity i Syria tia ny Siriana rehetra. ||| It is interesting how Syria loving Syrians can disagree on the same article.
Mpitoraka blaogy maro hafa ivelan'i Syria no nihetsi-po mafy tamin'ilay lahatsoratry ny National Geographic. ||| Other bloggers outside of Syria had strong feelings about the National Geographic article as well.
Evan Hill, manoratra ao amin'ny blaogy iraisana The Majlis, dia nahatsapa fa mametraka an'i Syria ho toy ny tavela aoriana (taraiky tsy maharaka toetr'andro) ilay lahatsoratra, ka manamarika fa: ||| Evan Hill, who writes for group blog The Majlis, felt that the article displayed Syria as behind the times, stating:
Isika dia tavela miaraka amina Syria mihisatra, ara-toekarena sy ara-politika, amina toe-tsaina antitra be efa ho 40 taona be izao raha kely indrindra. ||| We're left with a Syria that seems stuck, economically and politically, in a mindset that's at least 40 decades old.

Palestina: Ny Fisondrotana Kilasy any Gaza ||| Palestine: School Graduation In Gaza
tawjihi dia ny fanadinana ankapobeny aorian'ny dingana faharoa any amin'ny faritr'i Gaza, sisiny andrefan'i Jordana, ary mamaritra ny safidin'ny mpianatra iray momba izay anjerimanontolo sy ny sampana horaisiny. ||| The tawjihi is the general secondary examination in Gaza, the West Bank and Jordan, and it determines a student's choice of university and major.
Tamin'ity taona ity, ny fiatrehana miaraka ny fanadinana any amin'ny sisiny andrefana sy ao Gaza dia noraisina ho toy ny taratry ny firaisam-pirenena sahady. ||| The fact that this year the exams were held simultaneously in the West Bank and Gaza was hailed as a sign of national unity.

Nampiasa ny vatatenany indray ny maro amin'ireo maherifo naratra hiantohana ny zon'izy ireo ara-drariny hahazo ny fitsaboana sahaza azy ireo, sy ny zavatra tsotra indrindra azontsika atolotra azy ireo. ||| So some of the wounded heroes resorted to fighting, once again using their bodies, to guarantee their legitimate right for treatment, which is the simplest thing we can offer them.
Rehefa avy nandondom-baravarana hatraiza hatraiza nefa akatontsika aminy hatrany hatrany izany dia indreo ry zareo nitokona tsy hihinan-kanina, taloha kelin'ny fifidianana. ||| After knocking on every door, which were shut in their faces again and again, they went on an open hunger strike shortly before the elections.

Horohorontany goavana no nisy tany Padang, Sumatra Andrefana nanodidina ny tamin'ny 5ora hariva (ora teny an-toerana) ny Alarobia teo. ||| A strong earthquake hit Padang, West Sumatra around 5 PM local time Wednesday.
Niteraka faharavan-trano lehibe sy tra-boina maro ilay horohoron-tany tany ambany ranomasina izay mirefy 7.6 amin'ny maridrefy Richter, indrindra tany amin'ny faritr'i Pariaman, izay morontsiraka any Padang. ||| The undersea quake measuring 7.6 on Richter Scale has caused massive building damage and casualties, mainly around Pariaman, a coastal area of Padang.

Fampidirana ny feo voarahona ||| Introducing Threatened Voices
Tsy mbola nisy hatramin'izay hamaroan'olona voarahona na voagadra noho ny zavatra nosoratany tamin'ny aterineto. ||| Never before have so many people been threatened or imprisoned for what the words they write on the internet.
Koa satria moa nitombo aoka izany ny olo-tsotra no nampiasa ny aterineto hanehoany ny heviny sy ifandraisany amin'ny hafa, dia maro ihany koa ny mpitondra fanjakana no nanamafy ny fanaraha-maso, nanasivana, fitoriana eny amin'ny fitsarana ary ny fanorisorenana. ||| As activists and ordinary citizens have increasingly made use of the internet to express their opinions and connect with others, many governments have also increased surveillance, filtering, legal actions and harassment.
Ny tena henjana indrindra amin'ny maro dia ny fisamborana ny mpamaham-bolongana noho ny resaka politika nosoratany an-tserasera sy/na an-toeran-kafa, ary misy aza indrisy ny mitarika hatrany amin'ny fahafatesana. ||| The harshest consequence for many has been the politically motivated arrest of bloggers and online writers for their online and/or offline activities, in some tragic cases even leading to death.
Mahatratra ny 45%-n'ny mpiasan'ny fampitam-baovao mameno ny fonja ankehitriny no mpanao gazety an-tserasera sy mpamaham-bolongana avokoa. ||| Online journalists and bloggers now represent 45% of all media workers in prison worldwide.
Ankehitriny, namoaka vohikala vaovao antsoina hoe Threatened Voices (feo voarahona) indray ny Global Voices Advocacy (Global Voices mpisolovava) ho entina manara-maso ny fanapenam-bava an-tserasera. ||| Today, Global Voices Advocacy is launching a new website called Threatened Voices to help track suppression of free speech online.
Mampiseho ny sarintanin'izao tontolo izao sy ny fivoarana misy ka hanampy amin'ny fitopaza-maso ny trangam-pandrahonana sy fisamborana mety hahazo ny mpamaham-bolongana manerantany izy io, ary ho ivon-tsehatra fanangonam-baovao avy aminn'y fikambanana sy mpikatroka tena mavitrika, ka tafiditra ao ny Vaomiera miaro ny mpamaha-bolongana, Fikambanana Arabo miaro ny Zon'olombelona eo amin'ny vaovao, Mpanangom-baovao tsy voasakan-tsisintany (Reporters Sans Frontieres), Human Rights Watch (Mpiaro ny Zon'olombelona), CyberLaw Blog, Amnesty International, Komity mpiaro ny mpanao gazety, Global Voices Advocacy. ||| It features a world map and an interactive timeline that help visualize the story of threats and arrests against bloggers worldwide, and it is a central platform to gather information from the most dedicated organisations and activists, including Committee to Protect Bloggers, The Arabic Network for Human Rights Information, Reporters without Borders, Human Rights Watch, CyberLaw Blog, Amnesty International, Committee to Protect Journalists, Global Voices Advocacy.
Mpamaham-bolongna inona ary Aiza? ||| What blogger, where?
Maro ny antony mahasarotra ny mikaro-baovao miresaka mpanoratra an-tserasera sy mpamaham-bolongana voarahona sy voasambotra. ||| Finding accurate information about arrested and threatened bloggers and online writers is difficult for several reasons.
Voalohany, sarotra dia sarotra ny mamantatra azy noho ny tsiambaratelo manodidina ny fanasivanana an-tserasera sy ny fangejana. ||| First, the secrecy surrounding online censorship and repression makes it extra difficult to be accurate.
Tsy misy herinandro izay tsy andrenesana mpanao gazety an-tserasera hafa na mpikatroka voasambotra amina firenena tahaka an'i Ejipta na Iran, saingy zavamiafina tanteraka matetika ny anton'ny fisamborana sy ny antsipiriany. ||| Not a single week passes without stories of arrests of yet another online journalist or activist in countries like Egypt or Iran, but the details and reasons are often shrouded in mystery.
Faharoa, mbola mifangaroharo be hatramin'izao ny famaritana ny antsoina hoe "mpamaham-bolongana". ||| Second, there is still some confusion about the definition of a "blogger".
Mihamaro dia mihamaro ny mpanao gazety matihanina no mikisaka mankany amin'ny gazety an-tserasera sy mamaham-bolongana fa any nomisy fahafahana kokoa, ka manasaritaka ny famaritana napetraka teo aloha. ||| Professional journalists are increasingly migrating to online media and blogs in pursuit of more freedom, blurring the old lines of definition.
Ary maro amin'ireo antsoina hoe cyber-dissidents any Shina, Tonizia, Vietnam, na Iran no tsy manana bolongana ho azy manokana. ||| And many so-called cyber-dissidents in China, Tunisia, Vietnam, or Iran, do not have personal blogs.
Misy ihany koa ny fotoana noho ny zavatra natao amin'ny fiainana andavanandro no isamborana ilay mpamaham- bolongana fa tsy amin'izay navoakany an-tserasera. ||| Other times, bloggers are arrested for their offline activity, rather than for what they have published online.
Io fisavoritahana io no manasarotra ho an'ny mpiaro ny fahalalaham- pitenenana an-tserasera amin'ny fametrahana teti-panorona mahomby sy ahazoana fiaraha-miasa matotra hiarovana ny mpamaham-bolongana sy ny mpitolona an-tserasera, fa efa tena zava-dehibe aloha ny manandrana aloha. ||| This confusion has sometimes made it hard for online free speech advocates to come up with a good strategies and partnerships to defend bloggers and online activists, but it has never been more important to try.
Andao hiara-miasa ||| Let's work together
Mitarika ny vondrona mpanoratra, tonia sy mpandika teny izahay ato amin'ny Global Voices, mampahalala anay amin'izay mety hisiana fihoaram-pefy rehetra mikasika ny fahalalaham-pitenenana sy ny zon'olombelona. ||| At Global Voices we engage a community of authors, editors, and translators, who help keep us all informed of free speech and human rights abuses.
Kendrentsika ny hanakaikezana ny olona rehetra mety hanam-baovao mikasika izany miaraka amin'ny Threatened Voices. ||| With Threatened Voices we aim to open the process of reporting up even further to any person who has information.
Miantso izay rehetra manana havana, namana, mpiray tanindrazana izay efa nahazo fandrahonana izahay mba hametraka ao sy hilaza ny vaovao farany y mombamomba ireo izay nanjavona na voasambotra, mba ahafahanay mikaroka loharanom-baovao hafa, hanamarina, sy hametraka rohy an-tserasera natokana mba hanafahana azy ireny. ||| We're calling on those whose friends, relatives, colleagues, or compatriots, have been threatened to help create and update the profiles of those missing or under arrest, so we can seek additional sources, verify, and link to online campaigns dedicated to freeing them.
Amin'ny alalan'io fomba io, dia manantena izahay hahalala bebe kokoa hoe oviana, taiza ary tamin'ny fomba inona na nanao ahoana no nahatonga ny mpamaham-bolongana ho voahosihosy ny zony any amin'ny firenentsamihafa any, mba hahafahana mizara ny vaovao amin'ny mpanao gazety, mpikaroka, ary ny mpikatroka, sy hananganantsika aterineto ahafahan'ny rehetra mampihatra ny zony hiteny amin-kahalalahana, ary mba tsy hanadinoana ireo mpamaham-bolongana any am-ponja. ||| In the process, we are hoping to learn more about when, where, and to what extent bloggers are being subjected to abuse in different countries, so we can share that information widely with journalists, researchers, and activists, and work towards creating an internet where everyone can exercise their right to speak freely, and where bloggers in prison are not forgotten.
Aelezo maneratany. ||| Help spread the word.

Tarataratra fa tahaka ny manaraka izany fomba ratsy izany ihany koa ny Blogspotn'ny Google, ary dia nosakanany tsy nisy antony mazava ihany koa ny Bolongan'i Nawara Negm (Tahyees). ||| Apparently, Google's Blogspot has decided to join the bandwagon, and has blocked Nawara Negm's Blog (Tahyees), without specifying any reasons.
Ankehitriny dia nanoratra momba ny bolongana iray hafa nanjavona ihany koa i Ahmed El Sabbagh: ||| Now, Ahmed El Sabbagh writes a post about yet another blog that has vanished:
Toy ny miatrika toe-javatra mampahonena mitovy hatrany isika. ||| We are very likely to face the same unfortunate situation.
Ekeko fa tsy hoe izay akory no faran'izao tontolo izao raha foana ny bolongana iray, ary mbola afaka mamorona bolongana tsaratsara kokoa hafa indray i winky, amin'izato toetrany maha-te-ho-tia, saingy tsy tokony hionona amin'izao ihany koa isika. ||| I know that deleting a blog is not the end of the world and that Winky, with her lovely spirit, could create a new and a better blog but still it is not the best of situations.
Manao izao sosokevitra izao i Ahmed El Boohy mba handefa izao hafatra manaraka izao any amin'ny Blogger isika amin'ny 10 desambra: ||| Ahmed El Boohy suggested that we all send the following message to Blogger on December 10:
Mpamaham-bolongana Ezipsiana izahay. ||| We are Egyptian bloggers.
Miangavy indrindra re mba tsy hofoanana tsy amin'ny antony na idirana an-tsehatra any amin'izay navoaka raha tsy nisy ny fandikana ny fifanarahana. ||| Please stop blocking the Egyptian blogs without cause and intervention in the published materials without violation terms of use.
Miangavy indrindra re mba aoka tsy handray ny toeran'ny mpanaramaso tsy mendrika manoloana ny bolonganay. ||| Please do not take the position of unjustified supervisor with our blogs.
MIANDRY VALINY IZAHAY. ||| WE WAIT FOR REPLY
Ary dia nanoratra ny fandraisana fepetra manokana ho fiarovana ihany koa izy ka nanoro ny handikana ny dika mitovy ny bolongana ao amin'ny solosaina: ||| He also posted a special note on precautionary measures and on how to keep a copy of your blog on your PC
Ankehitriny dia efa afaka manao dika mitovy ny bolonganao amina endrika dosie ao amin'ny solosainanao ianao ary afaka maka an'io raha sanatria tonga izay olana amin'ny bolonganao. ||| Now you can keep a copy of your blog in the form of a file on your PC and you can reload it in case you have trouble with your blog.
Fa nizara tamintsika ny tsiambaratelo ambadik'izao fanjavonana bolongana i Bella: ||| Bella also shared with us the secret behind the disappearance of blogs:
Nanokatra ny mailako toy ny mahazatra aho ka nahita ny hafatra avy amin'ny ekipan'ny Gmail amin'izato lohateny manaitra mampitandrina ahy fa ho very ny fisoratako anarana (mailaka) sy ny bolongako. ||| Today I opened my email as usual only to find a message from Gmail team with an alarming title in the subject line warning me against loosing my account and blog.
Ary dia nisy rohy moa nolazainy mba hotsindriana. ||| There was a link that I was asked to click.
Nangovitra aho na dia mieritreritra ny hahavery ny bolongana fotsiny aza na dia manana ny dika mitovy any amin'ny WordPress aza, nanontany ny hevitry ny namana iray aho. ||| I freaked out just thinking of loosing my blog although I have a copy on WordPress so I decided to consult a friend.
Soa ihany fa nahita an'i Mohamed El Gohary teo an-tserasera aho tao amin'ny MSN ary dia nalefako tany aminy ny dika mitovin'ny hafatra azoko. ||| Luckily I found Mohamed El Gohary online on MSN and I sent him a copy of the message I got.
Nolazainy ahy ary fa fandrika (scam) fampiasan'ny mpisovoka io mba hahazoany ny mailakanao sy hanafoanany ny bolonganao miaraka amin'ny votoatiny. ||| He told me that it is a scam used by hackers to take over your account and delete your blog and its content.
Faritr'i Sahel: Momba ny fandoavana tamby hanavotana ireo takalonaina ||| Sahel Region: On Paying Ransom for Hostages
Ny fakàna takalonaina nataona vondrona Islamika iray antsoina hoe Al-Qaeda in The Islamic Maghreb (AQIM) izao no malaza any amin'ny Faritr'i Sahel izay nipariaka nanerana ny firenena maro any avaratr'i Afrika. ||| Hostage-taking by a militant Islamist group called Al-Qaeda in The Islamic Maghreb (AQIM) is on the rise in the Sahel region which spans across several countries in the north of Africa.
Ho fanafahana ireo takalonaina dia manao tsindry ara-politika amin'ireo firenena Afrikana voakasika amin'izany ireo governemanta sy orinasa, na hizotra amin'ny fandoavana mivantana tamby ara-bola. ||| In order to free hostages, governments and companies have put political pressure on the African nations involved, or opted to pay ransoms directly.
Na izany aza, ny tetikasa hoe handoa tamby dia mazàna no dradraina ho tsy mahomby sy mampidi-doza ao anatin'ny fotoana maharitra. ||| However, the strategy of paying ransom is often decried as ineffective and dangerous in the long run.
Ny fakàna ankeriny tao Niger tamin'ny Septambra nakàna mpiasa miisa dimy avy amin'ny orinasa frantsay Areva mikirakira ny nokleary sy mpiasa roa avy amin'ny orinasa Satom dia manipika fa lasa faritra mena mamoa-doza izy ity any amin'ilay faritra. ||| The kidnapping in Niger in September of five employees of French nuclear company Areva and two employees of engineering-firm Satom underscores that this is becoming an increasingly dangerous region.
Nilaza ny maha-tompon'andraikitra azy tamin'ny fakàna ankeriny an'ireo olona fito (teratany Frantsay dimy, miampy teratany Togole iray, ary iray avy any Madagascar) ny AQIM. ||| AQIM has claimed responsibility for the seven kidnappings (five French citizens, plus one Togolese citizen, and one citizen of Madagascar).
Tamin'ny Aogositra 2010, nitatitra ny AFP fa takalon'aina espaniola roa nalain'ny AQIM no efa nafàhana rehefa nandoa vola ny governemanta Espaniola, ary nanamora ny fifanakalozana babo tamina mpaka ankeriny avy amin'ny AQIM voafonja tany Maoritania ny governemanta tao Mali. ||| In August 2010, AFP reported that two Spanish hostages captured by AQIM were freed when the Spanish government paid a ransom, and the government of Mali facilitated a prisoner exchange with a convicted AQIM kidnapper who was jailed in Mauritania.
Ny gazety an-tsoratra Alzeriana La Tribune dia nitatitra fa ny amiraly mibaiko ny andian-tafika frantsay any amin'ny faritra, Edouard Guillaud dia niteny hoe raha ny toerana raisin'i Frantsa nilazany fa "tsy tetikady mahomby" mihitsy ny fandoavana tamby dia tsy mandà ihany koa ry zareo raha toa ka mety mitranga izany làlana izany. ||| Algerian newspaper La Tribune reported that the admiral heading the French army in the region, Edouard Guillaud said that although France's position is that paying ransoms is "not a sustainable strategy" they would not exclude the possibility if circumstances called for it.
Tao anatina lahatsoratra iray mitondra ny lohateny hoe "Tamby ara-bola, fitaovana iray mahomby ho an'ny vondrona mpampihorohoro," dia manindry i Ali Boukhlef fa ny fandoavana tamby ara-bola dia fandrisihana sy fanohanana ny asa fampihorohoroana. ||| In an article entitled "Ransom, a formidable weapon for terrorist group," columnist Ali Boukhlef argues that payment of ransoms amounts to funding and support for terrorism.
Nahatonga ny mpandinika maro hametra-panontaniana manahiran-tsaina ny fakana ankeriny farany teo. ||| The recent hostage situation leads many observers to pose troubling questions.
ny zava-nisy momba ilay fakàna ankeriny dia mampanontany tena ny tsirairay amin'ny fahamoran'ny nanatanterahana ilay fakàna ankeriny, ka nanome varavarana misokatra ho an'ny manampahefana Frantsay hirotsaka ara-tafika. ||| the fact of the kidnapping have to make one wonder about the relative ease with which the kidnapping took place, giving the French authorities a golden opportunity to intervene with the army.
Raha ny marina, ny AREVA sy ny manampahefana Frantsay dia efa nahazo fampitandremana tamin'ny fomba maro samihafa fa tandindonin-doza ny mpiasan-dry zareo ao amin'ny toby fitrandrahana uranium ao Niger. ||| In fact, AREVA and the French authorities were alerted by various means that threats were looming on their employees at the Niger uranium mines.
Hatramin'izay, zara raha nisy ny fanamafisana ny fiarovana tokony hilaina ary sahala amin'ny hoe nandà ny fanampian'ny manampahefana avy ao Niger aza hoe ny AREVA. ||| Still, little was done to provide the necessary protection and it seems that AREVA even refused the help of the Niger authorities.
Ho fanoherana ny asan'ny AQIM izay mahazo vahana any amin'ny faritra rehetra akaikin'ny sisintanin'ny Sahel, ilay tranonkala Borkinabe San Finna dia mametra-panontaniana raha tokony hanome alalana ny fametrahana tobim-pamaharana tafika vahiny ao amin'ny tanin-dry zareo ireo firenena Afrikana. ||| To counter the activities of the AQIM that are expanding in all the regions at the border of the Sahel, the Burkinabe website San Finna questions if African states should allow foreign military bases on their territories.
Manome fomba fijery roa mifanohitra mikasika ity olana ity ilay tranonkala: Voalohany, Tomi, izay mankasitraka ny mety ho endrika fiaraha-miasa iraisam-pirenena rehetra dia miteny ny heviny: ||| The article offers two opposite viewpoints on the subject: First, Tomi, who is in favor of some form of international collaboration opines:
Olana maro samihafa toy ny fanondranana zava-mahadomelina, SIDA, fiparitahan'ny fitaovam-piadiana atomika, loto sy fampihorohoroana no tsy ho voavaha mihitsy raha tsy misy fiaraha-miasa iraisam-pirenena, ary tsy asiana resaka izay tanjaky ny firenena tsirairay amin'izany. ||| Many issues such as drug trafficking, AIDS, the spread of atomic weapons, pollution and terrorism cannot be resolved without international collaboration, no matter how powerful each individual nation is.
Atsy ankilany i Tozi manazava fa: ||| On the other hand, Tozi argues:
... Andiany vitsivitsy (tobin-tafika) etsy sy eroa ao Niger, Borkina Faso sy Maoritania tsy hahafongotra velively ny asa fampihorohoroana efa mamàka lalina ao Sahel. ||| ... A few elements (military bases) here and there in Niger, Burkina Faso and Mauritania will not get rid of the terrorism that has taken roots in Sahel.
Any Somalia, inona izao no mba efa vita hanoherana ny Shebabs sy ny mpikambana ao amin'ny Hezb al-Islam? ||| In Somalia, what was achieved against the Shebabs and the members of Hezb al-Islam?
Any Iraka ary indrindra indrindra fa ao Afghanistan, mba nisy nataontsika ve hamongorana ireo mpino mahery fihetsika ireo? ||| In Iraq and especially in Afghanistan, did we do anything to eradicate the religious fanatics?
Ny antony mampiroborobo ity zavatra ity dia satria mitombo be ny tahan'ny tsy mahay mamaky teny sy manoratra, ny mahantra, ny olona very fanantenana azon-dry zareo karamaina. ||| The reason this phenomenon grows is because there is a growing number of illiterate, impoverished, desperate people that they can recruit.
Raha isika no tsy manome izay fitaovana tena ilaina sy mirotsaka an-tsehatra amin'ny ady atao amin'ny fampihorohoroana, dia ho pehan'ny vondrona AQIM ny foto-drafitrasantsika, ho fatiny ny fizahantanintsika (ohatra fotsiny, manodidina ny 400,000 ny mpizahatany any Borkina Faso ary 900,000 any Senegal) ary izany no hiteraka karazan-korontana sy fivakisana ara-tsosialy maro samihafa. ||| If we don't give ourselves the necessary means and engage in this war against terrorism, the AQIM groups will hit our infrastructure, they will kill our tourism (about 400,000 tourists in Burkina Faso and 900,000 in Senegal for instance) and it will be the dawn of a whole new range of all kinds of trouble, and multiplied social fractures.
Mametraka izao fanontaniana manaraka izao ny bilaogy Mecanopolis: Inona marina moa ny AQIM ary iza no ao ambadik'izy io? ||| The Mecanopolis blog poses the following question: What exactly is AQIM and who is behind it?
Manoloana ny loza mitatao mandrakariva ateraky ny AQIM ao Sahel, tsy maintsy ialantsika ny sangodina tsy misy fiafaran'ny herisetra mba hitadiavantsika vahaolana maharitra hizorana mankamin'ny fandriampahalemana, na izany ho an'ny vahoakan'ny faritra, na ho an'ireo vahiny tonga ao mba honina na hiasa. ||| In view of the worrisome threat of AQIM in the Sahel, we must exit the vicious cycle of violence to find sustainable solutions to provide security for both the population of the region and the foreigners who come to live or work there.
Ny zavatra mifanohitra amin'izay, raha maka ny toeran'i dokotera "Johny-hoavy-tsyhoela" i Frantsa, vao mainka hanasaro-javatra izany toy izay mijery hatrany ifotony ny olana misy. ||| Otherwise, when France plays the "Johny-come-lately" doctor, it will only make things worse instead of addressing the roots of the problem.
Nanamaloka ny fankalazana ny fetin'ny fahaleovantena Maliana ny fakàna ankeriny farany teo. ||| The latest kidnapping certainly tainted the Malian independence celebration.
i Bark Biiga dia manoratra ao amin'ny tsanganany fa: ||| Bark Biiga again writes in his column:
Tsy ny fahantrana lalina sy ny tsy fisian'ny rafi-pitantanana ara-panjakana any amin'ny faritra Sahel Maliana ve no mahatonga azy ho toeram-pamaharan'ny AQIM ao amin'ilay faritra? ||| Isn't it the immense poverty and the lack of administrative presence in the Malian Sahel that made the bed for AQIM in the region?
Tsy hoe fotsiny ho fanafahana ireo takalonaina fa koa mba hahazoana antoka fa i Mali, Niger, Maoritania, Alzeria na i Borkina Faso dia tsy ho paradisan'ny mpampihorohoro ary tsy hanohintohina ny fandrosoan'ny vahoaka Afrikana izay efa nandoa betsaka tamin'ny fanjanahantany, ny tsy fahaiza-mitantana, ary ny fihisatry ny fandrosoana. ||| It is not only about freeing the hostages but also to make sure that Mali, Niger, Mauritania, Algeria or Burkina Faso are not a haven for terrorists and do not compromise the development of African population that have already paid a heavy toll to colonisation, bad governance, and under-development
i Niger dia iray amin'ireo firenena mitàna ny lohany manerantany amin'ny famokarana uranium, nefa dia izy koa no manana ny tahan'ny harin-karena faobe farany ambany isam-batan'olona ao Afrika. ||| Niger is one of the world's leading uranium producer, yet it has one of the lowest average GDP per capita in Africa.
Ny fitsinjarana ny tombontsoa azo avy amin'ny fitrandrahana an'io loharanon-karena an-kibon'ny tany goavana io dia mbola tena olana isaky ny ambaratonga maro. ||| The sharing of revenues from the exploitation of this strategically important mining resource is problematic at many levels.
Ny fifandraisana manokana nisy teo amin'i Frantsa sy Niget tany aloha tany dia nitondra tamin'ny fanaovan'i Frantsa ampihimamba ny uranium amin'ny vidiny izay tena ambany dia ambany sy toa mananihany, vokatry ny fifanarahana manokana nosoniavina tamin'ny 1961. ||| The special relationship between France and Niger in the past led to exclusive access for France to the uranium at a ridiculously low cost, thanks to a special accord signed in 1961.
Ny fifanarahana iray nifanaovana tamin'ny Imounaren dia tsy nisy valaka tamin'ny taloha izay tsy nahazoan'ny fitondrana ao Niger afa-tsy ny 33% amin'ilay orinasa. ||| A contract with Imounaren was of the same vein that resulted in the state of Niger getting only 33% of the share of the company.
Na izany aza, ny vidiny ivarotana ny uranium dia mbola ambany noho izay hita eo amin'ny tontolon'ny tsenam-barotra iraisam-pirenena amin'izao fotoana. ||| Meanwhile, the selling price of uranium is still well below what is currently available on the global market.
Tsy ela akory izay dia nisy fihaonambe roa natao mba hitadiavana tetikady, ny iray dia fihaonamben'ny mpitantana ambony avy amin'ireo firenena any Sahel tamin'ny 26 Septambra. ||| Two meetings have been held recently to help develop a strategy, one was a meeting of the major Sahel states on September 26.
Io dia narahan'ny fihaonambe iray nahitàna irao lohandohan'ny sampam-pitsikilovana avy any Alzeria, Maoritania, Niger ary Mali tamin'ny 29 Septambra. ||| This was followed by a meeting of the heads of the intelligence agencies of Algeria, Mauritania, Niger and Mali on September 29.
Ny Vondrom-piarahamonina Eny Anivon'ny Aterineto Ao Costa Rica Dia Mirotsaka Hiady Amin'ny SOPA Sy Ny Sivana ||| Costa Rica's Online Community Joins Fight Against SOPA and Censorship
Taorian' ny fitokonana virtoaly niadiana tamin'ny Stop Online Piracy Act (SOPA) tany Etazonia fikatonan'ny Megaupload nanaraka izay, izay tranokala fizaràna failo, ny vondrom-piarahamonina eny anivon'ny aterineto ao Costa Rica dia tsy mijanona teny ivelan'ny sehatry ny ady amin'ny fanivànana ny aterineto intsony. ||| Following the virtual strike against the the United States' Stop Online Piracy Act (SOPA) and the subsequent shutdown of Megaupload, a file-sharing website, Costa Rica's online community is no longer staying out of the fight against Internet censorship.
Ny 17 Janoary dia, ilay fivondronanà bialogera ao Costa Rica TicoBlogger dia nanambara ny fanohanany ny ady tarihin'ny Wikipedia (izay "nanakatona" ny pejiny amin'ny fiteny anglisy nandritry ny 24 ora). ||| On January 17, Costa Rican blogger community TicoBlogger announced its support for the fight led by Wikipedia (which "turned off" its English page for 24 hours).
Satria izahay dia fitambaranà olona maro manana hevitra samihafa, kanefa mino marimarina izahay fa izahay isan'isany avy dia manana fahafahana hilaza ny heviny manokana, ary hanomboka mason'andro anio ka hatramin'ny fanatevananay laharana ny Wikipedia mba ho endriky ny ady amin'ny SOPA sy PIPA. ||| Because we are a united community of people who think differently, but we firmly believe in the right that each one of our members has of freely expressing him or herself, and starting from this day forward, we are joining Wikipedia to form a symbolic fight against SOPA and PIPA.
Ireo mpitsidika ny bilaogy samihafa ao amin'ny ticoblogger dia hahita ireo hafatra miady amin'ny Fanivànana Aterineto ary ireo votoaty voasakana amin'ny ampahany ao amin'ny pejy fandraisana. ||| Visitors to any blog on ticoblogger will find messages against Internet Censorship and partially blocked content on the homepage.
Ireo bilaogy isan-karazany ao anatin'ny tambajotra TicoBlogger no nanohana ny fihetsiketsehana, namerina nandefa indray ny fanambaràna, nanivana ny ampahany amin'ny lahatsorany na nampiditra ny heviny manokana mba hiadiana amin'ny SOPA, toy ny El Alumbrado Público, izay nambaran'ny mpanoratra azy fa: ||| Various blogs pertaining to the TicoBlogger network joined the protest, re-posting the statement, censoring parts of their posts or contributing their own reasons to fight against SOPA, like El Alumbrado Público, whose author asserts:
Izaho, amin'ny maha bilaogera ahy, dia tsy afaka ny hanohana lalàna izay mitetika ny tsy hahazoan'izao tontolo izao vaovao, fialamboly, ary manoatra noho izany rehetra izany, kolontsaina sy fahalalana. ||| As a blogger, I cannot be in favor of a law that looks to deprive the world of information, entertainment, and above all, of culture and knowledge.
Tamin'ny anarany manokana, i Julio Córdoba, mpanoratra ny Ciencia Ficción dia manambara fa: ||| On his own behalf, Julio Córdoba, author of Ciencia Ficción affirms:
Niha-nitombo ny aterineto noho ireo lehilahy sy vehivavy maro mizara ny heviny amin'ny fomba malalaka. ||| The Internet has grown because of men and women that freely share their ideas.
Ny fialambolim-pirenena sy iraisam-pirenena, ny fahalalana sy ny finamànana dia sasan-tsasany amin'ireo vokatra tsara indrindra nentin'ity fitaovana ity. ||| National and international recreation, knowledge and friendship are some of the greatest results of this tool.
Ireo izay manery ny zon'ny vahiny sy manome vahaolana tsy tonga lafatra ihany no mikiky manimba ny toe-panahin'ny aterineto. ||| Those who force alien rights and flawed solutions only undermine the very spirit of the web.
Ankehitriny, amin'ny maha mpikambana ao amin'ny ticoblogger ahy, ity bilaogy ity dia manatevin-daharana ny ady amin'ny SOPA. ||| Today, as a member of ticoblogger, this blog is joining the protest against SOPA.
Iray hafa amin'ireo bilaogin'ny fikambanana, Conejitos Suicidas, no nizara famintinana izay novolavolain'ny derechoaleer.org, izay manazava ny fomba mety hahazoan'ny SOPA mandona ireo mpampiasa azy, eny fa na dia any ivelan'i Etazonia aza. ||| Another of the collective's blogs, Conejitos Suicidas, shared an excerpt that derechoaleer.org elaborated upon, which explains how SOPA can affect users even outside of the United States.
Raha ny mikasika izany, dia mitanisa ireto manaraka ireto ry zareo: ||| With respect to this, they cite the following:
Raha tena hifehy marina ao amin'ny faritry ny tanin'i Etazonia tokoa ilay lalàna, amin'ny fanangonana ny ankamaroan'ny foto-drafitr'asan'ny aterineto amin'ny firenena, dia saika ny sampan-draharaha rehetra sy ny tranonkala izay ampiasantsika andavanandro no tena ho voakasika tanteraka: Youtube, Wikipedia, Google na Twitter, raha hanonona anarana vitsivitsy. ||| If the law will truly only govern on U.S. territory, upon concentrating the majority of this country's web infrastructure, almost all of the services and sites that we use daily will be affected: Youtube, Wikipedia, Google, or Twitter, to name a few.
Amin'ny lafiny iray, i Etazonia dia mampiantrano tolotra fototra eo amin'ny aterineto, toy ny fanaraha-maso ireo anaran-tsehatra (.com,.net,.org) izay, na any anatin'ny tranonkala ivelan'ny faritry ny taniny aza, aorian'ny fampiatoana ny fampiharana azy io any Etazonia, ary tsy ijerena ny rafitry ny lalàna misy ao amin'ilay firenena tratra izany, araka ny fanentanan'ny tsy mpankasitraka ny SOPA izay nalefany tao amin'ny tranonkala. ||| On the other hand, the United States houses basic web services, such as control over generic domains (.com,.net,.org) that, while belonging to websites outside its territory, after its application can be disabled from the United States, without considering the judicial system of the affected country, according to the "anti SOPA" campaign published on the website.
Ny vaovaon'ny fanakatonan'ny FBI ny Megaupload sy ny valin-kafatry ny Anonymous namely ny governemantan'i Etazonia (nanakatona ny tranonkalan'ny FBI, ankoatra ny hafa) ihany koa dia nanangana tabataba tao amin'ny tambajotra ara-tsosialy tany Costa Rica. ||| The news of the FBI's shutdown of Megaupload and Anonymous' counterattack against the U.S. government (closing the FBI website, among others) also generated commotion on social networks in Costa Rica.
Ary tamin'izany, ny mpampiasa Twitter dia nihetsika faran'izay haingana. ||| As such, Twitter users were swift to react.
Fihetsika ara-politikanà "ours" voro-damba ny an' ny FBI, fihantsiana ady mahatsiravina ny fanakatonana ny Megaupload nanaraka ny StopSopa. ||| The FBI has the political instinct of a teddy bear, to close Megaupload after StopSopa was a terrible provocation.
Ho valin'izany fepetra noraisina izany, ny mpanoratra ny El Alambrado Público dia namosaka ny heviny fa: ||| In response to this outlook, the author of El Alambrado Público expressed the opinion that:
Ampahany betsaka tamin'ny aterineto, izay fantatsika ankehitriny, no nanjavona. ||| A huge part of the Internet, as we know it today, has disappeared.
Bilaogy sy vovonana anarivony no tsy azo nampiasaina intsony. ||| Thousands of blogs and forums were left unusable.
Mila miainga hatrany amin'ny voalohany mihitsy isika, inona no mba tavela? ||| We have to start from zero, what else is left?
Tianao ho fantatra ve ny hevitro raha ny mitovy amin'izany no hitranga any Taringa? ||| Would you understand my point if the same thing happened to Taringa?
Ny votoaty amin'ny fialamboly no ampahany kely tamin'ny hadisoana goavana nataon'ny Departemantan'ny fitsarana ao Etazonia. ||| Entertainment content is a small part of the huge mistake that the U.S. Department of Justice has committed.
Izany anefa tsy fijerena manokana ny fampandehanana tsara ny ara-toe-karena ao Hollywood na ny Universal Music; Fa kosa momba ny fanomezana antoka sy ny fanamoràna ny fahazoana fahalalàna, kolontsaina, ary vaovao ho an'izao tontolo izao. ||| It's not about watching over the economic well being of Hollywood or Universal Music; it's about guaranteeing and facilitating access to knowledge, culture, and information to the world.
Tari-dàlana maimaim-poana amplony maro, fanadihadiana nozaraina maimaim-poana, sary marobe, antontan-taratasy mikasika ny ara-kolontsaina sy ara-tantara no nanjavona tsy hita popoaka. ||| Dozens of free tutorials, freely distributed documentaries, photos, cultural and historical documents have disappeared.

Malaoi: Fantaro Ny Mpanoratra Eto Amin'ny Global Voices, Victor Kaonga ||| Malawi: Meet Global Voices Author Victor Kaonga

mpilaza vaovao Malaoita, mpitoraka bilaogy sy mpanoratra ao amin'ny Global Voices Victor Kaonga ||| Malawian broadcast journalist, blogger and Global Voices author Victor Kaonga
Eremipagamo Amabebe: Ahoana no nahatonga anao tafiditra ao amin'ny Global Voices? ||| Eremipagamo Amabebe: How did you become involved in Global Voices?
Victor Kaonga: Toa hoe nanaraka ny lahatsoratra tamin'ny bilaogiko nandritra ny roa herinandro tamin'ny taona 2006 hatramin'ny voalohandohan'ny taona 2007 ny Mpamoaka lahatsoratra aty amin'ny faritra ao amin'ny GV, Ndesanjo Macha. ||| Victor Kaonga: It appears GV Regional Editor Ndesanjo Macha had been following my blog posts for a couple of weeks in 2006 to early 2007.
Izy no nandefa mailaka tamiko nanontany ahy raha mahaliana ahy ny ho lasa mpanoratra ao amin'ny GV. ||| He is the one who sent me an email asking if I would be interested in being a GV author.

Satria nonina tany Soedy aho tamin'izany fotoana izany, dia nanontany ny namako mpanao gazety Soedoa izay toa efa naheno mikasika ny GV. ||| As I was living in Sweden at that time, I asked one of my Swedish journalism friends who apparently had heard about GV.
Nandrisika ahy ny hirosoko izy ary hanomboka handrakotra am-bilaogy mikasika an'i Malaoi sy Zambia. ||| He encouraged me to take it up and start covering blogs for Malawi and Zambia.
Dia nirotsaka tamin'ny Global Voices aho tamin'ny Desambra 2006 ary tamin'ny 23 janoary 2007 no nivoaka ny lahatsoratro voalohany. ||| So I joined Global Voices in December 2006 and my first post published was on 23rd January 2007.
Toy ny ahoana ny fiainanao ivelan'ny Global Voices? ||| What is your life like outside Global Voices?
Manana ny ankohonako aho, i Thembi no vadiko. ||| I have a family, married to Thembi.
Efatra ny zanakay, telovavy ary lahy iray eo amin'ny 9 hatramin'ny 1.5 taona. ||| We have four children, three girls and a boy ages between 9 and 1.5 years.
Amin'ny maha fianakaviana, dia matahotra an'Andriamanitra izahay ary izany dia saika noho ny fitaizana anay tamin'ny fomba kristiana fa ny tena zava-dehibe dia ny fanapahan-kevitray hanaraka an'i Kristy. ||| As a family we desire to fear God and that comes partly from our Christian upbringing but most importantly from individual decisions to follow Christ.
Ankoatry ny fitiavako mandany andro miaraka amin'ny fianakaviako (zavatra izay nanjary niha nahàlana tsikelikely), dia lany amin'ny asa hafa tsy maintsy atao ao amin'ny Onjam-peo Trans World ny tenako izay mitovy amin'ny tranoko faharoa raha atao amin'ny teny feno fanajana! ||| Apart from liking to spend time with my family (something that is becoming increasingly scarce), I am busy with executive oversight work at Trans World Radio which in some respects is like my second home!
Na izany aza, tsindriako ihany fa amin'ny asa dia mpanao gazety mpilaza vaovao kokoa aho noho ny hoe mpiasa tsotra mpanatanteraka!. ||| However, I should state that by function I am more of a broadcast journalist than an executive officer!
Azonao ampahafantarina ve ny tena ifantohanao ao amin'ny Global Voices –ho an'ireo izay tsy tena mahalala ny asanao?. ||| Can you describe your focus at Global Voices –for those who aren't familiar with your work?
Miresaka ny zavatra rehetra izay tena ilaina aho raha toa ka mahakasika an'i Malaoi. ||| I cover anything that is newsworthy as far as Malawi is concerned.
Na izany aza, raha ivelan'ny fijerena an'i Malaoi, dia manana jery todika amin'ny haino aman-jery sosialy sy vaovao foana ny tenako amin'ny ankapobeny. ||| However outside the Malawi focus, I generally have a bias towards new and social media.
Inona no olana tena miavaka amin'ny faritra misy anao, izay raha ny hevitrao no anontaniana, dia tokony mbola resahana misimisy kokoa ao amin'ny haino aman-jery fototra?... ||| What are issues specific to your region that, in your opinion, should have more coverage in the mainstream media?
Ny tena olana amin'ny ankapobeny dia ny fampandrosoana ara-toe-karena sy ara-politika. ||| The main issues in Malawi are political and economic development.
Eny rehetra eny isika manana ny tantara ara-java-kanto sy hevitra mikasika ny fiainan'olombelona. ||| Here and there we have had some artistic and human interest stories.
Ny tena olana amin'izao fotoana izao dia mikasika ny toe-karena sy ny fandaharana ho amin'ny handimby ny filoha ankehitriny. ||| Main issues currently have to with the economy and succession plan of the incumbent president.
Raha ara-toekarena, niaina ny tsy fisiana vola vahiny nandritra ny herintaona mahery i Malaoi izay niafara tamin'ny isan'ny fandraharahana maro. ||| Economically, Malawi has experienced shortage of forex for more than a year which has resulted into a number of consequences for businesses.
Mifandray amin'ity tsy fisian'ny solika ity ihany koa noho ny famatsiana mitsitaitaika nateraky ny tsy fahampian'ny tahirim-bola vahiny teo amin'ny firenena. ||| Also linked to this is the shortage of fuel due to erratic supplies resulting into low forex reserves in the country.
ka dia voatery milahatra solika indray ny vahoaka amin'izao fotoana noho ny tsy fahampian'ny fanafarana.. ||| As such people have been queuing for fuel now and again as supplies are erratic.
Raha eo amin'ny lafiny ara-politika, manomana ny rahalahiny ny filoha Bingu wa Mutharika mba hisolo azy amin'ny 2014 rehefa voararan'ny lalampanorenana tsy hifaninana izy tenany. ||| Politically, President Bingu wa Mutharika is grooming his brother to take over in 2014 when he himself will be barred by the constitution to contest.
Maro ny Malaoita no nanantena fa hanohana ny filoha lefitra (Joyce Banda) izy izay toa vehivavy voalohany Veep tany Malaoi. ||| Many Malawians had hoped that he would support his vice president (Joyce Banda) who happens to be the first female Veep in Malawi.
Indrisy anefa, niova ny làlan'izy ireo ka dia afaka niditra mora foana ny rahalahiny. ||| Unfortunately, they have parted ways so that his brother can easily come in.
Afaka lazainao anay ve ny lahatsoratra tena tianao amin'ireo nosaratanao ho an'ny GV? ||| Can you point us to some of your favorite posts you've written for GV?
Misy lahatsoratra roa izay tena ireharehako manokana. ||| There are a couple of posts that I am really proud of.
Saika misy ifandraisany amin'ny politika sy karazana fifandirana ny ankamaroan'izy ireo. ||| Most of them have been political and sort of conflict-related.
Fa ny tena nanaitra ahy ary nahafaly ahy (tanatin'ny maro) dia nahitàna ny lahatsoratra farany mikasika ny fahalalahana akademika nataoko tamin'ny volana Aprily tamin'ity taona ity, ary indrindra ny fodiamandrin'ny Vadin'ny filoham-pirenena Malaoi tamin'ny taona 2007. ||| Though surprisingly the ones I felt most happy with (among many) include the last post about academic freedom I did in April this year, and then when Malawi's First Lady passed away in 2007.
Ity no vaovao nanintona ny sain'ireo mpitoraka bilaogy maneran-tany. ||| This was news that attracted attention of bloggers all over the world.
Manana endrika ahitana ny fiainan'ny olombelona ireo lahatsoratra roa ireo sy ny hafa maro ihany koa noho izy ireo mikasika ny olona fanta-daza ary resaka olana avy amin'ny politika. ||| The two posts and many other have a human interest aspect much as they are about prominent people and issues that stem from politics.
Inona no tena isan'ny mahaliana amin'ny asanao? ||| What is the most interesting part of your work?
Tena hitako hoe tena mahaliana sy mampahiratra ny mamaky ny lahatsoratry ny olona. ||| I find reading people's posts extremely interesting and enlightening.
Tena mahazo hery hoe misy Malaoita mizara ny heviny sy miresaka amin'ny aterineto. ||| I get encouraged that there are Malawians who are sharing thoughts and conversations online.
Fitahiana sahady ny hoe misy olona iray izay manoratra zavatra amin'ny aterineto satria amin'ny ankapobeny dia kely zavatra hita amin'ny aterineto mikasika an'i Malaoi indrindra fa hoe avy amin'ny Malaoita ihany. ||| The fact that someone has written something online is itself a blessing because generally there is very little content online about Malawi especially by Malawians themselves.
Ny tena manahirana ahy dia ny momba ireo vehivavy mpitoraka bilaogy. ||| My biggest concern though is about female bloggers.
Tsy manana maro izahay ary irariako ny hànana maro. ||| We don't have many and I wish we had many.
Ny vitsy izay mitoraka bilaogy indray aza zara raha mahita resahina eo amin'ny GV ary na izy ireo aza dia milaza fa amporisihina mihitsy hanohy. ||| The few that blog have had fairly a good amount of coverage on GV and they themselves have confessed recieving a lot of encouragement to carry on.
Ny tenako manokana aloha dia maniry ny hahita vehivavy maro mitoraka bilaogy. ||| I personally wish to see more women blog.
EA: Mankasitraka, Victor. ||| EA: Thanks, Victor.
Alohan'ny handehananay, afaka manome anay loharano azo jerena momba an'i Malaoi ve ianao ho an'ireo izay te-hahalala bebe kokoa? ||| Before we leave you, can you point us toward some resources on Malawi for those who want to learn more?
Iray amin'ny vavahady malaza ny www.nyasatimes.com. ||| One of the popular portals in www.nyasatimes.com.
Mitondra aminà tantara maro mikasika ny politika sy ny mikasika ny Filoha lefitra miaraka amin'ny olan'ny fifandimbiasana koa aza ilay vavahady. ||| The portal carries many stories on politics and even the one about the Vice President and the succession woes.
Ary mitondra fanavaozam-baovao ho anareo koa ity bilaogy ity. ||| And this blog gives you updates.
Raha te hahare bebe kokoa avy amin'i Victor, tsindrio eto raha hamaky ny mombamomba azy ao amin'ny "Mpitoraka bilaogin'ny herinandro" tamin'ny 2007. ||| If you'd like to hear more from Victor, click here to read his "Blogger of the Week" profile from 2007.
Azia Atsimo: Isan'Andro Ny Antsika Misy Ora Irain'Ny Tany ||| South Asia: Every Day Is Earth Hour for Us
Hetsika fanentanana manerantany ny Earth Hour izay karakarain'ny World Wide Fund for Nature ary isaky ny Asabotsy faran'ny volana Martsa isan-taona no fankalazana izany. ||| Earth Hour is a worldwide awareness event organized by the World Wide Fund for Nature and it is held on the last Saturday of March annually.
Tamin'ity andro ity, niangaviana ireo tokantrano sy orinasa mba hamono ireo jiro izay tsy ilaina mandritra ny adiny iray mba hanaovana fanairana momba ny fiovaovan'ny toetr'andro. ||| On this day households and businesses are requested to turn off their non-essential lights for one hour to raise awareness about climate change.
Tanàna sy tanàn-dehibe maherin'ny 5200 manerana ny firenena 135 no namono ny jirony ho amin'ny Ora Irain'ny Tany 2011 ary tamin'ity taona ity, tanàna maro tahaka an'i Dhaka, Bangladesh no nandray anjara ihany koa. ||| More than 5,200 cities and towns in 135 countries worldwide switched off their lights for Earth Hour 2011 and this year many more cities like Dhaka, Bangladesh, will be joining.
Faritra ahitana firenena marobe mandroso ary mangetaheta angovo (herinaratra) i Azia Atsimo. ||| South Asia is a region with many developing countries hungry for power.
Olona an-tapitrasany ao India no tsy manana herinaratra, ary hanjakan'ny kolikoly sy ny tsy fahombiazana ny sehatry ny angovo. ||| Millions of people in the Indian sub-continent have no access to electricity, and the power sector is plagued by corruption and inefficiency.
Betsaka kokoa ny fangatahana amin'izany noho ny tolotra ka maro ireo firenena miaritra ny delestazy (delestazy fantatra mialoha) mba handaminana ny fitsinjarana ny herinatra. ||| The demand is much bigger than supply so many countries use load shedding (planned rolling blackouts) to manage the electricity distribution.
Ao amin'ny firenena tahaka an'i Nepal, Pakistan ary Bangladesh, misy delestazy eo amin'ny 4-12 ora isan'andro eo, izay miovaova araka ny zava-misy andavanandro. ||| In countries like Nepal, Pakistan and Bangladesh daily there are 4-12 hours of load shedding varying on the situation everyday.
Manana ny holazainy ny mpiserasera mikasika ny fijeriny ny "ora irain'ny tany" ao amin'ny fampahalalam-baovao sosialy. ||| Netizens are vocal on the issue of observing earth hour in the social media.
Raha mangataka famatsiana herinaratra ny sasany, ny hafa kosa manome lanjany ny Ora irain'ny Tany, ny sasany indray mihevitra fa vazivazy fotsiny ihany izany. ||| While some are requesting others to observe Earth Hour, some are thinking that this is not more than a joke.
Ireto tweet manaraka avy amin'ny faritra ireto no mampiseho ny hevitry ny tsirairay. ||| The following tweets from the region reflect what they have in mind.
(vaovao malaza isan'andro) vao voalohany no hanome lanjany ny Ora irain'ny Tany i Bangladesh androany alina ..." Nanao izany hatrany izahay talohan'ny nanomezana anarana azy noforonina toy izao. ||| "Bangladesh for the first time tonight will observe Earth Hour" ... We were doing that long before it had such a fancy name.
Tsy mahagaga Bangladesh no anisan'ny firenena iray mpandala ny tontolo iainana manerantany. ||| No wonder Bangladesh is one of the most environment conscious countries in the world.
Mankalaza ny Ora irain'ny Tany izahay isan'andro, in-12! ||| We celebrate Earth Hour every day, 12 times!
Androany, hankalaza ny Ora irain'ny Tany 2012 ny Power Development Board (PDB) amin'ny alalan'ny fanomezana delestazy 12 ora ao Bangladesh. ||| Today Power Development Board (PDB) is going to celebrate Earth Hour 2012 by giving 12 hours of load shedding of electricity in Bangladesh.
Ora Irain'ny Tany tao Dimapur, Firenena Avaratra-Atsinanana ao Inde. ||| A view of an Earth Hour in Dimapur, Northeastern State of India.
Nampiato ny famatsiana herinaratra ny Sampandraharaha momba ny angovo ao Nagaland ho fankalazana ny Ora iray ny Tany. ||| Power Department of Nagaland, shut down power supplies to celebrate Earth Hour.
Sangy mihoatra ny loha ny Ora Irain'ny Tany ao India. ||| Earth Hour in India is a cruel joke.
mankalaza ny ora irain'ny tany ireo 72% tsy manana herinaratra ao India. ||| 72% of India with no power connection celebrate earth hour.
Ny 1% ambiny ihany no mamono ny jirony, sy ny fifandraisana aman'olona ary ny hafatra fiarahabana ||| 1% from the rest switch off their lights, and issue PR and congratulatory msgs
Ao India, izay misy ahy indrindra, ora irain'ny tany foana no iainanay isan'andro. ||| In india especially where I am we have earth hour everyday.
Ka ho anareo olona rehetra mamono ny jirony mandritra ny adiny iray, fanaontsika isan'andro izany. ||| So all you people who are switching their light off an hour we do it everyday.
Tsy tokony hanahy ny amin'ny ora irain'ny tany ny olona manerantany, heverin'i India avokoa ny zava-drehetra!! ||| People of the world should not worry about the earth hour, India has got it all covered!!
Vonoy ny jironao azafady ho fankalazana ny Ora Irain'ny Tany!! ||| Please Switch off your lights for the Earth Hour!!
Olona mankalaza ny fandaharan'asa mikasika ny 60+Earth Hour ao Kathmandu, Nepal. ||| People participate in a programme on 60+Earth Hour in Kathmandu, Nepal.
Tokony hanome lanjany ny Ora Irain'ny Tany koa ve i Pakistan? ||| Is Pakistan also supposed to observe Earth Hour?
Efa mankalaza ny Ora Irain'ny Tany izahay farafahakeliny 6-8 ora isan'andro. ||| We already observe Earth Hour at least 6-8 hours a day everyday.
Olana lehibe ny Ora Irain'ny tany ka tsy misy na iray aza tokony hanohitra izany. ||| Earth Hour is a serious issue and one must not write against it.
Olana lehibe indrindra noho ny delestazy izay iainantsika isan'andro manerana ny faritra rehetra ao amin'ny firenena ve ny Ora Irain'ny tany? ||| Is it a bigger issue than load-shedding that we experience daily in all parts of the country?
Olana lehibe noho ny fahaverezana an-tapitrasany mahazo antsika noho ny tsy fisian'ny herinaratra eo amin'ny indostria? ||| Is it a bigger problem than the losses in millions we attain due to the absence of electricity to the industries?
Olana lehibe noho ny tsy famatsiana herinaratra eny amin'ny hopitaly ao an-toerana izay misy marary atao fandidiana amin'ny alalan'ny gropy (mpiteraka angovonaratra) satria tsy misy ny herinaratra? ||| Is it more serious an issue than the non-availability of electricity in a local hospital where patients are operated upon under standby generators because the electricity doesn't show up?
Tsy mino aho fa lehibe indrindra noho ireo tranga-javatra tsy tambo isaina ireo ny ora irain'ny tany, satria tsy ho antsika vahoaka miaina ety amin'ny firenena andalam-pandrosoana izany. ||| I don't think it is more serious than countless scenarios like these, because it is not for us, people living in third world countries.
Ho an'ny mpiserasera twitter 40 000 sy ireo mpikaroka vaovao avy amin'ny loharanom-baovao misy eo an-toerana izay tsy mitsaha-mitombo dia i Andy Carvin no fijanonana voalohany ao amin'ny twitter raha hijery vaovao manerana ny ilany andrefana sy avaratry Afrika. ||| With 40,000 Twitter followers and a dedicated stream of local sources, Andy Carvin has become a first stop on Twitter for news throughout the Middle East and North Africa.
Manam-pahaizana manokana momba ny tetik'ady ao ami'nny NPR, nanakaiky hatrany ny media sosialy i Carvin - tsindriana manokana amin'izany ny twitter - satria io no tahaka ny filazam-baovao manara-potoana. ||| An NPR strategist, Carvin has approached social media–and Twitter in particular–as a platform for real-time reporting.
Niasa efa hatramin'ny ela ho an'ny Global Voices i Carvin, noho izany tsy manavao azy ny asa ataontsika, sady efa fantany hatramin'ny ela ny lanjan'ny asa fanaovan-gazety. ||| An early contributor to Global Voices, Carvin is no stranger to the work that we do, and has long seen the value of citizen journalism.
Tamin'ny volana febroary nandritra ny resadresaka nifanaovana tamin'i Ethan Zuckerman, notsindriany tamin'izany ny maha-zava-dehibe ny "fitondrana olona any an-toerana hitantara ny zava-nisy tahaka ny hoe nanatri-maso teo ry zareo." ||| In a February an interview with Ethan Zuckerman, he emphasized the importance of "getting actual people on the ground telling their story as they participate in the event".
Fanontaniana napetraky ny ekipan'ny Global Voices avy any andrefana sy avaratry Afrika no hita ao amin'ity resadresaka ity. ||| This interview is comprised of questions contributed by members of Global Voices' Middle East and North Africa team.
Inona no fitaovana ampiasainao rehefa hiserasera twitter, ary inona no tsapanao fa banga amin'izany fitaovana izany? ||| What tools do you use to mine Twitter, and what do you feel is missing from the tool arsenal?
Amin'izao fotoana izao dia ireo fitaovana ankapobeny rehetra no ampiasaiko - tweetdeck, fanaovana fikarohana amin'ny twitter, sy ny sisa. ||| Right now I'm using pretty standard stuff – Tweetdeck, Twitter Search, etc.
Rehefa fantatro ny hoe iza no hotadiaviko sy ny hoe mifandraika amin'ny inona dia tsy misy dikany loatra ny fitaovana ampiasaina fa ampy izany rehefa ahazoako mandamina ny fampiasako twitter. ||| As long as I have a sense of who I'm looking for and in what context, the tools themselves generally don't matter as long as they allow me to organize my Twitter monitoring.
Misy fitaovana mba tiako ananana ihany anefa, tahaka ny hoe ireo izay afaka manampy ahy hitantanako ny fahabetsahan'ny mamaly ahy, izay matetika sarotra amiko ny mamantatra ny olona te hiresaka amiko fotsiny sy ny olona manome fijery vaovao ho ahy. ||| Having said that, there are some tools I'd like to get my hands on, like ones that can help me manage my ever-increasing flow of replies to me, which sometimes make it hard to separate people who just want to chat with me from those who have news tips.
Efa manomboka mahazatra ankehitriny ny media sosialy eo amin'ny tontolon'ny media; mahita fiovana hatrany amin'ny fotony ve ianao amin'ny fomba famoahana vaovao, indrindra ny vaovao maneran-tany? ||| Social media coverage is becoming increasingly common across media; do you see a fundamental shift happening in the way news is covered, particularly internationally?
Ataoko fa mamirapiratra tokoa ny lohatenim-baovao any amin'ny media sosialy raha ny iraisam-pirenena no jerena, satria na dia ireo media matanjaka indrindra aza tsy manana olona afaka miparitaka etsy sy eroa amin'ny fotoana iray. ||| I think social media as part of news coverage really shines when it comes to international coverage, basically because even the largest news orgs can't have people in every place at once.
taorian'ilay tsunami vita noely, tsy nahazoana vaovao tanteraka amin'ny fotoana rehetra ny toerana sasany tahaka an'i Maldives sy ny nosy Andaman, noho izany dia tena nilaina ny fanangonam-baovao tany amin'ny olona nahalalana ny tena zava-nisy marina. ||| After the Boxing Day tsunami, news wires didn't necessarily have full-time staff in place like the Maldives or the Andaman Islands, so getting information from citizen journalists was vital to cover the story.
miaraka amin'ny twitter sy ny tranonkala tahaka ny YouTube ohatra, dia tena azo antoka tsara ny mahazo endrika hafa amin'ny vaovao rehetra miseho manerana ny tany rehetra iay afaka mahita aterineto. ||| With the advent of Twitter and content sharing sites like YouTube, it's possible to get a peek into any news story around the world where there happens to be Internet access.
Ary raha mila fanampiana ianao, tsy takatry ny sainao ny isan'ny olona avy amin'ireny toerana ireny te hanampy anao amin'ny fanaparitahana vaovao. ||| And if you ask for help, you'd be amazed by how many people in these places are willing to assist you in your reporting.
Hitanay fa nanadihady momba ny fihetseham-bahoaka ianao tany Tonizia, Ejipta, Libia, Baraina, ary izao koa i Siria. ||| We've watched you report on the uprisings in Tunisia, Egypt, Libya, Bahrain, and now Syria.
Matetika ianao no mizara sary sy lahatsary avy any an-toerana. ||| You often share graphic images and videos from the ground.
Tsy mahatsiaro tena ho leo sy reraka ve ianao amin'ny famoahana vaovao mandratra fo tahaka ireny? ||| Do you ever feel overwhelmed or exhausted by covering such often heartbreaking events?
Mazava ho azy, tena sarotra be indraindray, indrindra rehefa misy lahatsary na tantara mikasika ankizy maratra. ||| Sure, it can be really tough sometimes, especially when there are videos or stories about children getting hurt.
Manan-janaka kely anankiroa aho ka rehefa mahita ankizy mitovy taona aminy tafahitsoka ao afovoan'ny afo toy ireny aho dia tena mandratra ahy tokoa. ||| I've got two very young kids and when I see kids of a similar age caught in the crossfire, it really shakes me up.
Tahaka izany ihany, raha vao mahita olona mpiserasera twitter misy manafika ianao, dia tena koditra mihitsy, satria tsy maintsy manao sary an-tsaina ny zava-niseho ianao, ary matetika ohatry ny tena mafy kokoa noho ny tena zava-nisy ny ao an-dohanao ao. ||| Also when you see people on twitter live-tweeting being attacked, it can really rattle you, because you have to create a picture in your head of what's going on, and that's sometimes even more vivid than the reality of it.
Kanefa efa fantatro izao hoe rehefa inona aho no afaka manalavitra ny solosainako sy ny iPhone-ko. ||| But I've made a point of knowing when to step away from my laptop or iPhone.
Ny zavatra tiako atao farany izao dia ny mandoro azy avy eo miala amin'izay kanefa mbola tsy ho ato ho ato aloha izany. ||| The last thing I want to do is burn out and give up, but I don't see that happening any time soon.
Hitanay fa tsy mijanona manana finiavana handray andraikitra hatrany ianao amin'izay zavatra rehetra ataonao - avy aiza no nahatonga izany? ||| We assume you keep going out out of a strong sense of responsibility to keep on doing what you're doing — where did that come from?
Vokatry ny fanaovanao ity asa ity ve sa ny mifamadika amin'izay? ||| Is it as a result of doing this job, or the other way around?
Sarotra ny tena mamantatra izany. ||| It's hard to pin down precisely.
Anisan'ireny angamba ny hoe adalam-baovao aho, ary tena manaraka akaiky ny zava-misy eto amin'ny faritra aho satria ohatry ny hoe izay no antom-pisiana. ||| Part of it is simply that I'm a news junkie, and I'd be closely following events in the region because it's of such global significance.
Fa efa niasa antserasera foana koa aho nandritra ny taona maro rehefa misy loza voa-janahary, anisan'izany ny 9/11, ny rivo-doza Katrina, ny horohorontany tany Haiti. ||| But I also have worked a lot in online disaster response over the years, including 9/11, Hurricane Katrina and the Haiti earthquake.
Noho izany dia fantatro fa manana filana goavana aho hiaina rehefa misy zavatra mitovy amin'ireny. ||| So I'm sure I have a strong inner need to bear witness in situations like this.
Tany Ejipta sy Baraina, moramora kokoa no nahazoana mpiserasera twitter. ||| In Egypt and Bahrain, it was relatively easy to find and vet Twitter users.
Any Libia sy Yemen kosa, ohatra, dia somary sarotra. ||| In Libya and Yemen, for example, it's much more difficult.
Ahoana no fomba ataonao hifaneraserana amin'ny media sosialy any amin'ny firenena tsy dia marisika loatra mampiasa azy ireny? ||| How do you manage to locate social media content from less active countries?
Tsy misy olom-pantatro manokana any amin'ireny firenena ireny, noho izany dia miezaka aho hanana fifandraisana an-tserasera amin'ny terantany monina any Etazonia amin'ny alalan'ny herin'ny tanako manokana. ||| I didn't know anyone personally in either countries, so I started by trying to find connections to expat communities in the US through my own personal networks.
Vetivety ihany aho dia mahita olona miresaka amiko ary manome ny hevitr'izy ireo ny amin'izay olona mpiserasera isaky ny firenena. ||| Soon enough I found people who were willing to talk with me and give me their impression of who the leading online players were in each country.
Raha eo amin'ny lafiny fikarohana momba ny lohahevitra indray dia mora tsy araka ny eritreretanareo azy. ||| As for finding content, it's easier than you'd think.
Fitaovana tena ahitanao sary sy sary miaina betsaka indrindra ny facebook, tahaka ny YouTube ihany, mila mahafantatra fotsiny ianao hoe aiza no tokony ahitana azy. ||| Facebook has been a goldmine for photos and videos, as has YouTube. You just need to know where to look for them.

mampitaha ny vokatry ny fandatsahan-dranomaso amin'ny sarimihetsika amin'ny fandevenana any ambanivohitr'i Sina: ||| compares the tear shedding effect of the movie with the funeral ceremony in rural China:
Tamin'ny farany dia ritra ny ranomason'ireo olona ary afaka nampiseho ny fankasitrahany ireo havana, namana, mpiray tanàna sy ireo pretra, etc miaraka amin'ny fiaraha-misakafo ny fianakaviana. ||| Eventually everyone were exhausted from crying and the family would express thanks to relatives, friends, neighbors and monks, etc with huge banquet.
Nahatratra ny famaranana azy izany fandevenana izany ary samy niverina ny ain'ireo olona ireo tamin'io fandevenana nampitomany io... ||| The ceremony reached its climax and people recovered their spirit from the crying funeral...
Ny fomban'ny fandevenana dia mety hamadika ny fahoriana ho fifaliana, fandevenana ho lanonana. ||| The funeral custom can transform sadness into happiness, funeral into ceremony.
Ny fahafatesan'olona iray dia lasa fifaliana lehibe. ||| Someone's death becomes a great happiness.
Nanana ny fahafahana nijery ny sarimihetsik'i Feng vaovao "Tang Shan Earthquake" aho vao haingana izay. ||| I had the opportunity to view Feng's new movie "Tang Shan Earthquake" recently.
Ilay fijerena sarimihetsika dia rakotry ny feon'ireo olona mitomany... Ny tantaran'i Feng dia nampahatsiaro ahy ny fandevenana tany ambanivohitr'i Jiangxu, "catharsis" izay namadika ny fahavoazana ho fahafaliana, fandevenana ho lanonana... ||| The dark cinema was filled with people's sobbing sound... Feng's story reminded me of the funeral in rural Jiangxu, a catharsis that transforms tragedy into happiness, funeral into ceremony...
Ny Granite Studio nitanisa ireo tsikeran'i James Palmer izay nilaza fa tena tsy mifanaraka amin'ny fandehan'ny tantara iny sarimihetsika iny: ||| Granite Studio quoted James Palmer's comments who pointed out that the movie is very ahistorical:
Amin'ny maha mpahay tantaran'ny horohorontanin'i Tangshan ahy, toa diso fanantenana kely aho; lasa tahaka ny mijery Titanic izany ary mijery ny sambo rendrika ao anatin'ny atsasak'adiny. ||| As a historian of the Tangshan Earthquake, I was a little disappointed; it was like going to see Titanic and watching the boat sink in the first half hour.
Mety noho ny fanakaikezana azy amin'ny tsy fifanarahany amin'ny tantara, azo heverina ihany koa ho fanoharana ara-politika eo amin'ny fianakaviana sy ny firenena iny. ||| It is probably through the ahistorical approach, a political allegory between family and nation is made possible.
Ao amin'ny Aftershock, any amin'ny lafin'ny "bitika "ny fianakaviana ny fianakaviana, ary any amin'ny lafin'ny "lehibe" kosa ny Firenena! ||| In the Aftershock, on the micro level it is the family, on the marco level it is the State!
Ny Tale Feng dia mivoatra, sarimihetsika mikasika ny politika io ary mijery ny fivoaran'ny firenena. ||| Director Feng is making progress, it is a politically charged movie with a vision on the nation's progress.
Tamin'ny voalohandohan'ity taona ity, nisy fanadihadihana mikasika ny horohorontanin'i Tang Shan, Buried, nibata ny fandresena tamin'ny fankalazana ny horonantsary fanadihadihana Sinoa. ||| Earlier this year, a documentary on Tang Shan earthquake, Buried, has won the Chinese documentary film festival.
Ny fangatahan'ny Tale Wang Libo fa "tsy mety may ny marina" dia notononina imbetsaka ary nivadika ho fanamarihana ratsy amin'ny Aftershock-n'i Feng. ||| The director Wang Libo's claim that "truth cannot be buried" has been quoted widely online and turned into a critical footnote of Feng's Aftershock.

Ejipta: Tokony Hisarom-boaly Koa Ny Lehilahy! ||| Egypt: Men Should Wear the Veil!
Ity dia ampahany amin'ny tatitray manokana momba ny Revolisiona ao Ejipta 2011. ||| This post is part of our special coverage Egypt Revolution 2011.
Niaraka tamin'ny fitroaran'ireo Islamista talohan'ny revolisiona, nitombo ny tahotra ny hisian'ny faneriterena ara-pinoana teny anivon'ny tanora, ireo vitsy an'isa ary ny vehivavy. ||| With Islamists rising in post-revolution Egypt, fear of religious oppression is growing among youth, minorities, and women.
Tsy ela akory, vondrom-behivavy Ejiptiana iray no nanangana pejy Facebook amin'ny teny Arabo, antsoina hoe "Mampanako ny Hiaka" manondro ny fanavahana ny lahy sy ny vavy eo amin'ny fiarahamonin-dry zareo sy ny teritery mety ho avy miaraka amin'ny fahatongavan'ny Islamista eo amin'ny fitondràna. ||| Recently, a group of Egyptian women started a Facebook page in Arabic called "Echoing Screams" pointing out sexism in their society and the oppression that might be coming with the expected arrival of Islamists in power.
Ilay vondrona dia nanangana ihany koa hetsika iray "Fitondrana Hijab ho fanehoana firaisankina amin'ny vehivavy" izay voasoritra araka izao manaraka izao: ||| The group has also started an event "Wearing Hijab in solidarity with women" that had the following description:
Lazain-dry zareo fa ny voaly (Hijab) dia fahafahan'ny tena manokana fa tsy endri-panandevozana ny vehivavy, izay heverin-dry zareo ho toy ny fitaovana fakàn-taranaka fotsiny, toy ny entam-barotra, Awrah iray, nefa ry zareo ihany dia efa mampiasa ny hijab ho toy ny mari-pamantarana ny tsy fanajàna rehefa milaza "ireo lehilahy mitafy hijabs" ho toy ny manompa ny toerana misy an-dry zareo lehilahy. ||| They say the veil (Hijab) is a personal freedom and not a sign of enslaving women whom they look at as a sex object, a commodity, an Awrah, yet they use Hijab as a reference of disrespect when saying "men who wear hijabs" as to insult their manhood.
Amin'izany, ireo izay miantso ny vehivavy hitafy hijab dia tsy tokony hanenjika ny lehilahy raha toa izy ireny misafidy ny hitafy hijab. ||| Thus, those who call on women to wear Hijab should not attack men if they chose to wear Hijab.
Ilay vondrona dia nampakatra sarin- dehilahy maro mitafy Hijab ao amin'ny pejin'ilay hetsika, ny iray amin'ireny dia nalaina avy amin'ny fanentanana izay natomboky ny Iraniana tao anaty aterineto roa taona lasa izay ho fanohanana lehilahy iray mpianatra izay nosamborina noho izy nitafy toy ny vehivavy mba handosirana an'i Teheran, araka ny filazan'ireo manampahefana. ||| The group posted several pictures of men wearing Hijab in the event page, one of which was taken from the campaign that Iranians launched online two years ago in support of a male student who was arrested for dressing up as a woman to escape Tehran, as authorities claimed.
Nandray anjara tamin'ity hetsika ity ihany koa ireo Toniziana mpampiasa aterineto ary nitondra fanehoan-kevitra niharo hehy tao amin'ny rindrin'ilay hetsika, namela fanehoan-kevitra manadrohadro manohitra ny antoko Ennahda, izay nandrombaka ny ankabeazan'ireo fifidianana Toniziana tamin'ny volana lasa iny, ary i Rached Ghannouchi no lohany. ||| Tunisian netizens have also taken part in this event and have commented with laughter on the event's wall, leaving sarcastic comments against the Ennahda party, which won a majority in Tunisia's constituent elections last month, and its head Rached Ghannouchi.
Abdelhadi Ben Seghir dia nanamarika momba ilay hetsika, miaraka amin'ny fanakianana an'i Ghannouchi: ||| Abdelhadi Ben Seghir commented on the event with criticism to Ghannouchi:
Tohanako ireo rahalahy te-hitafy Hijab ho firaisankina amin'i Ghannouchi izay misafidy ny Chador! ||| I support my brothers who want to wear Hijab in solidarity with Ghannouchi who prefers the Chador!
Ao amin'ny fanbehoan-keviny dia tsy manam-panantenana loatra i Ines Ben Hamida momba ilay hetsika: ||| Ines Ben Hamida was not optimistic about the event in her comment:
Indrisy fa ho tena ho vitsy dia vitsy ireo lehilahy hitafy hijab ho fanehoana firaisankina. ||| Men who will wear Hijab in solidarity will unfortunately be a small minority.
Emad Basta, mpampiasa Facebook, dia nanoratra ny tsy fitovian-keviny ao amin'ny rindrin'ilay hetsika: ||| Facebook user Emad Basta wrote in disagreement on the event's wall:
Tsy afaka ny hanaiky an'izao aho, na ny vehivavy aza dia tsy tokony hisalobona, tsy henatra akory ny vehivavy fa mitovy amin'ny lehilahy amin'ny resaka zo satria ry zareo no tomponandraikitra amin'ny fitohizan'ny taranak'olombelona, ry zareo no mpanjakavavin'izao tontolontsika izao. ||| I cannot agree to this, women should not cover up either, women are not a disgrace they are as equal in rights to any man if not even needing more rights as they are the ones responsible for the reproduction of the human race they are the queens of our world.
Ejiptiana iray antsoina hoe (tsia amin'ny fanaovana tsinontsinona sy ny fakàna an-tendrony) dia nanoratra fa izy dia manohitra ny fanararaotana ara-pinoana atao amin'ny anaran'ny politika: ||| An Egyptian user called (no to backwardness and extremism) wrote he was against abusing religion in the name of politics:
Lavina ny fampiasàna ny marika ara-pivavahana ary lavina ny fitsabahan'ny politika amin'ny resaka finoana. ||| No to using religious signs and no to politicizing religion.
Masina loatra ny fivavahana, ary ny finoana ara-pivavahana dia ekena ambonin'ny fiovàna ara-politika izay mbola isokafan'ny adihevitra sy ny tsy fitovian-kevitra. ||| Religion is sacred and religious beliefs are agreed upon while political changes are open to interpretation and disagreement.
Ejiptiana iray hafa, Amre El-Abyad, no nanoratra fanamarihana iray mikasika ny tokony ho anjara toeran'ny Lohataona Arabo amin'ny fandrisihana ny vehivavy: ||| Another Egyptian Amre El-Abyad wrote a comment about the role the Arab Spring should play in empowering women:
Ny Lohataona Arabo dia tsy tokony ho fanonganana mpanao jadona ihany. ||| Arab Spring should not be about toppling dictators.
Ny demaokrasia dia miainga amin'ny toe-tsaina. ||| Democracy starts at the mind level.
Mila mamongotra ireo fadifady manohintohina ny herim-panovàna isika: ny fanjakan'ny lehilahy, ny fivavahana diso toerana ary ny fironana be loatra amin'ny ara-nofo. ||| We have to topple the taboos that are holding back our innovative potentials: patriarchy, misplaced religiosity and sexual obsessions.
Fomba tranainy ho an'ny Semitika ny hijab izay nandraman'ny kolontsaina maro taminà vanim-potoana iray voafaritra. ||| Hijab is an ancient Semitic custom experienced at one time by so many cultures.
Na dia efa toa an-dalan'ny fanjavonany aza izy io tamin'ny taonjato faha-20, dia mbola tafatoetra sy niha-nahazo vàhana be manerana ny tontolo Arabo amin'izao fotoana misy antsika izao. ||| Although it had seemed to be on its way of vanishing in the 20th century, it persisted and has gained wide currency all over the Arab world in our present time.
Mazava tsara, tondro ho an'ny filàntsika mivaivay manao revolisiona miainga amin'ny kolontsaina sy ny toe-tsaina io ||| Clearly, an indicator of our dire need to take the revolution up the cultural and mind levels.
Ny hany lehilahy nampakatra ny sariny dia i Magdy Abdelraheem ilazany fa maneho firaisankina izy: ||| The only male to have posted his picture was Magdy Abdelraheem saying he is showing solidarity:
Sa Neb dia tonga hatramin'ny firesahana raha toa marina ka zavatra takian'ny finoana ny Hijab na tsia. ||| Sa Neb went to discuss whether Hijab is a religious obligation or not:
Raha mitafy Hijab ny lehilahy ho fanehoana firaisankina amin'ny vehivavy ka lazaina fa mariky ny maha-vehivavy ny Hijab dia tsy hitako izay tena maha-Islamika an'izany. ||| If men wore Hijab in solidarity with women that will be a confession that Hijab is part of a woman's femininity and I do not see it as an Islamic must.
