Makedonia: Mitohy Ny Raharaham-Panarahamaso Ny Fahalotoan-dRivotra ao Skopje ||| Macedonia: Skopje's Pollution Monitoring Saga Continues
Nandray fepetra tamin'ny tsy fisian'ny rafi-pandrefesana ny taha-pahadiovan'ny rivotra an-tserasera ao Skopje tamin'ny alalan'ny famoahana saripika eo amin'ny bolongana ny ONG Greenbox. ||| NGO Greenbox is compensating for the lack of web interface for the air pollution measuring system in Skopje by posting photos of the display on their blog.
Nitsahatra tsy nanome vaovao an-tserasera intsony nanomboka hatramin'ny fiandohan'ny taona 2012 ny rafi-pandrefesana ny fahadiovan'ny (fahalotoan'ny) rivotra tao an-drenivohitra Makedonianina. ||| The system for measuring air pollution in the capital of Macedonia stopped providing online data at the beginning of 2012.
Ela loatra ny fandraisan'ny fiadidiana ny tanàna ny andraikiny, ka niteraka fahatezerana teo amin'ny mponina ao an-toerana izany, izay naneho ny fisalasalany tamin'izay antony nanapahana ny fanatanterahana ity fomba mampiseho mangarahara ity. ||| The city government, which owns the system, was slow to react, and this fueled the dissatisfaction of the local residents, who expressed doubts about the motives behind the discontinuation of this transparent practice.
Manohy mijery akaiky ny fandrosoan'izany raharaha izany ny Greenbox, mandefa vaovao farany foana ao amin'ny bilaoginy sy ny pejy Facebook. ||| Greenbox continued to track the progress of this case, posting regular updates on their blog and Facebook profile.
Tamin'ny Febroary, niteraka tsy fifaliana faobe teo amin'ny olom-pirenena ihany koa ny tsy fahaizana manatanteraka ny fandraisana andraikitra. ||| On February 15, 2012, the measuring station's display malfunctioned also, causing a new wave of citizen dissatisfaction.
Hafatra tao amin'ny Fisefoana Skopje Milaza fa misy zavatra tsy mety kely tamin'ny 15 Feb 2012. ||| The message on the Skopje Breathing display declaring that something went wrong on Feb. 15, 2012.
Namaly ihany ny tanàna tamin'ny fanofana orinasa iray hanamboatra ny efijery toa andro taoriana, ary taorian'izany dia namoaka filazana fa eo ampikarakarana mandritra ny taona. ||| The city finally reacted by hiring a company to repair the display two days later, and after that published a tender for maintenance services during the year.
Araka ny antontan-kevitra navoakan'ny tanànan'i Skopje eo amin'ny fitaovana elektronika mampanao tolo-bidy dia tokony hametraka tolo-bidy mialoha ny 2 marsa ny orinasa, ka izay mahavita ny mora indrindra no hofantenana. ||| According to the documentation published by the City of Skopje on the electronic system for public procurement, the companies should submit offers by March 2, and the cheapest offer will be selected.
Tsy milaza manokana ny filazana raha voatery hamelona indray ny takelaka an-tserasera "Fisefoana Skopje", fitaovana mamoaka mivantana ny marik'isa tondroin'ny mari-pandrefesana, izay mahazo ny tolo-bidy na tsia. ||| The available tender documentation does not specify if the tender winner will be obliged to re-activate the webpage "Skopje Breathing", which published live data feed based on the measurements.
Io takelaka io no ahafahan'ny mponina an'arivony mahalala vaovao haingana indrindra momba ny fahalotoan'ny rivotra, izay avy folo heny noho izay fetra farany ambony azo leferina indraindray. ||| This page enabled thousands of citizens to get first-hand information about the air pollution, which at times was up to 10 times higher than the allowed maximum.
Screenshot of a post from Greenbox blog with photos of the Skopje Breathing display. ||| Screenshot of a post from Greenbox blog with photos of the Skopje Breathing display.
Nandritra izany fotoana izany, Greenbox nanambara fa hamoaka izay marik'isa miseho amin'ny alalan'ny bolongana ny mpikambana ao aminy isa-maraina ary nanao izany nandritra ny folo andro farany. ||| In the meantime, Greenbox declared that their members will provide the data from the display via their blog, and have been doing that every morning for the past ten days.
Nanasa ny mpiara-monina ihany koa ry zareo haka sary izay hita eo amin'ny efijery amin'ny fotoana hafa mandritra ny andro k handefa izany any amin'ny Greenbox, satria mety hiova noho ny fiasan'ny orinasa sy ny fifamoivoizana ny taha-pahalotoana. ||| They also invite citizens to take snapshots of the display at other times of the day and send them to Greenbox, because the levels of pollution may vary, depending on the intensity of industrial and traffic activity.
Ny fandrefesana voarakitra mivoaka ao amin'ny Sokajy "Fisefoana Skopje" ao amin'ny bolongana Greenbox dia nampiseho ny ambaratongan'ny kalitaon'ny rivotra nandritra ny andro faramparany, miainga amin'ny "mahafarofy" mankany amin'ny "eo ho eo ny fahalotoana" ka hatramin'ny "madio." ||| The recorded measurements published in the "Skopje Breathing" category of the Greenbox blog showed various levels of air quality in the past few days, from "unhealthy" to "moderately polluted" to "clean".
Siria: Fanomezam-boninahitra Ilay Mpanao Gazety Teratany Amerikana Marie Colvin Namoy Ny Ainy Tao Homs ||| Syria: Homage to American Journalist Marie Colvin Killed in Homs
Ampahany amin'ny vaovao manokana mikasika ny hetsi-panoheran'i Syrie taona 2011/12 ity lahatsoratra ity. ||| This post is part of our special coverage Syria Protests 2011/12.
Maty tamin'ny herinandro lasa teo i Marie Colvin sy Rémi Olchik, raha nisy nanafika ny toerana vonjimaika natao ho ivon'ny haino aman-jery tao an-tananan'i Baba Amr, tao Homs, ao Syria. ||| Marie Colvin and Rémi Olchik were killed last week, when the makeshift media centre they were at in Baba Amr, in Homs, Syria, was attacked.
Samy mpanao gazety nasaina namita iraka avokoa izy roa ireo. ||| Both were journalists on a mission.
Solotena vahinin'ny Sunday Times mpifandray avy any ivelany no andraikitr'ilay vehivavy ary mpaka sary ho azy no asan'ilay lehilahy. ||| She was the Sunday Times' foreign correspondent and he was her photographer.
Tamin'ny Alakamisy 23 Febroary 2012, dia taitra ny tany tontolo raha naheno ny vaovao mikasika ny nahafatesan'izy ireo tao anatin'ny fatin-korontan'ilay ivontoeran'ny mpanao gazety nataon'ny hery mpmba an'i Assad ho lasibatra. ||| On Thursday, February 23, 2012, the world woke up to the news of their death under the debris of the press center that was targeted by pro-Assad forces.
Samy naneho fihetsika ho fahatsiarovana ireo mpanao gazety namoy ny ainy ireo ny haino aman-jery rehetra sy ny mponina amin'ny aterineto maneran-tany, fahafatesana izay navoaka tamin'ireo lohateny vaventy, nisarika ny saina amin'ny zava-manjo ny vahoaka Siriana namoy ny ainy isan'andro noho fihetsiketsehana fanoherana ny fanjakan'i Assad. ||| Both international media outlets and netizens around the world paid homage to the murdered journalists, whose death captured headlines, drawing attention to the plight of Syrians being killed on a daily basis for protesting against the Assad regime.
Mpikambana ao amin'ny Facebook an-jatony maneran-tany no nanolotra ny teny fampiononana ho an'ny mpiara-miasa aminy. ||| Hundreds of Facebook users from across the world expressed their condolences on the group.
Ny sasany amin'izy ireo dia mpankafy azy, ny hafa dia mpiara-miasa taminy fahiny ary ny ambiny dia mpanao gazety izay niara-niasa taminy tany amin'ny toeran-kafa toy ny tany Misrata, Libya. ||| Some were fans, others were former colleagues and the rest were journalists whom she had worked with on other battlefields, such as in Misrata, Libya.
Santionany amin'ny fihetseham-po tao amin'ny takelaka Facebook ireto manaraka ireto: ||| Here is a sample of reactions from the Facebook page:
Mandria am-piadanana... Vehivavy mahery fo! ||| Rest in peace... Heroine!
Vehivavy be fahasahiana ianao...Tena midera anao aho ...velona mandrakizay ny lova navelanao... RIP ||| What a courageous woman you were...I truly admire you ...youre legacy will live on.. RIP
Ireo mpanoratra ireo dia nahatsiaro tsara an'i Colvin ho mpanao gazety sahisahy nanana fahasahiana mitatitra momba ny ady avy any ampotony any, lohalaharana tao Chennai, Inde, hatrany Misrata, tao Libia hatrany Homs, tao Siria. ||| The commentators remembered Colvin as a brave journalist who had the courage to cover wars from the front lines, from Chennai, India, to Misrata, Libya to Homs, Syria.
Nampiasa haino aman-jery sosialy ihany koa ireo olona fanta-daza maro amin'ny sehatry ny fampahalalam-baovao mba hanomezam-boninahitra an'i Colvin tamin'ny alalan'ny famoahana ny sanganasany faramparany teo amin'ny maha mpanao gazety azy. ||| Many other known personalities in the media also used social media to pay tribute to Colvin by sharing her latest's journalistic work.
Vao avy namaky teny fanomezam-boninahitra nahavariana natolotra ho an'i Marie Colvin nosoratan'ilay tonian-dahatsorany John Witherow tao amin'ny Sunday Times aho tao amin'ny gazety androany. ||| Just read a quite brilliant tribute to Marie Colvin by her Sunday Times Editor, John Witherow, in tonight's paper.
Maty ny alarobia i Colvin. ||| Colvin died on Wednesday.
Ity no hafatra maika farany sady nampalahelo nalefany avy tao Baba Amr: ||| This is her last, heart-breaking dispatch from Baba Amr
Saingy roa andro monja taorian'ny nahafatesan'i Olchik sy Colvin tampoka, izay nampihetsi-po, dia nanely horonantsary iray ny fahitalavitry ny fanjakana Siriana Al Ikhbaria Suria nanda ny hadisoany tamin'ny fahafatesan'ireo mpanao gazety roa ireo. ||| But, only two days after the tragic death of Olchik and Colvin, the Syrian state television Al Ikhbaria Suria released a video denying any responsibility over the murder of both Journalists.
Nanambara io horonantsary io (rohy etssy ambony) fa mety ho mpanao gazety mpitsikilo i Colvin sy Ochlik, izay angamba niditra an-tsokosoko teo amin'ny firenena - izay mihitsy no nataon'izy ireo - saika hanohana ireo vondrona mitam-piadiana avy amin'ny ankolafy mpanohitra. ||| The video (link above) suggested that Colvin and Ochlik could have been intelligence agents who got into the country secretly - which they did - to help support armed groups in the opposition.
Andro vitsivitsy taorian'io fanafihana io dia nilaza ny fanjakana Siriana fa halevina ao Siria ny nofo mangatsiakany fa tsy ho averina any Etazonia. ||| A few days after the attack, the Syrian regime said the slain journalist will be buried in Syria and will not be extradited back to the United States.
Tamin'io fotoana io ihany, - tao anatin'ilay fandaharana Anderson Cooper AC360 - dia namoaka horonantsary iray misy ny renin'i Colvin, Rosanne Colvin ny CNN izay mitalaho manao hoe: "Tiako hody an-tanindrazana ny zanako vavy." ||| At the same time, CNN - Anderson Cooper's AC360 - just released a video of Colvin's mother Rosanne Colvin: "I want my daughter home".
Tao anatin'ilay horonantsary iray teo aloha, tao anatin'ny fandaharan'i Anderson Cooper nivoaka ny Alatsinainy alina, dia nanamafy i Rosanne Colvin fa "tsy maintsy ho tanterak'izy ireo (ny fianakavian'i Colvin) izany na amin'ny fomba ahoana na amin'ny fomba ahoana ary na haharitra ela aza izany." ||| In the preview video of Anderson Cooper's Monday night show, Rosanne Clovin asserted that "they (Colvin's family) are going to do it no matter how difficult it is or how long it will take".
Vaovao nampalahelo ny nahafatesan'i Colvin ho an'ny haino aman-jery maneran-tany sy ho an'ireo manome lanjany ny vaovao izay namoy vehivavy mpanao gazety malaza mahafantatra tsara ny hasin'ny fampielezam-baovao. ||| The death of Colvin was a sad news for the media world and news junkies who had lost a great female journalist who clearly understood the essence of journalism.
Fifidianana filoham-pirenena an-tsary ||| Presidential Election in Pictures
Nanatontosa ny fandrotsaham-batony tamin'ny alalan'ny fifidianana filoham-pirenena voalohany indray tao anatin'ny folo taona izao ny alahady 31 oktobra teo ny mpifidy voasoratra anarana any Cote d'Ivoire, izany dia noho ny ady an-trano izay vaky nanomboka ny taona 2002 sy ny fifandirana nanaraka izany. ||| On this Sunday, October 31st, registered voters in Cote d'Ivoire cast their ballots in the first presidential election in 10 years, due to the Civil War that broke out in 2002 and the subsequent issues that arose from it.
In'enina nahemotra ny fifidianana nanomboka ny 2005 rehefa tonga teo amin'ny fetrany ny fe-potoana 5 taona nitondran'i Laurent Gbagbo amin'ny fomba ofisialy noho ny savorovoro nanodidina ny fanesorana ny fiadiana teny ampelatanan'ny mpioko sy ny lisi-pifidianana. ||| The election date had been postponed six times since 2005, when Laurent Gbagbo's five-year mandate officially came to an end, amid rows over rebel disarmament and voter registration.
Hotanterahina amin'ny 28 novambra ho avy izao moa ny dingana faharoa. ||| A second round is scheduled for November 28.
Na dia nisinisy ihany aza ny fahatarana teo amin'ny fisokafan'ny biraom-pifidianana dia nilamina ihany tamin'ny ankapobeny ny fandrotsaham-bato. ||| Despite some initial delays in some polling stations, voting has been reportedly peaceful and the turnout appears to have been good.
Nanangana kaonty Twitter ny African Elections Project hanaraha-maso ny fivoaran'ny fifidianana nandritra ny dingana voalohany, ary nisioka an-tsarasera (ni-tweet) tamin'ny alalan'ny fampiasana ny tenifototra CIV2010 kosa olo-tsotra tia mitati-baovao sy ny mpisioka an-tserasera tany Cote d'Ivoire nandritra io tontolo andron'ny fifidianana io. ||| The African Elections Project created a Twitter account to follow the developments of the voting day, and various citizen journalists and Twitterers in Cote d'Ivoire also tweeted updates throughout the day using the hashtag CIV2010.
Indreto ny sary voafantina hita tao amin'ny Twitter nandritra ny androm-pifidianana: ||| Here is a selection of pictures of the voting day shared on Twitter:
Filaharana teo ivelan ny biraom-pifidianana iray tany Abidjan. ||| Lines outside of polling station in Abidjan.
Mpifidy iray falifaly nampiseho ny fanondrony voamarika ranomainty avy nifidy. ||| Happy voter showing the ink mark on her finger after casting the ballot.
Raha somary afa-po sy nilamindamina ny mpifidy tany Cote d'Ivoire nandritra ny androm-pifidianana, dia hita ho nanam-pahasahiranana kosa ireo mpiray tanindrazana aminy any Frantsa tamin'ny fanefana ny adidiny. ||| While voters in Cote d'Ivoire enjoyed a relatively smooth and peaceful election day, it seems that their fellow Ivorians living in France had a harder time casting their ballots.
Teo ho eo amin'ny 11.500 eo ny isan'ny mpifidy voasoratra anarana tany amin'ny biraom-pifidianana 28 nisy tany amin'ny faritr'i Paris, saingy araka ny nolazain'ny France24 dia maro tamin'izy ireo no tsy nisokatra tamin'ny alahady ka niteraka hatezerana tamin'ny mpifidy. ||| About 11,500 voters were registered to vote in one of the 28 polling stations in the Paris region, but according to France24, several of them failed to open on Sunday sparking anger among voters.
Naka sary ireo 500 nivorivory ivelan'ny masoivoho Ivoariana tao an-drenivohitra frantsay boriborintany faha-16 ny mpisioka an-tserasera Jolan. ||| Twitterer Jolan photographed some of the 500 voters gathered outside the Ivorian consulate in French capital's swanky 16th district.
Ireo Ivoariana miandry ny fotoana hifidianany eo ivelan'ny masoivoho any Paris. ||| Ivorian expats waiting to vote at the consulate in Paris.
Ny mpanoratra Amerikana Carol Spindel izay nanoratra boky momba ny fiainana an-tanàna ambanivohitra Ivoariana iray nitondra ny lohateny hoe In the shadow of the sacred grove, roapolo taona lasa izay dia nizotra nankany Cote d'Ivoire indray hiresaka momba ny fifidianana filoham-pirenena. ||| American writer Carol Spindel, who wrote a book 20 years ago about life in an Ivorian village titled In the shadow of the sacred grove, recently traveled to Cote d'Ivoire to write about the presidential elections.
Noho io toe-javatra iray io indrindra no nananganany bolongana iray, One village votes, izay anangonany antontan-kevitra miresaka ny fomba fifidianana. ||| For that purpose she set up a blog, One village votes, in which she's been documenting the electoral process.
Tamin'ny alahady moa dia namoaka sary maromaro nitranga nandritra ny fifidianana tany avaratr'i Korhogo izy: ||| On Sunday she posted some photos of the election day in the northern town of Korhogo:
Fifidianana tany Korhogo. ||| Voting in Korhogo.
Andro vitsy lasa izay dia namangy fikambanam-behivavy iray izay nianatra ny fomba atao rehefa mifidy tao anaty aizina, miaraka amin'ny fanilo sy ny dikasarin'ny vatom-pifidianana tany an-tanàna kely ambanivohitra akaiky an'i Korhogo i Carol: ||| A few days earlier, Carol visited a group of women in a village near Korhogo who were learning how to vote in the dark, with the aid of a flashlight and a photocopy of a ballot:
Vehivavy nianatra ny fomba fifidianana andro vitsy nialoha ny fifidianana. ||| Women learning how to vote a few days before the election.
Tokony ambara amin'ny fomba ofisialy ao anatin'ny 72 ora manaraka moa ny valim-pifidianana tamin'ny alahady teo. ||| The results of the Sunday Presidential election should be officially announced within the next 72 hours.
Filipina: Adihevitra Mikasika ny Volavolan-dalàna Momba Ny Fisarahana Am-Panambadiana ||| Philippines: Debate on Divorce Bill
Mialoha ny adihevitra mafàna mikasika ny Volavolan-dalàna Momba Fahasalamana ara-Pananahana, efa tsy miombon-kevitra amin-javatra iray sahady indray ny Filipiana amin'ny fandinihana ilay ampahan-dalàna iray mahabe resaka: ny lalàna momba ny fisaraham-panambadiana. ||| Just before the intense debate on the Reproductive Health bill, Filipinos are once more at odds with each other in considering another controversial piece of legislation: the Divorce bill.
Ilay adihevitra momba ny fandinihana ny lafiny araka ny lalàna momba ny fisaraham-panambadiana dia nanomboka tamin'ny nahenoana tany Filipina ny vaovao mikasika ny fitsapan-kevi-bahoaka natao tany Malta nanome alàlana sy nampanjary ho ara-dalàna ny fisaraham-panambadiana andry vitsy talohan'izao. ||| The debate on legalizing divorce took a kick-start when news of Maltese referendum favoring divorce reached the Philippines a few days ago.
Io dia nanosika koa ireo vondrona tia fanavaozana hampiaka-peo hitaky ny firenena hanaraka ny dian'i Malta ka hanao izay haha ara-dalàna ny fisaraham-panambadiana ao amin'ity firenena ity izay Katolika no betsaka amin'ny vahoakany. ||| This has prompted progressive groups to make a bolder call for the country to follow in Malta's steps and legalize divorce in a predominantly Catholic nation.
Tsy zava-baovao ny adihevitra momba ny fisaraham-panambadiana, jereo eto ny fantina momba ireo fomba fijery nandritra ny atrikasa AttyatWork tamin'ny taona lasa manodidina io olana io. ||| The debate on divorce is nothing new, see here AttyatWork's round-up of talking points on the issue from last year.
Filipino Thinkers dia manana famehezana goavana tokoa momba ny fomba nitondràna ny adihevitra sy ny safidy hanao ny fitsapankevi-bahoaka tao Malta. ||| Filipino Thinkers has a great digest of how the debate was settled and how the referendum unfolded in Malta.
Mbola tsaratsara kokoa noho izay, manao fampitahàna ny olana misy ao Filipina sy tany Malta ihany koa izy io. ||| More importantly, it provides a side by side comparison of the issue between the Philippines and Malta:
Ankoatry ny fiafarany nahafaly, izay nametraka an'i Filipina ho hany firenena tokana tsy misy divorce1, misy itovitoviany amin'ny adihevitra nataontsika momba ny fahasalamana ara-pananahana ny fitsapankevi-bahoaka momba ny fisarahana am-panambadiana tany Malta: ||| Aside from the happy ending, which left the Philippines the only country without divorce1, the story of Malta's divorce referendum shares similarities with our own reproductive health debates:
Ireo firenena roa ireo dia samy kitro ifaharan'ny fivavahana Katolika: Malta ao Eoraopa, ary Filipina any Azia; Ny Katolika no tena betsaka any amin'ireo firenena roa ireo: 95% ao Malta, 80% aoFilipina; ireo ady roa ireo dia eo amin'ny eveka mpifikitra amin'ny teo aloha sy ireo Katolika mpandàla fihavaozana no tena misy. ||| both countries are last bastions of Catholicism: Malta in Europe, the Philippines in Asia; both countries are predominantly Catholic: 95% in Malta, 80% in the Philippines; and both battles are primarily between progressive Catholics and conservative bishops.
Ary amin'ireo tranga roa ireo, ireo eveka mpifikitra amin'ny teo aloha dia mampiasa ny fampitahorana mba hitazonana sy hifehezana ny ondriny. ||| And in both cases, the conservative bishops use fear mongering to keep their flock in line.
Mba hijerena malaky ny fahasamihafana misy amin'ny fisarahana am-panambadiana, ny fanafoanana ary ny fisarahana araka ny lalàna, manana toro-làlana malaky momba ireo tranga samihafa i Lyle R. Santos. ||| For a quick refresher on the differences between divorce, annulment and legal separation, Lyle R. Santos has a quick guide in layman's terms.
Miaraka amin'ny fankatoavana ny fisarahana am-panambadiana any Malta, i Filipina izany sisa no firenena tokana mandràra azy io manerana izao tontolo izao. ||| With Malta's approval of divorce, the Philippines is now the lone country in the world that prohibits it.
Ho an'i Blue Dela Kanluran, ny adihevitra momba ny fisarahana am-panambadiana dia tsy tokony hafototra fotsiny amin'izay zava-misy izay: ||| For Blue Dela Kanluran, the debate on divorce should not be framed on this fact alone:
Tahaka izay efa nambarako tany aloha dia manohitra ny fisarahana am-panambadiana aho na izany aza, tsy misakana firenena iray izay manana ny fiandrianany aho hisafidy izay heveriny ho mendrika ho an'ny firenena sy ho azy ireo, sahala amin'izay nasehon'i Malta. ||| As i had stated earlier my stand is against divorce however, I will not begrudge a sovereign nation of their right to decide whats best for their country and themselves as Malta has displayed here.
(Jereo, izany no ohatra amin'ny fisarahan'ny Fitondrana sy ny Finoana. ||| (See, that is an example of the separation of Church and State).
Nitarika ahy hanontany tena izany, inona no ho fiantraikan'ny maha- hany firenena tokana an-tany mandràra ny fisarahana am-panambadiana ao Filipina? ||| Which leads me to wonder, what effects will the stigma of the only country which outlaws divorce have on the Philippines?
Raha ny hevitro manokana, hampanano-sarotra ny lalàna mankasitraka ny fisarahana am-panambadiana io amin'ny ho avy, tsy hoe fotsiny noho ny fitsabahan'ny fiangonana fa noho ny holatra efa nambara tany aloha (izay tsy amin'izany mihitsy no tokony hifandresen-dahatra momba ny lalàna) ||| Personally, I think this will make pro-divorce legislation in the future more difficult not only because of the meddling of the Church but with the stigma earlier stated as well (Which is not how legislation should be argued).
Cocoy mahita fa efa naman'ny lany sahady ny volavolan-dalàna momba ny Fahasalamana ara-pananahana ary amin'izao fotoana ny volavolan-dalàna momba ny fisarahana am-panambadiana dia tahaka ny "reboot" ho an'i Filipina (Avy amin'ny mpandika: raha amin'ny resaka solosaina, dia fiaingana vaovao indray no hevitry ny 'reboot'), miala amin'ny toeran'ny fanjakana anjakan'ny resa-pinoana ho amina fitondrana laika: ||| Cocoy views the near-approval of the Reproductive Health and now the Divorce bill as a "reboot" of the Philippines, moving from a predominantly religious state in a secular one:
Ka raha mivadika ho lalàna moa ilay volavolan-dalàna momba ny Fahasalamana ara-pananahana, ary arahan'ny volavolan-dalàna momba n y fisarahana am-panambadiana avy eo? ||| If the Reproductive Health bill becomes law, and it is followed by a divorce bill?
Dia fiaingàna roa sosona ho an'i Filipina izany. ||| That would be one continuity reboot for the Philippines.
Manamarika izany fa miofo miandàlana ho firenena laika tsy ho eo ambany vahohon'i Vatikana intsony. ||| It signals that the nation is slowly becoming secular and less under the thrall of the Vatican.
Amin'ny maha-Katolika, ho ahy, manome vintana iray ho an'ny fiangonana izany mba hifantohany bebe kokoa amin'ny ara-panahy. ||| As a Catholic, for me, it presents an opportunity for the Church to focus on the spiritual.
Mila toriteny sy tari-dàlana aho mba hahatonga ahy ho olona mendrika. ||| I want sermons and direction that make me a better person.
Tsy ilaiko akory ny fiangonana hiteny hoe inona no tsy mety ao amin'ny governemanta ao. ||| I don't need the Church to tell me what is wrong with government.
Ireo Filipiana any rehetra any dia efa mahalala sahady ny tsy mety eo amin'ny fireneny. ||| Filipinos everywhere already know what's wrong with our nation.
Fotoana hanan-tantara izao mba hanitsiantsika izany. ||| It is that time in history that we fix it.
Ilaiko hitondra fanampiana ho an'io ramatoa mpikarakara tokantrano matetika matim-bonon'ny vadiny io ny fiangonana. ||| I need my church to help guide that poor maid who is always beaten up by her husband.
Ilaiko ho mpitari-dàlana ireo ankizy mpirenireny an-dalambe sy hampiditra azy ireny an-tsekoly ny fiangonana. ||| I need a Church that guides street children away from the streets, and into education.
Mila io fiangonana io hanao zavatra aho. ||| I need this church to be relevant.
Dreamwalker mahita fifaliana amin'ny zava-misy hoe ity volavolan-dalàna ity, tsy raharahiana izay fisamantsamahana sy fifanoheran-kevitra any, dia miteraka adihevitra eo amin'ny fiarahamonina, ary dia mandrisika ny tsirairay handray anjara amin'ny fifanakalozan-kevitra eto amin'ny firenena: ||| Dreamwalker takes delight in the fact that this proposed laws, no matter how dividing and controversial, sparks debate among society, thus encouraging everyone to take part in the national discourse:
Mitohy zendana hatrany aho amin'ny fahitàna ny Filipiana toa lasa manara-maso akaiky ny zava-mitranga ao amin'ny fireneny sy ny fomba ataontsika hahazo vaovao misimisy kokoa mikasika ny lalàna eto amintsika - na ny vao atolotra na ny efa nisy. ||| I continue to be amazed by how Filipinos seem to be more aware of what is happening in the country and how we seek to be more informed about our laws - both proposed and existing.
Raha ny hevitro, hitondra ho amin'ny zavatra tsara ihany izany. ||| In my opinion, this can only lead to more good.
Maju di amitondra tohan-kevitra mazava amin'ny fampitandremana fa hoe mpanao lalànantsika dia tokony hijery tsara an'ilay laàna momba ny fisarahana am-panambadiana amin'ny maso mahiratra tsara: ||| Maju brings forward a valid point in cautioning that our lawmakers should take up the divorce law with a keener eye:
Tokony horaisintsika anaty kajikajy ihany koa ny tsara sy ny ratsy amin'ny fisian'ny lalàna momba ny fisarhana am-panambadiana. ||| We should also get onto considerations on how good or bad are existing divorce laws.
any amin'ny firenena maro, indrindra fa ireo fehezin'ny Sharia, tsy mitovy ny zon'ny lahy sy ny vavy faritan'ny lalàna amin'ny resaka fisarahana am-panambadiana. ||| In many countries, notably those under the Sharia, the rights of women and men in divorce are not the same.
Farany, ity misy resaka mahasoa avy amina mpisolovava iray, Connie Veneracion, momba ny fanafoanana fanambadiana, ny fisarahana araka ny lalàna misy amin'izao fotoana ao anatin'ny lalàna Filipiana ary ny fomba mety hanentsenan'ny fisarahana am-panambadiana ny lavaka eo amin'ny Fepetran'ny fianakaviana ankehitriny: ||| Lastly, here's a good discussion by a lawyer, Connie Veneracion, about annulment, legal separation under current Philippine laws and how divorce could plug the holes in the current Family Code:
Taoriana kely, na izany aza, nazava ihany fa na teo aza ny hakelin'ny fahafaha-mihetsika omen'ilay hoe tsy fahatomombanana ara-psikolojika, misy lavaka mangotanatàna be ao anatin'ilay lalàna. ||| Later on, however, it became clear that despite the leeway allowed by the concept of psychological incapacity, there was a huge gaping hole in the law.
Làlana lavitr'ezaka be ny fanafoanana fanambadiana araka ny lalàna raha jerena amin'ny ara-bolan'ny ankabeazan'ireo Filipiana. ||| Annulment is a very expensive legal procedure beyond the financial capacity of majority of the Filipinos.
Ny mpanasa lamba miaina anaty trano tsy zarizary ary iharan'ny herisetra ara-nofo ataon'ny vadiny mpimamo lava dia tsy ho afaka mihitsy hanao an'izany. ||| The laundrywoman living in the slums who is physically abused by the drunken jobless husband could not afford it.
Ankoatry ny fandaniana, elabe sy mandreraka ny dingana arahana. ||| In addition to the expense, the process was a long and tedious one.
Farany, ireo mpomba ny fisarahana am-panambadiana dia nanomboka nitabataba indray. ||| Eventually, the divorce advocates started making noise again.
Araka ny efa nahiana, ny fiangonana Katolika dia manana fomba fandinika misimisy kokoa nentiny niaraka tamin'ny fandresena lahatra hanoherana ny fisarahana am-panambadiana. ||| As expected, the Catholic church is getting more imaginative in coming up with arguments against divorce.
Mampalahelo fa betsaka amin'ny Filipiana no tsy afaka mijery n y fanambadiana ivelan'ny sehatry ny ara-pinoana. ||| It is sad that most Filipinos cannot view marriage independently from its religious context.
Fa mbola mampalahelo kokoa ny mahita fa ny ankabeazan'ny Filipiana dia tsy mihevitra ny fanambadiany ho misy lanjany sy ara-dalàna raha tsy nandalo fiangonana. ||| It is even more sad that most Filipinos do not consider themselves validly married unless married in church.
Faran'izay mampalahelo. ||| Very sad indeed.
Noho izay, hameno ny banga amin'ny fahabangana misy ao amin'ny Fepetran'ny Fanambadiana ve ny fandaniana lalàna momba ny fisarahana am-panambadiana? ||| So, will the passage of a divorce law patch the loopholes in the Family Code?
Miankina amin'ny hoe inona no avelan'ny lalàna hataontsika ho antony ara-dalàna hisarahana am-panambadiana ary inona no dingana harahana. ||| It depends on what the law will allow as valid grounds for divorce and what the required procedure will be.
Tany aloha dia efa nitranga ny hoe lalàna iray nolaniana toy ny vatomamy fitsentsitra (bonbon secette). ||| It has happened before that a law is passed as some sort of pacifier.
Afaka mandany lalàna iray momba ny 'fisarahana' am-panambadiana ny Kongresy, izay sehatra tery kely sy dingana manahirana mety handà ny tena anton'ilay fisarahana am-panambadiana. ||| Congress can pass a "divorce" law which such narrow grounds and complex process that it will effectively negate the very purpose of a divorce.
Mba fantatrareo, mba hilazana fotsiny fa hoe lany ilay lalàna momba ny fisarahana am-panambadiana. ||| You know, just so it can be said that a divorce law has been passed.
Manahy aho ny hoe ho afa-po amin'izany ireo mpandàla fiovàna sy ny mpandàla ny fisarahana am-panambadiana. ||| I doubt if that will satisfy the progressives and the divorce advocates.
Rosia: Ankamantatra alohan'ny Fifidianana ao Vladivostok ||| Russia: Vladivostok's Pre-Election Puzzle
Mialoha ny fifidianana filoham-pirenena rosiana amin'ny 4 Martsa izao, mafampana tanteraka ny rivo-politika. ||| On the eve of the March 4 presidential election in Russia, the level of political voltage has reached its tipping point.
Sady odian'ny manam-pahefana Rosiana fanina ny fisian'ny fihetsiketsehana goavana manerana ny firenena, no tsy mamaly araka ny tokony izy ny fitakian'ny vahoaka izy ireo. ||| The Russian authorities are neither able to ignore the large-scale protests across the country, nor able to adequately respond to the people's demands.
Lasa resa-politika avokoa ny ataon'ny tsirairay sy ny zava-drehetra ankehitriny, tratran'izany rivo-politika mafana mialoha ny fifidianana izany ihany koa ny tanàn-dehibe farany atsinanana indrindra ao Vladivostok. ||| Everyone and everything has turned political now, and the Far Eastern city of Vladivostok has caught this pre-election fever as well.
Ny ohatra farany indrindra izao dia ny fisian'ny dokambarotra fanentanana mifono misitery izay miteraka adihevitra eo amin'ireo mpiserasera maro ao Vladivostok amin'izao fotoana izao. ||| The most recent example is the mysterious ad campaign that many of Vladivostok's netizens are discussing right now.
Mety ho lasa resa-barotra fotsiny ihany izany, fa tsy resa-politika - kanefa mahaliana indrindra ny vahoaka sy mampafàna ny adihevitra eo amin'izy ireo izany amin'ny alalan'ny fampiasana ny vaovao farany momba ny kisarisari-politika. ||| It may turn out to be a purely commercial, non-political project, but it definitely plays on public interest and ignites the debate by using up-to-date political images.
Voalohany tamin'izany, sora-baventy lehibe manontany hoe "Iza? ||| First, large banners asking "Who?
Mety tsara amin'ireo kandidà mirotsaka hofidiana filoham-pirenena amin'ny 4 Martsa izao izany fanontaniana izany - na tsy mety. ||| This question may well refer to the presidential candidates running in the March 4 election - or it may not.
Mitovy amin'ny fanentanana ara-barotra sy ara-politika avokoa ny fomba fijery eto: ny dokam-barotra voalohany tsy mampisongadina tsara ny mampiavaka ny entana/kandidà. ||| The approach here is common for both commercial and political campaigns: the initial ads do not point at any specific product/candidate explicitly.
dokam-barotra ara-politika mitovy amin'izany no niseho tao Vladivostok vao haingana, eto eto: ny voalohany milaza fa nanomboka tamin'ny taona 1917 no nopotehana ny firenena, nandritra ny revolisiona Rosiana, ary avy eo tamin'ny taona 1991, tamin'ny fiafaran'ny vanim-potoana Sovietika, ho hita eo izay hitranga amin'ity taona 2012 ity; ny faharoa kosa manontany hoe, "Faharavana, indray?" ||| Examples of similar political ads that have appeared in Vladivostok recently are here and here: the first one states that the country was first destroyed in 1917, during the Russian revolution, and then some more in 1991, at end of the Soviet era, while what happens in 2012 remains to be seen; the second one is asking, "Chaos, again"?
Tsy niandry ela ny valinteny - saingy, toy ny tamin'ny voalohany "Iza? ||| It did not take long for the answers to appear - but, just like the initial "Who?
Fotoana fohy taty aoriana, mpamahana bolongana gaga tamin'izany dokam-barotra izany ahitana sarin'olona mitovy amin'i PrimPogoda.ru, vavahadin-tserasera momba ny toetr'andro ao an-toerana: ||| Somewhat later, bloggers caught these ads with the same characters on PrimPogoda.ru, a local weather portal:
Mpisera LJ Alexhitrov nanome vahaolana amin'izany ankamantatra izany izay toa nankasitrahan'ireo fikambanana mpiserasera an-toerana. ||| LJ user Alexhitrov's solution to this puzzle is the one that the local online community seems to favor the most.
Nanamarika izy fa ahitana boaty misy marika ny dokam-barotra mikasika an'i PrimPogoda.ru ary ahitana tarehimarika koa isaky ny sarin'olona eo ambony - ary namoaka pikan-tsary avy amin'ny fandaharana amin'ny fahitalavitra ihany koa izy izay mampiseho santionana vato-pifidianana ampiasaina amin'ny fifidianana hoavy: ||| He pointed out that the PrimPogoda.ru ads had a checked box with a number next to each of the characters mentioned above - and he also supplied a screenshot of a TV news program that showed a sample voting ballot for the upcoming election:
Ny kandidà tsirairay hirotsaka hofidiana (ao anatin'ilay santionana vato-pifidianana avokoa) no asehon'ny sarin'olona iray (ao amin'ny dokam-barotra hafahafa) ary, eny, ahitana nomerao mifanaraka amin'izany amin'ilay vato-pifidianana. ||| Each presidential candidate (on the sample voting ballot) is represented by one of the characters (in the mysterious ads) and, of course, there's a corresponding number on the ballot.
Araka ny hevitr'i alexhitrov, Toruk Makto no misolo tena an'i Vladimir Zhirinovsky, lehiben'ny Antoko Liberaly Demokraty ; Bob Spaonjy kosa Sergey Mironov, lehiben'ny antoko Just Russia (rosia ihany); ary Vladimir Putin, #5, no mety ilay Soavaly mipalitao. ||| According to alexhitrov, Toruk Makto represents Vladimir Zhirinovsky, the leader of the Liberal Democratic Party ; Sponge Bob is Sergey Mironov, the leader of the Just Russia party; and Vladimir Putin, #5, has to be the proverbial Horse in the Coat.

Tsy ho ela dia ho fantatr'i Rosia ny anaran'ny filoham-pireneny manaraka. ||| Russia will learn the name of its next head of state relatively soon.

Global Voices Podcast: Bodoy Ity! ||| Global Voices Podcast: Occupy This!
Miarahaba ny rehetra! ||| Hello World!
Amin'ity fizarana ity no iresahantsika ny hevitra sy ny olana manodidina ny hetsi-panoherana ataon'ny Hetsika Bodoy manerantany, rehefa mihaino ny raki-peo alefan'ny ekipa avy amin'ny vazantany efatra isika ||| In this episode we talk through some of the ideas and issues surrounding the global Occupy movement and protests, as we listen to recordings from our team in different parts of the world.
Amin'ity fizarana ity, "bodoiko" ny podcast miaraka amin'i Asteris Masouras, mpanoratra ao amin'ny Global Voices sy tonian-dahatsoratra ao amin'ny Global Voices amin'ny teny Grika ||| In this edition, I "occupy" the podcast with Asteris Masouras, Global Voices author and Global Voices in Greek editor.
Nanaraka akaiky ny hetsika an-tserasera Occupy manerantany hatramin'ny nanombohany Asteris. ||| Asteris has been monitoring the global Occupy movement online since it all began.
Koa iza indray ary no hiara-dia amintsika amin'ity andiana podcast iray ity? ||| Who better to accompany us through this edition of the podcast?
Niaraka niresaka tamin'ny alalan'ny Skype sy niady hevitra momba an'i Gresy, Eoropa, ary ny Bodoy izao tontolo izao izahay, indrindra momba ny fifampitan-kafatra ao anatin'ny hetsika sy amin'ny hetsika hafa. ||| We got together on Skype and discussed Greece, Europe, and the Occupy world, especially in regards to how the movement communicates with itself and others.

Pakistan: Fisaonana ireo namoy ny ainy tamin'ilay fianjerana fiaramanidina ||| Pakistan: Mourning Victims Of Plane Crash
Fahitana ny toeran'ny fianjerana tany Islamabad avy eo amin'ny tafo trano. ||| View of Islamabad crash site from rooftop.
Tamin'ny marainan'ny 28 Jolay, 2010, nianjera tao amin'ny vohitr'i Margalla tany Islamabad, renivohitr'i Pakistan, ny zotram-piaramanidina Airblue ED 202 avy any Karachi,. ||| On the morning of July 28, 2010, Airblue flight ED 202 flying from Karachi crashed into the Margalla Hills in Islamabad, the capital of Pakistan.
Mihoatra ny 150 ireo mpandeha tao anatiny tamin'ny fotoana nianjerany, tsy nisy na iray aza avotra. ||| Over 150 passengers were on board at the time of the crash, none of them survived.
Niteraka hatairana sy alahelo ity tranga voina ity. ||| The tragic incident has left many in shocks and grieves.
Mbola eo ampanaovana ny fanadihadiana ireo antony mety nahatonga ity fianjerana ireo tompon'andraikitra. ||| Investigations to determine the cause of the crash are still underway.
Raha mbola misaona ity loza ity ny maro, ny sasany kosa dia mametram-panontaniana maro momba iny fianjerana iny. ||| While many continue to mourn the tragedy, others are also raising critical questions about the crash.
Kalsoom Lakhani ao amin'ny CHUP-Changing Up Pakistan nisaona ity voina mampahalahelo ity: ||| Kalsoom Lakhani at CHUP-Changing Up Pakistan mourned the tragic incident:
Ity tranga androany dia mazava ho azy fa naseho tamin'ireo sary sy ireo horonantsarin'ireo fianakaviana sy naman'ireo izay namoy ny ainy, izay nihazakazaka nankany amin'ny hopitaly sy tany amin'ireo fakana tapakila any amin'ny seranam-piaramanidin'Islamabad tamin'io maraina io nitady vaovao mikasika ireo havany tamin'alahelo. ||| The tragedy of today of course is expressed in the images and videos of the victims' families and friends, who swarmed the hospital and ticket counters at Islamabad's airport this morning desperately seeking information about their loved ones.
Nilaza ny primatiora tantanin'i Yousaf Raza fa nanapa-kevitra ny minisitera federaly hametraka ho "andro fisaonana manerana ny nosy" ho an'ireo maty tao anatin'ilay Airblue sidina ED202 ny andro androany. ||| The office of PM Yousaf Raza Gilani said in a statement that the federal cabinet has declared today a "national day of mourning" for the victims of Airblue flight ED202.
Atokanay ho an'ireo fianakaviana sy ireo namoy ny ainy androany ny eritreritray sy ny vavakay. ||| Our thoughts and prayers go out to the families and friends of those who lost their lives today.
Koa satria mbola mitohy ny fanadihadihana dia mbola aloha loatra ny maminaviana ny antony mety nahatonga ny fianjerana. ||| As the investigation continues it is too early to suggest the possible cause of the crash.
Ireo tatitra faramparany dia nilaza fa hita ny boaty mainty, izay manamora ny fanadihadiana. ||| Recent reports have suggested that the black box has been recovered, which makes the investigation process easier.
Manadihady lalina amin'ireo fomba rehetra mety hanampona ireo fanadihadihana i Kalsoom Lakhani: ||| Kalsoom Lakhani further elaborates on the issues that might hinder investigations:
Inona marina ny "boaty mainty," hoy ianao? ||| What exactly is a "black box," you ask?
Araka ny voalazan'ny HowStuffWorks, mitodika any amin'ny rakitry ny sidina sy ny feo voaray ny fahadihadiana hamantarana izay nampianjera ity fiaramanidina ity. ||| According to HowStuffWorks, investigators generally turn to the airplane's flight data recorder (FDR) and cockpit voice recorder (CVR) for answers on how the plane crashed.
Eo amin'ny $10,000 ka hatramin'ny $15,000 eo ho eo ny vidiny (tsy fantatra na manana modely mitovy amin'izany ny orinasam-pitaterana an'habakabaka Pakistaney na tsia), ireo boaty mainty ireo no mirakitra amin'ny antsipiriany ireo zava-nitranga nialoha indrindra ity loza ity. ||| Costing between $10,000 and $15,000 (not sure if Pakistani airlines get similar models), these black boxes reveal details of the events immediately preceding the accident.
Araka ny voalazan'ny Dawn, Mpandraikitra ny mikasika ny Fiaramanidina Sivily (CAA) dia efa hita ity boaty mainty ity, noho izany dia holazaina amin'ny manaraka ny antsipiriany mikasika ny nampianjera ity fiaramanidina ity, (na dia tsy nanan'i Pakistan aza ny "manamora" ny fikirakirana ireo fitaovana ireo araka ny tatitry ny GEO). ||| According to Dawn, the Civil Aviation Authority (CAA) told reporters that this black box has been recovered, so details surrounding the crash will presumably be released soon, (though GEO reports that Pakistan actually lacks the "facility" to decipher these gadgets).
Ho fahatsiarovana ireo amoy ny ainy tamin'ity fianjerana ity. ||| Remembering the victims of the Crash.
Maryam Piracha nizara ny alahelony: ||| Maryam Piracha shares her grief:
Miady ny saiko eo amin'ny hevitra sy ny finoana, miady eo anoloan'ny fanamarinana sy ny fanekena. ||| I am torn between reason and belief, justifying and accepting, reasoning and understanding.
Tsy misy ny fomba tsotra hizorana an'izany, afa-tsy ny fivavahana ho an'ny fanahin'ireo maty sy ny fankaherezana ireo nilaozana. ||| There is no easy way to process this, except to pray for the souls of the dead and for the fortitude and patience of those they left behind.
Nahazoana fanakianana henjana ny fomba fitateran'ny media an'ity tranga mampahalahelo ity. ||| The media coverage of the tragic incident has been heavily criticized.
Ahsan Butt ao amin'ny Five rupees, namely ny tsy firaharahiana filazalazana momba ity fianjerana ity: ||| Ahsan Butt of Five rupees, lashed out at the irresponsible coverage of the crash:
Noho ireo zava-mahagaga ao amin'ny aterineto, afaka mijery ireo famoaham-baovao Pakistaney maro aho min'ny fotoana maro aho na dia mipetraka any Chicago aza, fa tsoriko fa nopihiko manodidina ny 90 segondra aloha taorian'ny namelomako azy ny maraina teo. ||| Thanks to the wonders of the Internet, I can watch most Pakistani news channels at most times even sitting in Chicago, but I must confess I turned it all off about 90 seconds after putting it on this morning.
"Tsy mampihetsi-po" ka naleo aza tsy notaterina akory. Fampahatsiarovana ho an'ny vondrona mampita vaovao: TOKONY IDIFIANA NY MANENJIKA NY HAVAN'IREO MATY NIARAKA AMINA FANDRAISAMPEO SY FAKANTSARY KA MAKA AMPAHANTENY HANAOVANA LAHATSORATRA. ||| "Insensitive" doesn't even begin to cover it. Memo to media organizations: RUNNING AFTER RELATIVES OF PEOPLE JUST KILLED WITH MICROPHONES AND CAMERAS AND BADGERING THEM FOR A QUOTE IS KIND OF A DOUCHEY THING TO DO.
Hotahian'Andriamanitra ianareo, ajanony izany fanao izany. ||| For the love of God, stop it.
Ataonao aorian'ny fanafihan'ireo mpampihorohoro sy ireo fanapoahana izany, ataonao aorian'ny loza voajanahary ary izao dia aorian'ny fianjerana fiaramanidina. ||| You do this after terrorist attacks and bombings and you do it after natural disasters and now you're doing it after a plane crash.
Fa ataonao inona izany e? ||| What's wrong with you?
Nandritra ny fitateran'ny media ny mikasika ity fianjerana ity dia hita fa maro ireo fantson'ny TV no mifantoka amin'ny fivarotana izany vaovao izany fa tsy mitatitra amim-pahamatorana. ||| During the media coverage of the crash it appeared that most TV channels were focusing more on marketing the news rather than reporting responsibly.
Ao amin'ny blaogiko, niresaka mikasika ny tsy fandraisan'ny media andraikitra sy ny fomba fitantarana tsy mampihetsi-po: ||| On my own blog, I talked about media's irresponsible and insensitive coverage:
Manorisory ny fianakavian'ireo namoy ny ainy mba hanoratana lahatsoratra momba azy ireo, manaraka ao aoriana sy mampanakaiky ny amin'ny fakantsary ny endriky ny olona misaona ny fahafatesan'ireo havany. ||| Reporters kept badgering families of the victims for quotes, following and zooming in on faces of people mourning the deaths of their loved ones.
Mbola loza noho izany ireo sary mipoitra avy eo amin'ny toeran'ilay fianjerana, manakaiky ireo pentin-drà sy ireo tapatapaky ny vatan'olona miparitaka miaraka amin'ireo fatim-by, raha nisy mpanao gazety iray tsy manafina ny hafaliany manofahofa ny antotan-taratasy sy ny kara-panondro hita tao an-toerana. ||| Even worse were the images being shown from the crash site, close ups of blood stains and scattered body parts along with debris, while a reporter gloatingly waved travel documents and identity cards from the site.
Tsy nieritreritra ny mety ho fiantraikan'ny fitaterana vaovao tsy tompon'andraikitra tahaka izao ireo fantson'ny media na indray mandeha aza, ny hahatonga ireo vaovao hahataitra sy hampaminavina ny fisian'ny theorie de la conspiration ihany no ao an-tsain'izy ireo. ||| None of these media channels for once thought of the implications of such irresponsible reporting, perhaps the only thing on their mind was to sensationalize the news and develop conspiracy theories.
Tsy niandry ora vitsy akory izy ireo mialoha ny hanapaingorana ny fisian'ny fahadisoana, ary tsy ampy elanelan'ora fohy monja dia lasa fanadihadihana mikasika ny fianjeran'ny fiaramanidina ny fitatera-baovao. ||| News anchors could not even wait for a few hours before pinning the blame, and within a span of a few hours news coverage of the event turned into aircrash investigations.
Mba haharatsiratsy kokoa ny toe-draharaha, nisy fantsona manokana iray lasa lavitra ary niteny fa hamboraka ny tahirim-peon'ny resaka nifandraisan'ny Mpanamory sy ny eny amin'ny tilikambo, alohan'ny hivoahan'ny fanambaranaofisialy mahakasika izany. ||| To make matters worse, one private channel went even further and claimed to disclose the Pilot-to-tower recording, even before any official statement was issued.
Tsy misy mihitsy hanamarinana ny fitateram-baovao tsy manana fitsipi-pitondran-tena amin'ny iray amin'ireo loza mampalahelo indrindra nitranga tany Pakistan. ||| There is absolutely no justifications for the unethical coverage of one of the most tragic incidents in Pakistan.
Mampifantoka ny sain'ny olona fotsiny amin'ny filana ny fanamafisana ny fitsipi-pitondrantena sy mahatonga fandrafetana lalàna misahana ny fandikan-dalàna ny fomba fitateram-baovao tsy manjary tahaka izao. ||| Miserable reporting only draws more attention to the need of reinforcing media ethics and to form regulatory bodies monitoring violations.
Mampifantoka amin'ny tokony hanatsarana ny rafitra fikarakarana sy famonjena voina ny fisian'ny loza tahaka izao, filazana vaovao tompon'andraikitra amin'ny tranga tahaka ireny ary ifotorana tsy azo idifiana ny fisian'ny manampahaizana manokana hanafaingana ny fanadihadihana. ||| The tragic incident has drawn attention to the need for a better disaster management and relief system, responsible reporting of such incidents and dire need of specialists and facilities that could help make the investigation process faster.
Koa satria miresaka ny tohin'ity loza ity izao, mamarana aho: ||| Talking about the aftermath of the tragedy I concluded:
Hatramin'ny nielezan'ny vaovao, mila mifehy tena aho tsy hanombatombana ny antony nahatonga iny fianjerana iny. ||| Since reports from the crash are still pouring in, I must refrain from speculating on the reasons of the crash.
Fa ny zavatra fantatro amin'izao aloha dia 152 ireo olona namoy ny ainy tamin'iny loza iny, amin'ny maha firenena misaona antsika dia mila miaraka amin'ireo namoy ny havany isika, mila mitandrina mba tsy hamadi-dresaka sy ny fanomezana vahana eritreri-dratsy. ||| But what I know now is that 152 people lost their lives in the tragic incident, as a nation in mourning we must stand in solidarity with those who have lost their loved ones, we must avoid speculation and top feeding on conspiracy theories.
Raha misy ny zavatra iray tokony hisongadina, tokony ny fanirian'ireo olon-tsotra izay nihazakazaka teny amin'iny toerana iny sy nalala-tanana hanampy sy hanohana ireo ekipa mpamonjy izany. ||| If there is one thing that should stand out, it should be the brave impulse of ordinary people who rushed to the scene and volunteered to help and support the rescue teams.
Ejipta: Tsy 'tongasoa' ve i Obama? ||| Egypt: Is Obama not Welcome?
Valo amby efapolo ora mialoha ny kabary andrasan'ny tontolo arabo sy silamo fatratra hataon'ny filoha amerikana Barack Obama avy ao amin'ny Anjerimanontolon'i Cairo, dia saiky miray feo daholo ny tontolon'ny fitorahana blaogy Ejiptiana. ||| Forty-eight hours before US president Barack Obama delivers his much awaited speech to the Arab and Muslim worlds from Cairo University, the Egyptian blogosphere is almost unified by the same feeling.
Tsy faly amin'ny endrika mibaribary sy tafahoatra atao ho fikarakaràna sy fiarovana raisin'ny governemanta ejiptiana ho an'ity fitsidihana ity ny mpitoraka blaogy, ary maro amin'izy ireo no misalasala hoe hitondra fiovana mivaingana kely marina ve ity kabary niomànana ity. ||| Bloggers are outraged by the massive and exaggerated preparations and precautions being taken by the Egyptian government to secure the visit, and most of them are doubting if the anticipated speech would usher any real change.
Ilay mpaka sary Waleed Nassar, izay miasa ao akaikin'ny Anjerimanontolon'i Cairo, dia nanoratra momba ireo fanomànana natao teo amin'ny faritra manodidina azy: ||| The photographer Waleed Nassar, who works near Cairo University, wrote about the preparations taking place in his neighbourhood:
Miasa eo akaikin'ny Anjerimanontolon'i Cairo aho ary tao anatin'ny alina iray monja dia niova tanteraka ity faritra ity. ||| I work next to Cairo University and this area has transformed over night.
Ny làlana nikitaontaona mankany amin'ny Anjerimanontolo izao dia lasa malama toy ny sily. ||| The bumpy streets leading to the University are now as smooth as silk.
Na ireo trano avo manodidina ny faritra aza dia notifirina soson-doko tokana daholo, saingy tsy ny trano avo rehetra an, izay mitodika any amin'ny làlana ihany. Tsara ery izany rehetra izany nefa mba hainao ve ny fandraisan'ny mponin'i Cairo an'ireny? ||| Even buildings around the area have been given a fresh layer of paint, but not the whole building, just the side that faces to the street.

Ny gazety mpiseho isan'andro Al-Shrouk nanipy toro-hevitra ny tokony hijanonana any an-trano, ny làlana manodidina rahateo efa hakatona ihany. ||| Al-Shrouk daily newspaper adviced Egyptians to stay home, as the streets will be nearly blocked.
Zeinobia dia nanoratra manodidina ny fandaharam-potoan'i Obama any Ejipta. ||| Zeinobia wrote about Obama's schedule in Egypt.
Nampiany ihany koa tato aoriana fa ny filoha Ejiptiana Hosni Mubarak dia tsy hanatrika ilay kabary: ||| She also added an update that the Egyptian president Hosni Mubarak will not attend the speech:
Mubarak tsy hihaona amin'i Obama ao amin'ny Koubbah Palace fotsiny, tsy hanatrika ny kabary ao amin'ny Anjerimanontolon'i Cairo izy araka ny nambaran'ny Al-Muslamany tao anaty fandaharan'ny fahitalavitra Dream TV 2!!!! - Heveriko fa ny tsy fahatongavany hanatrika ilay kabary dia hanangana fanontaniana maro momba ny toe-pahasalamany taorian'ny nahafatesan'ny zafikeliny (lahy) ||| Mubarak will meet Obama at Koubbah Palace only, he won't attend the speech in Cairo University according to Al-Muslamany's TV show on Dream TV 2!!!!
Egyptian Leftist nanoratra taratasy iray ho an'i Obama (teny mahery) arahana sary manambara izay tian-kolazaina manao hoe: "Tsy mino anao izahay!" ||| Egyptian Leftist wrote a letter to Obama (strong language) with an expressive picture saying: "We don't believe you" !

Nazavainy fa ny ho hitany dia tsy ny fikarakarana ny fitsidihany ihany, fa raha hanandrana hitsidika Anjerimanontolo iray hafa izy dia hahita zavatra hafa dia hafa mihitsy; hatramin'ny làlana izay tsy tsara, milamina sy madio toy izay hotsidihany. ||| He explained that what he will see is only preparations for his visit, but if he tried to visit the other universities he'll find something different; even streets which will not be as beautiful, organized and tidy as what he will see.

Fantatrao ve ny Anjerimanontolon'i Cairo hotsidihanao? ||| You know Cairo University you'll be visiting?
Eny ary!... Anjerimanontoloko io... Tao aho no nahazo ny diplaomako taona maro lasa izay... Reko koa fa dolara an-tapitrisany maro no nolaniana hanarenana ny toerana ho an'ny ora roa monja hijeren'ny masonao azy... I got my degree from there years back... I also heard that millions of dollars were spent to fix up the place just for you to lay eyes on it for couple of hours...
Amin'ny lafiny iray hafa, Dalia Ziada, mafana fo iray mpiaro ny zon'olombelona izay nametraka ny fanantenany ihany amin'ny fitsidihan'i Obama, dia namarana ny hafany "Young Egyptian Activists and the Obama effect!" amin'ny filazana hoe: ||| On the other hand, Dalia Ziada, a human rights activist who has retained some of her hope towards Obama's visit, concluded her " Young Egyptian Activists and the Obama effect!" post saying:
Voalohany izao ny Ejyptiana, tanatin'ny ampolotaonany, no mba afaka hahita maso filoha Amerikana iray maniry hametraka fifandraisana amin'ny fitondrana Ejiptiana, na teo aza ny hamaintin'ny zava-bitany tamin'ny fanaovan-javatra mifanohitra amin'ny demokrasia sy ny zon'olombelona. ||| For the first time, in tens of years, Egyptians can see an American president who is not eager to establish a relationship with the Egyptian regime regardless of its black record of practices against democracy and human rights.
Manery ny fitondrana Ejiptiana izany mba haneho fandeferana sy fahalefahana manoloana ireo olona sy vondrona mafana fo mpiaro ny zon'olombelona. ||| This forced the Egyptian regime to show more tolerance and flexibility towards human rights activists and groups.
Na izany aza, tsy azo ihodivirana ny fanontaniana, eo ampiandrasana fatratra ny fitsidihana hataon'i Obama ao Cairo afaka andro vitsy, mety hanao hoe: Hiseho hahavaly ny zavatra mampangetaheta fatratra ny tanora mafana fo Ejiptiana ve i Obama ka hanohana azy ireo amin'ny adin'izy ireo ho fametrahana fanavaozana anatiny sy hanatanteraka ny nofinofin'izy ireo hahita fiovana, izay nofinofiny rahateo, marina? ||| Yet, the inevitable question, while waiting impatiently for Obama's visit to Cairo within few days, would be: is Obama willing to live up to the high expectations of young Egyptian activists through supporting them in their struggle for domestic reform and making their dream of change, inspired by him, true?
Anatina fanamarihana iray hafa, ny hetsika Ejiptiana Kifaya dia miantso fitokonana (sit-in) iray andro alohan'ny fitsidihana, ho fanoherana ny fanohanan'ny governemanta Amerikana an'i Israely sy ny fitondrana Ejiptiana: ||| On a different note, Egyptian movement Kifaya called for a sit-in on the eve of the visit, opposing any intended support by the American government to Israel and the Egyptian regime:

Ho setrin'ny antso hanao fitokonana, Ahmed el Gizawy tahaka an'i Dalia, izay mino koa fa i Obama dia ho avy eto Ejipta miaraka aminà fikasana tsara momba ny tontolo Silamo sy Arabo, dia nangataka ny vahoaka mba hihaino ny kabariny aloha vao hanapa-kevitra hanao fitokonana (sit-in) na tsia. ||| In a reply to the sit-in call, Ahmed el Gizawy who like Dalia, also believes Obama is coming to Egypt with good intentions towards the Islamic and Arab world, asked the people to listen first to the speech then decide whether they want to proceed with a sit-in or not.

Tany: Diabe Manerantany Manohitra ny Mpanao Didy Jadona Syriana ||| World: Global March Against the Syrian Dictator
Tamin'ny Marsa 2011, raha nidina an-dalambe ny Syriana mitady fahafahana sy rariny, dia sarotra ny hieritreritra fa herintaona taty aoriana dia namono olona an'arivony sy nisambotra ka nampijaly olona tsy voaisa intsony ny fitondrana tao. ||| In March 2011, when Syrians started taking to the streets to demand freedom and justice, it was hard to imagine that a year later the regime would have killed thousands of people and tortured and arrested countless others.
Tratry ny fahirano ny mponina ao Homs hatramin'ny fiandohan'ny volana Febroary ary tsy mbola nisy toy izany ny famoretana ny mponina iray manontolo ao aminy, izay ahitana taham-pahafatesana 100 isan'andro. ||| The city of Homs has been besieged since the beginning of February and suffers an unprecedented crackdown against its entire population, with a death toll of 100 every day.
Raha mbola tsy nifanara-kevitra amin'ny filàna fanerena ny fitondran'i Assad ny iraisampirenena, mihamiroborobo kosa ny fiaraha-mientan'olotsotra manerantany amin'ny Syriana ary mbola hahazo olona hatrany satria mahatratra ny tsingerintaona ny revolisiona Syriana. ||| While international powers have not agreed on the need to pressure the Assad regime, global citizens solidarity with Syrians has been increasing and it will likely garner more support now that we are reaching the anniversary of the Syrian revolution.
Misy ny fandraisana an-tanana miantso Diabe Manerantany ho an'i Syria mikendry ny hahazo olona avy amin'ny lafivalon'ny tany hidina an-dalambe amin'ny 15,16 ary 17 Marsa ho fanohanana ny tolon'ny vahoaka Syriana. ||| An initiative called Global March for Syria aims to take people from all over the world to the streets on March 15, 16 and 17 in support of the Syrian people's struggle.
Ny fanentanana dia azavaina amina lahatsary antsoina hoe "Fanoherana ny mpanao didy jadona iray" izay ifampizarana tokoa an-tserasera. ||| The campaign is explained in a video called "Against a Dictator" that has been widely shared online:
Efa voakasa amina tanàna 16 ny diabe ho an'i Syria ary mihalava isan'andro ny lisitra. ||| Marches for Syria are already planned in 16 cities, and the list keeps growing every day.
Nanangana hetsika Facebook ahitana fampahafantarana isan-karazany momba ny filaharana tsirairay, sy ahitana ny fandrisihana ny olom-pirenena manerantany hijoro hanohitra ny famoretana ao Syria: ||| Activists have created a Facebook event with information on the different marches, where they encourage citizens worldwide to stand with Syria against oppression:
Herintaona no nanombohan'ny revolisiona Syriana. ||| One year since the Syrian revolution began.
Herintaonan'ny herisetra atao amin'ny mpanao fihetsiketsehana milamina sy ny sivily tsy manantsiny. ||| One year of violence against peaceful protesters and innocent civilians.
Herintaonan'ny ra mandriaka. ||| One year of bloodshed.
Ary herintaonan'ny herimpo anoherana ny ratsy lehibe, saingy efa nivoady ny tsy hitsahatra ny vahoaka Syriana mandra-pirodan'ny fitondrana, mandra-pahazoana ny fahafahana sy ny fahamendrehana. ||| And one year of a brave stance against great evil, but the Syrian people have vowed to never stop until the fall of the regime, until they gain freedom and dignity.
Andao isika hijoro hiaraka amin'i Syria hanohitra ny famoretana amin'ny 15-17 marsa 2012 ary andao hanokana fotoana hahatsiarovana ireo lasa sorona hatramin'ny 15 Marsa 2011. ||| On March 15-17, 2012 let's stand with Syria against oppression and take a moment to remember the thousands of lives sacrificed since March 15, 2011.

Vazo miteny - Lahatsarin-kira vaovao avy any Tibet ||| Music With A Message - New Music Videos from Tibet
Mitodika any amin'ny "vazo miteny" indray ny bolongana manana tetikasa fandikan-teny High Peaks Pure Earth amin'ny fandikana ny tononkira Tibetana hita amin'ny lahatsarin-kira Tibetana misy mamoaka amin'ny aterineto. ||| The blog translation project High Peaks Pure Earth has recently focused on "music with a message" by translating the lyrics of Tibetan songs from music videos that have been uploaded onto the internet.
Tamin'ny faha-10 ny volana marsa tamin'ity taona ity dia nampiseho lahatsary hip hop mitondra ny lohateny hoe "Taranaka vaovao" (New Generation) avy amin'ny tarika malaza any an-toerana antsoina "Yudrug" amin'ny Tibetana ("Dragona Maitso" amin'ny teny Malagasy) ny bolongana. ||| On March 10 this year, the blog presented a hip hop video titled "New Generation" by the popular group known as "Yudrug" in Tibetan ("Green Dragon" in English).
Yudrug no namoaka voalohany ny lahatsary ao amin'ny bolongany ny volana mialoha. ||| Yudrug had first released the video on their blog the previous month.
Araka ny voalazan'ny High Peaks Pure Earth: ||| According to High Peaks Pure Earth:
Nampiady hevitra ny tontolon-tserasera Tibetana ity gadona vaovao heno ao amin'ny "Taranaka Vaovao" ity satria misy ireo mpamaham-bolongana midera ny Yudrug noho ny tononkirany sahisahy fa ny sasany kosa mitsikera fa lasa "tandrefana loatra" ny tarika Yudrug. ||| This bold new style of musical expression heard in "New Generation" has been quite controversial in Tibetan cyberspace, with Tibetan bloggers praising Yudrug for their outspoken lyrics, but some also criticising Yudrug for adopting a style that is seen as "too western".
Na ahoana na ahoana ny fironana an-kira anananao dia tsy azo lavina kosa kosa ny lanja sy ny tanjany miaraka amin'ireo mpiredona: ||| Whatever your musical taste may be, the song is undeniably powerful and energetic with a rousing chorus:

Korea Atsimo: Nabaribarin'i Hyo-ri mpanjakan'ny K-pop ny olana momba ny fakan-tàhaka ||| South Korea: K-Pop Icon Hyo-ri Brings the Plagiarism Issue Up To the Light
Ny rakikira faha-efatra navoakan'ilay mpanjakavavin'ny pop Koreana Tatsimo Lee Hyo-ri dia namelona adihevitra tamin'ny aterineto momba ny fakàn-tahaka ao amin'ny firenena noho ny famborahan'i Hyo-ri fa ny hira enina amin'ny rakikirany faha-efatra 'H-logic' dia dika tsy ara-dalàna avokoa. ||| South Korean pop queen Lee Hyo-ri's fourth album reignited discussion on the country's plagiarism over the internet as Hyo-ri came to admit that six songs from her fourth album 'H-logic' are the illegally copied.
Miady hevitra momba izay tena zava-nitranga ireo mpitoraka blaogy, momba ny hoe iza no hokianina ary nahoana ny fakan-tàhaka no manakorontana ny indostriam-pirenena momba nyhira. ||| Bloggers are debating over what really happened, who is to blame and why plagiarism is plaguing the nation's music industry.
Lee Hyo-ri dia fanta-daza amin'ny pop Koreana Tatsimo sy matihanina efa nahavita fampisehoana tanatin'ny 13 taona, izay mandray karama efa ho 10 arivo tapitrisa Won Koreana (8.1 tapitrisa dollars) isan-taona, araka ny tatitr'ireo fampahalalàm-baovao ao an-toerana. ||| Lee Hyo-ri is South Korea's pop icon and show business' 13 year veteran, who is earning almost 10 billion Korean Won(USD 8.1 million) a year, according to local news report.
Manana mpankafy maro maneran-tany izy noho ny fisehoany matetika amina fampisehoana sy ireo hira sy dokambarotra maro mifangaro. ||| She has a wide scope of fans from her active appearances at numerous hit variety shows and commercials.
Vao nivoaka ny rakikiran'i Hyori fahaefatra dia nalaza avy hatrany, nefa koa avy hatrany dia niteraka ahiahy fa toa mitovy loatra ireo hirany sasany ka mety tsy tena azy. ||| Hyori's fourth album 'H-Logic' made a instant hit after release, but at the same time immediately draw suspicions that some of her songs are too similar to be her original tunes.
Nandà izany ny orinasa mpiantoka an'i Hyori raha tsy izy mihitsy no nanazava tamin'ny volana Jona fa ireo hira enina izay azony tany amin'ilay tarika mpamoron-kira Bahnus Vacuum dia nalaina tahaka tamina hira vahiny. ||| Hyori's agency has denied the allegation till Hyori came clear on June that six songs she got from a songwriter group Bahnus Vacuum are plagiarized from foreign songs.
Tao amina fanambaràna ofisialy dia namoaka lahatsoratra i Hyori tao amin'ny sehatra fifandraisany amin'ireo mpankafy, naiky izy fa tena dika tsy ara-dalàna tokoa ireo hira niteraka disadisa ary miala tsiny amin'ireo izay nahatsapa ho tohina tamin'izany fihetsiny izany izy sady hiato kely amin'ny sehatry ny mozika aloha izy. ||| In an official statement Hyori posted on her fan cafe, she admitted the disputes songs were indeed illegal copies and she apologize for anyone who had been hurt from her acts and she will be taking a hiatus from music activity for the moment.
Bahnus izay nanome azy ireo hira kosa dia tsy mbola nanao fanambaràna ampahibemaso taorian'ireo fiakena ireo. ||| Bahnus who gave her the songs have not made any public appearance after the revelation.
Na dia olana resahina matetika aza ny fakan-tàhaka any Korea, tsy fahita firy izany mpihira miaiky tanteraka izany. ||| Even though the plagiarism itself is frequently brought up issue in Korea, a full-out confession by the singer is rare.
Ny ankamaroan'ireo mpitoraka blaogy dia nidera ny fiaiken'i Hyori ho fihetsika feno herim-po. ||| Majority of the internet bloggers praised Hyori's confession as a courageous act.
Nilaza ny Nilaza ilay mpitoraka blaogy Eunkoung fa toe-tsaina mahamenatra ny fakan-tàhaka ary fahafaham-baràka ny fihetsik'ireo mpihira hafa amin'izany, fa i Hyori kosa dia ohatra tsara ho azy ireo. ||| A blogger Eunkoung commented that the plagiarism is a shameful deed and other singer's reaction to it is a disgrace, while Hyori has shown a good precedent.
Tokony ekena ny herim-po nasehon 'i Hyori tamin'ny fiaikena ny fahadisoany sy ny fanazavany ny zava-drehetra.Na izany aza anefa dia tsy toe-javatra tokony deraina mihitsy izao zava-miseho izao. ||| The courage Hyori has shown by admitting her fault and coming clear on everything needs to be acknowledged. However, this case itself is not something to be applauded.
Tena mifanohitra tanteraka amin'izay fihetsik'ireo mpihira hafa izay tsy miaiky mihitsy ny zava-bitany ary tonga dia manjavona tampoka raha vao mivoaka ny marina. ||| This is quite contrary to other musicians' reaction who never admit their deeds and suddenly disappear when allegation broke out.
Zava-debibe ny nanaovan'i Hyori fifonana ampahibemaso. ||| It is great of Hyori to make an official apology.
Hafahafa loatra ny fitovian'ireo hirany nahabe resaka amin'ireo hira tena izy ka ampy niteraka ahiahy. ||| The resemblance of her disputed songs with the original tunes was quite uncanny enough to raise suspicions.
Raha tianao hamarinina ireo hira dia tsindrio eto. ||| To check the music yourself click here.
Ireo hiran'i Hyori niteraka disadisa dia arahin'ireo hira tena izy mitovy aminy. ||| Hyori's disputed songs are followed by each of their original counterparts.
Ireo tsikera dia manameloka an'i Hyori sy ny orinasa mpiantoka azy, Mnet, iray amin'ireo fahitalavitra lehibe indrindra misahana ny mozika any amin'ny firenena, noho ny tsy firaharahiana ny ahiahy naterak'ity fitoviana tsy azo iadian-kevitra ity. ||| Critics are blaming Hyori and her agency, Mnet, nation's one of biggest music cable television for ignoring the suspicion rose from this indisputable resemblance.

Fony vao nivoaka ilay rakikira fahaefatra, maro ireo olona niahiahy fa fakàn-tàhaka ireo hira, nefa ny avy amin'i Hyori sy Mnet kosa dia tsy nanadihady lalina momba izany fa nipetra-potsiny. ||| When the fourth album was released, many people raised suspicions that the song are plagiarized tunes, but Hyori side and Mnet have not made a thorough investigation on that, instead they just sat back idly.

Tena tsy mpandray andraikitra mihitsy ry zareo. ||| They are really irresponsible.
Miha-betsaka hatrany ny fiahiahiana ny fakàn-tahaka ankehitriny. ||| The plagiarism allegation is more frequently erupting nowadays.
Maro ny olona no mahita fa manome fomba maro ahafahan'ny olona mihaino ny hiran'ireo mpihira vahiny ny aterineto, ka miha-sarotra ho an'ireo mpamoron-kira ny hanao ny mpihaino ho toy ny adala. ||| Many people see this as the internet endowing people opportunities to listen to foreign musicians' tunes, making it much harder for songwriters to fool the audience.

Fa afaka kosa ireo tompon'ny zon'ny mpanomorona manenjika izay manao izany any amin'ny Komisiona Koreana ho an'ny zon'ny mpanmorona na any amin'ny fitsaràna, saika ny disadisa momba ny fakàn-tàhaka rehetra dia milamina amin'ny fifampiraharahana tsy mazàva avokoa. ||| Though copyright holders can sue the convicted in the Korea Copyright Commission or in court, nearly every plagiarism disputes are customarily settled through informal negotiations.
