Ny zava-niseho nateraky ny fakàna sary miafina tao an-tsekoly tany Krasnoyarsk, Siberia dia nanasongadina olana manan-danja any amin'ireo sekoly Rosiana: ireo mpampianatra manohana ny antoko eo amin'ny fitondrana, ny United Russia. ||| A scandal caused by a hidden camera recording at a school in Krasnoyarsk, Siberia has highlighted a serious problem in Russian schools: teachers campaigning for the ruling party, United Russia.
Sady tsy ampy karama no miankina amin'ny fanohanana ara-bola avy amin'ny fitondrana, ny mpampianatra dia anisan'ireo andrin'ny rafitra politika ankehitriny. ||| Underpaid and dependent on government funding, teachers are one of the pillars of the current political system.
Ny fifidianana dia matetika atao any amin'ny trano fianarana, ary ny komitim-pifidianana dia mpampianatra no tena mameno azy. ||| Local and regional elections often take place in school buildings, and the electoral committees in Russia often consist mainly of teachers.
Na avy amin'ny tahotra ny ho fahaverezan'ny famatsiam-bola, na avy amin'ny finoana ny toky napetraky ny United Russia, dia miteraka fifidianana tsy ara-dalàna ao an-tsekoly izany matetika. ||| Whether it's from fear of losing funding, or belief in United Russia's promises, this often leads to illegal electioneering in schools.
Mpianatra iray sahy nanohitra ny fahefana. ||| One brave student takes on the authorities
Ny 15 Novambra 2011 lasa teo, Matvey Tsivinyuk, tovolahy 15 taona, dia namoaka horonantsary tamin'ny Krasnoyarsk Gymnazium number 3 (tsy misokatra intsony io tranokala io taorian'ny fanehoan-kevitra marobe avy amin'ireo bilaogera), nampiseho ny tenany notezeran'ny talen-tsekoly, Alexandra Pronina. ||| On 15 November, 2011, 15-year-old Matvey Tsivinyuk, uploaded a video of himself being scolded by his school principal, Alexandra Pronina, at Krasnoyarsk Gymnazium number 3 (the website went offline after massive interest from bloggers).
Peta-drindrin'ny United Russia tao amin'ny sekoly Krasnoyarsk. ||| United Russia posters in Krasnoyarsk school.
Tsivinyuk dia tratra nanimba peta-drindrina mikasika politika izay nihantona tao an-dalatsaran'ny sekoly. ||| Tsivinyuk had been caught defacing political posters that were hanging in the school hallways.
Ireo peta-drindrina dia nitondra ny loko telon'ny saina rosiana ho lafika ary nisy ny sarin'ny praiministra Vladimir Putin, ny filoha Dmitry Medvedev ary mpanao politika roa hafa avy ao an-toerana (jereo ny sary eo ankavanana). ||| The posters with a Russian tricolor flag in the background bore portraits of Prime Minister Vladimir Putin, President Dmitry Medvedev and two local politicians (see photo right).
Talohan'ny nihaonany tamin'ny tale dia nalefan'i Tsivinyuk ny fandraisana sary tao amin'ny findainy. ||| Before meeting the principal, Tsivinyuk turned on the video recorder in his smartphone.
Ny resaka azo tao dia maneho porofo mazava ny hetsika tsy manara-dalàna ataon'ny manam-pahefana ao an-tsekoly, no sady koa manazava ny fomba fanohanana ny antoko eo amin'ny fitondrana amin'izao fotoana. ||| The dialogue captured by the device has been widely cited as evidence of unlawful actions from school authorities, and also lends a narrative to explain the support for the current political regime.
Tao aoriana kely iny andro iny ihany dia nofafan'i Tsivinyuk tao amin'ny pejiny ilay horonantsary, saingy tsy navelan'ireo bilaogera hanjavona kosa ilay horonantsary: ||| Later that day, Tsivinyuk removed the video from his own profile but bloggers have not let the video disappear:
Ity no fandikàna ny resaka: ||| Here is a translation of what is said:
Tale: Moa va fantatrao no dikan'izao ho anao? ||| Principal: Do you know what this means for you?
Tsivinyuk: Tsy midika na inona na inona amiko izao, satria raha araky ny teboka fahadimin'ny andininy fahasivy eo amin'ny lalàn'ny antoko politika dia.. (Matvey dia nanambara ny lalàna marina izay mandràra ny fijabahan'ny politika eo amin'ny tontolon'ny fampianarana) ||| Tsivinyuk: It means nothing to me because, according to the point 5 of the article 9 of the Law on Political parties... (Matvey correctly cites the law that forbids interference of the political process in education)
Tale: Aoka izay, aoka izay. ||| Principal: Enough, enough, Matvey.
Tsy misy andininy fahasivy sy fahafolo izany, hanao tatitra an-tsoratra fotsiny ry zareo (ny polisy) fa hoe nosimbainao ilay peta-drindrina. ||| There's no article number 9, number 10, they (the police) will write that you damaged the poster.
Manam-bola be ve ny ray aman-dreninao handoa sazy ho fanamboarana ny simba? ||| Does your family have lots of money to pay for the fine for the damage?
Tsivinyuk: Sazy ho fanamboarana ilay taratasy ve? ||| Tsivinyuk: A fine for the piece of paper?
Tale (mihiaka): Ho an'ny asam-boto! ||| Principal (screaming): For the hooliganism!
Fantatrao fa tsy taratasy fotsiny io, peta-drindrina politika io! ||| You understand it's not just a paper, it's a political poster!
Tsivinyuk: Tsy afaka atao aty am-pianarana io. ||| Tsivinyuk: It can't be in school.
Satria ny hetsika ataon'ny antoko politika dia voarara aty an-tsekoly. ||| Because the activity of political parties on the territory of schools is forbidden.
Tale: Azonao? Tsy fampielezn-kevitra io. ||| Principal: You understand, it's not campaigning.
Tsivinyuk: Fa inona io izany? ||| Tsivinyuk: So what is it then?
Tale: Tsy fampielezan-kevitra io. ||| Principal: It is not campaigning.
Apetaka eo amin'izay afaka vakian'ny olona ny tantaram-piainana (an'i Medvedev, Putin sy ireo mpanao politika hafa). ||| People put it there so that everyone could read the biographies (of Medvedev, Putin, and local politicians).
Manomboka izao dia raràko tsy hikitika an'ireo peta-drindrina ireo intsony ianao. ||| From now on I forbid you to do anything to these posters.
Efa betsaka izay no nosimbànao. ||| You've spoiled several posters.
Raha mbola manimba eo ianao dia antsoiko ny polisy. ||| If you will spoil more, I will call the police.
Tsivinyuk: Dia inona no ho ataony amiko? ||| Tsivinyuk: And what will they do to me?
Tale: Tsy fantatro. ||| Principal: I don't know.
Fa efa nampitandrina aho zay. ||| But I have warned you.
Avy eo dia nampitovy an'i Tsivinyuk tamin'i Lenin ilay tale, ary nampahatsiahy azy ny nahavoaroaka an'i Lenin tamin'ny sekoliny sy ny anjerimanontolo. ||| Then the principal compared Tsivinyuk to Lenin, and reminded him of Lenin's expulsion from his school and the university.
Avy eo koa dia naneso azy tamin'ny finoana arahan'i Tsivinyuk (kristiana ortodoksa ity farany) koa ilay tale ka nanampy hoe: ||| After a digression about Tsivinyuk's religious beliefs (he's an Orthodox Christian) the Principal exclaimed:
Tale: Ahoana no ahafahan'olona kristiana manatanteraka hetsika tsy kristiana tahaka izao? ||| Principal: How can a Christian person perform such non-Christian actions?
(mikasika ilay fanimbàna peta-drindrina) ||| (speaking of defacing a political poster)
Tsivinyuk: Ny fijery ara-politika sy ny fijery ara-pinoana dia tontolo roa samy hafa eo amin'ny fiainana. ||| Tsivinyuk: Political views and religious views are different spheres of life.
Tale (mihiaka): Raha tsy azonao izany teneniko izany dia ndao hihaona amin'ny mpitondra anareo (mpitondra ny vondrona kristiana ortodoksa misy an'i Tsivinyuk) ||| Principal (screaming): If you don't understand this, let's meet with your leader (of the Orthodox Christian group Tsivinyuk belongs to)
Tsivinuyk: Tsy misy idirany ity resaka ity. ||| Tsivinuyk: He has nothing to do with this.
Tale (mihiaka): Ahoana izany? ||| Principal (screaming): How is that?
Mino aho fa tsy misy mampianatra anao an'izany aty an-tsekoly aty, tsy misy mampianatra anao hanao zavatra tsy mety toy izao, manoratra zavatra ratsy amin'ny peta-drindrina. ||| For example, I think that no one is teaching you this in school. No one teaches you in school how to do such nasty things, to write bad things on posters.
Taiza ary iza no nampianatra anao an"izany ary? ||| Where and who teaches you then?
Taiza izany no niditra tao an-tsainao? ||| Where did you get this into your head?
Tokony hotadiavintsika ny toerana nianaranao an'izany. ||| We should find the place where you were taught this.
Averiko ihany, farafahakeliny tokony mandoa sazy ianao. ||| Once again, the minimum is a fine.
Tsivinyuk: Ho an'ny inona? ||| Tsivinyuk: For what?
Tale: Mbola tsy azonao ihany ve? ||| Principal: You still don't understand?
Tsivinyuk: Raha izany dia teneno ahy hoe andininy fahafiry tao amin'ny lalàn'ny sekoly no nodikaiko. ||| Tsivinyuk: Well, tell me the article number of the administrative code I have violated.
Ilay tale moa dia tsy nanazava tamin'i Tsivinyuk ny antony mazava mety hampisy fanenjehana avy amin'ny manampahefana na ny polisy noho ny fanimbàna peta-drindrina tsy ara-dalàna ||| The principal did not explain to Tsivinyuk why the defacement of illegally hung political posters would be cause for administrative or police charges.
Mety tsy ho niparitaka be teny imasom-bahoaka ity raharaha ity raha tsy nisy ny bilaogera tao Moskoa sy ilay mpanao gazety Vladimir Varfolomeev izay namoaka ny tantara tamin'ny blaoginy (izay nahateraka fanehoan-kevitramihoatra ny 2000). ||| The case may have never reached the public had it not been for Moscow blogger and journalist Vladimir Varfolomeev who published the story in his blog (the post attracted more than 2,000 comments).
Naverin'ny tranonkala Siberiana sy ny tao an-toerana navoaka haingana indray ny tantara avy eo. ||| Siberian and federal websites quickly re-published the story.
Ny governora lefitry any Krasnoyarsk, Sergey Ponomarenko, dia nilaza fa "tsy mendrika" ny fihetsik'i Tsivinyuk, ary nahasarika fanehoan-kevitra maro avy amin'ireo bilaogera izany ka ireo dia namely fa ny United Russia sy i Ponomarenko mihitsy no "tsy mendrika". ||| Vice-Governor of Krasnoyarsk, Sergey Ponomarenko, said that Tsivinyuk's actions were "mean" and this attracted critical comments from bloggers who said United Russia and Ponomarenko himself were the "mean" ones.
Ny harivan'io andro io dia nofafàn'i Tsivinyuk ilay horonantsary (tsy nisy vaovao ny mety ho famoretana nihatra taminy). ||| By the end of the day, Tsivinyuk removed his video (there is no information regarding what pressure was put on him).
Tamin'ny pejiny Vkontakte (tambajotra socialy mitovy amin'ny Facebook) dia izao no nambarany: ||| On his Vkontakte page (Russian equivalent to Facebook) he wrote:
Tsy nanaiky resy aho, saingy tsy hiditra amin'ny politika intsony. ||| I haven't given up, but I'm not into politics anymore.
Mino aho fa azonareo ny tiako Iazaina, tsy miditra amin'izany, mibanjina ny ho avy, ny namana no karakaraina. ||| I hope you get me right, don't get into this crap, think of the future, take care of your friends.
Maro ny tranga mitovy amin'ity iray ity no efa niseho amin'izao fiandrasana ny fifidianana Rosiana amin'ny Marsa 2012 izao. ||| There have been many incidents of this nature leading up to the Russian election in March 2012.
Ny Kartanarusheniy.ru, tranonkala dia mitatitra avy eny ifotony ny halatra amin'ny fifidianana, milaza tranga 737 mikasika manam-pahefana miangatra (amin'ireo mpilatsaka hofidiana sasany). ||| Kartanarusheniy.ru, a website that crowd-sources reports of electoral fraud, currently lists 737 cases of "Authorities creating preferential conditions (for candidates)".
Ary ny taona lasa teo, horonantsary iray tao amin'ny YouTube no nampiseho mpampianatra manolotra fanomezana an'ireo mpianatra nahazo mari-pahaizana sady miresaka momba ny fahatsaran'ny United Russia. ||| And last year, a video on YouTube showed teachers in one school giving first-graders gifts while talking about how great United Russia is.
Ny resaka nataon'ilay talen-tsekoly sorena mafy sy ilay mpianatra tony mahay lalàna dia maneho elanelana be misy eo amin'ny sokajin-taona, sy fanantenana fa ny haizina sy ny tsy fahalalàna (raha raisina hoe avy amin'ny sekoly no ahazoana ny fahalalàna rehetra) dia azo abaribary sy resena. ||| The dialogue between the hysterical principal versus the calm, tech-savvy Tsivinyuk who knows the law, represents a huge generational gap, and a hope that the obscurity and ignorance (for instance assuming that all knowledge comes from school) can be exposed and defeated.
Fanampim-baovao: Vladimir Varfolomeev dia nilaza fa voaantso tany amin'ny polisy ny renin'i Tsivinyuk. ||| Update: Vladimir Varfolomeev reports that Tsivinyuk's mother was called to the police.
Kolombia: Mitohy Mitokona Ireo Anjerimanontolo Ho Fanoherana Ny Lalàna 30 ||| Colombia: Universities Continue Strike in Protest of Law 30
"Tsy ity akory no andian-taranaka hahita ny fahafatesan'ny Anjerimanontolom-panjakana". ||| "This is not the generation that will see the public university die".
Miaraka amin'ity fanambaràna navoaka taminà karazana media samihafa ity, miezaka manaitra ny sain'ny governemantam-pirenena ireo mpianatry ny anjerimanontolo Kolombiana amin'ny fangatahan-dry zareo ny mba hanafoanana ilay fanavaozana ny Lalàna 30 mifehy ny fampianarana ambony. ||| With this statement disseminated through various media, Colombian university students are trying to call the attention of the national government as they demand that the bill to reform higher education Law 30 be revoked.
Mihevitra ireo mpianatra fa ilay fanavaozana dia hitondra amin'ny fanomezana ireo anjerimanontolom-panjakana ho lasan'ny tsy miankina, ary nanindry izy ireo fa tsy hanomboka raharaha akademika mihitsy - izay efa naaton-dry zareo roa herinandro lasa izao - raha tsy sintonin'ny governemanta any amin'ny Kaongresy ilay volavolan-dalàna. ||| The students argue that the reform would privatize public universities, and have emphasized they will not start academic activities - which were stopped two weeks ago - until the government withdraws the bill from Congress.
Niziriziry tamin'ny toerana nisy azy ny governemanta tamin'ny alalan'ny Minisitry ny Fanabeazana, nilazàny fa hitondra tombontsoa ho an'ny vahoaka Kolombiana ilay fanavaozana. ||| The government has been persistent on its position through the Minister of Education, stating that the reform benefits the interests of the Colombian people.
Tsy ela akory izay dia nandefa fanentanana tanaty fahitalavitra izy io izay mikendry ny handresy lahatra ny Kolombiana hanaiky ny fanavaozana tahaka izany. ||| It recently launched a television campaign which seeks to persuade Colombians to accept such reform.
Niteraka valin-kafatra tamin'ny alalan'ny lahatsary avy amin'ilay Solombavambahoaka Angela Robledo ilay fanentanana, izay mbola mitohy mihodina any anaty aterineto any. ||| The campaign triggered a video response by Representative Angela Robledo which is still circulating on the Internet.
Ao anatin'ilay lahatsary i Robledo dia mandalina ilay fanentanana ka milaza fa ny Lalàna 30 dia tetikasa manohitra ny demaokrasia, tsy mahazo izay fankatoavana sahaza ho azy. ||| In the video Robledo analyzes the campaign and argues that Law 30 is an undemocratic project that lacks legitimacy.
Tsindriany koa ny tsy fahampian'ny fampiasam-bola amin'ny sehatra fanabeazana satria ny vola dia navily ho any amin'ny ady sy ny fitrandrahana harena an-kibon'ny tany. ||| She also emphasizes the lack of investment in education because the money is being diverted to war and mining.
Any amin'ny farany i Robledo dia mangataka ny Minisitra sy ny Governemanta mba hisintona ilay volavolan-dalàna ka hifampiresaka amin'ireo mpianatra mba hitady izay fanavaozana tsara kokoa ho an'ny fanabeazana. ||| At the end Robledo calls on the Minister and the government to withdraw the project and consult with students to reach the best higher education reform.
Na izany aza, tsy mbola misy miverina an-dakilasy ny mpianatra ary manohy ny fanentanana any amin'ny faritra samihafa ao Kolombia. ||| However, college students are still not attending classes and continue with mobilizations in various parts of Colombia.
Nahavita nikarakara fihaonana tamin'ny governemanta ireo mpianatra tamin'ny Alatsinainy 31 Oktobra mba hanaovana tombana ny vakiraokan'ilay fanavaozana ny Lalàna 30. ||| The students accomplished to set up a meeting with the government for Monday October 31 to evaluate the current draft of the amendment to Law 30.
Kanefa, mbola eo foana ireo hetsika anaty aterineto miaraka aminà kaonty Facebook vaovao sy famoahana amin'ny tambajotra sosialy hafa. ||| Nevertheless, Internet demonstrations are still present with new accounts on Facebook and other publications on social networks.
Ny bilaogy El Salmón dia namoaka lahatsoratra isan-karazany mikasika ilay lohahevitra. ||| The blog El Salmón has published various entries on the subject.
Ao anatin'ny "Oroka sy Fihina tao Amin'ny Anjerimanontolon'i Tolima" dia miteny ity bilaogera ity hoe: ||| In "Kisses and Hugs at Tolima University" this blogger says:
Ny ady ataon'ny mpianatra amin'ny kolikoly ao amin'ny UT (Anjerimanontolon'i Tolima) sy hanoherana ny Lalàna 30, tsy hoe fotsiny ahitàna ady amin'ny anjerimanontolo-fandraharahana, izay ampiasàna ny fanabeazana ho fikatsahana tombontsoa ara-bola ho an'ireo mpampiasa vola, fa koa ady hangatahana amin'ny fanjakana ny hampakàrany ny fampiasam-bolany amin'ny sehatry ny sosialy (fahasalamana, trano fonenana, kolontsaina, fanatanjahantena sy fanabeazana). ||| The student struggle against corruption at UT (Tolima University) and against Law 30, not only includes fighting against the business-university, one that makes use of education to gain economic profit for investors, but the struggle is also demanding that the State increase its budget for social investment (health, housing, culture, sport and education).
Ny Gazetiboky Hekatombe dia mamoaka ireo teny nambaran'ny Minisitry ny Fanabeazana mikasika ny fitokonan'ny mpianatra: ||| Magazine Hekatombe publishes the words of the Minister of Education regarding the student strike:
Nandritra ny efa ho herinandro roa nisian'ny fitokonan'ny mpianatra tany amin'ireo anjerimanontolom-panjakana ho fanoherana ny fanavaozana ny Lalàna 30, ny Minisitry ny Fanabeazana, Maria Fernanda Campo, dia niteny ny mety hanafoanana enim-bolana amin'ny fotoam-pianarana, saingy ankinina amin'ny fitantanan'ny toeram-pianarana tsirairay. ||| With nearly two weeks of the student strike in the country's public universities in protest against the reform of Law 30, Education Minister Maria Fernanda Campo said the possibility of canceling the semester depends on the administration of each institution
Fabián Figueroa dia mitatitra fa ny Anjerimanontolo ao Pamplona koa dia nanatevin-daharana ilay fitokonan'ny anjerimanontolo: ||| Fabián Figueroa reports that the University of Pamplona also joined the university strike:
Nanatevin-daharana ny fitokonana eto amin'ny firenena i ¡Unipamplona! ||| ¡Unipamplona joins the national strike!
Tsy misy fialan-tsasatra, fa ora fiasàna hiadiana ny hoavy. ||| This is not vacation, it is working hours to fight for the future
Raha i Daniel Camilo kosa maneho ny hadisoam-panantenany amin'ny tsy firaikan'ireo mpianatra avy amin'ny anjerimanontolo tsy miankina: ||| While Daniel Camilo shows his disappointment at the indifference of students from private universities:
...mahatezitra ahy ny mamaky ireo mpianatra avy amin'ny anjerimanontolo izay mihevitra fa satria ry zareo mianatra amin'ny anjerimanontolo tsy miankina dia tsy mahakasika azy ireo ny fanavaozana ny lalàna 30 ||| ...it angers me to read university students that think that because they are studying at private universities the reform of ley 30 doesn't affect them
Laura Barreto dia mizara ny fomba fijeriny amin'ny maha-mpianatra avy aminà anjerimanontolo tsy miankina azy: ||| Laura Barreto shares her perspective as a student from a private university:
Miaraka amin'ity Lalàna 30 manelohelo ity dia mahatsiaro ho voahilikilika aho noho ny fianarako any aminà anjerimanontolo tsy miankina. ||| With all this surrounding Law 30 I feel discriminated for studying at a private university
Omar Ferrer dia nibitsika ho valinteny ho an'i Laura Guarín: ||| Omar Ferrer tweeted in response to a Laura Guarín:
Raha tsy mihetsika manohitra aho, dia satria angamba tsy heveriko ho asan-devoly be ho an'ny hoavin'ny firenena ny lalàna 30. ||| If I don't protest, it is because maybe I do not think that law 30 it is as satanic for the future of the country.
Fa tsy noho ny hoe maha-mpanapitrisa ahy akory ||| Not because I'm a millionaire
Mpianatra ao Bogotá mandray anjara amin'ny hetsi-panoherana. ||| Students in Bogotá participating in a protest.
Tati Triana dia manindry ny lesoka ankapobeny eo amin'ny fanabeazana: ||| Tati Triana emphasizes the general lack of education:
Tsy misy ny anjerimanontolo tsy miankina. ||| Private universities don't exist.
Ny ananantsika dia olona tsy omen-jo hahazo fanabeazana! ||| What we have is people deprived of education!
Kristian López dia mamaly bitsika iray nalefan'ny Filohan'i Kolombia mba hitarainana noho ny zava-misy sy ilay fanavaozana: ||| Kristian López responds to a tweet by the President of Colombia to lament the situation and the reform:
Te-hianatra aho, te-hanarina indray andro any ny fahavoazana zakain'i KOLOMBIA noho ny nataonao sy ireo teo alohanao ||| I want to study, I want to one day repair the damage that you and your predecessors have caused COLOMBIA
Sebastián Jaimes, mitanisa ny fifidianam-paritra tamin'ny 30 Oktobra, dia manolotra hevitra toy ity manaraka ity: ||| Sebastián Jaimes, referring to the regional elections on October 30, proposes the following:
Manome soso-kevitra aho ny hanoratana anaty biletàm-pifidianana ny hoe TSY EKENA NY FANAVAOZANA NY LALANA 30, TE-HIANATRA AHO! ||| I propose to write in the Electoral ballot NO TO REFORM OF LAW 30, I WANT TO STUDY!
Farany, Oscar Cuervo Ariza, mpianatra amin'ny sampana Toekarena, dia manontany ny amin'ny maha-matotra ity resaka fanavaozana ity: ||| Finally, Oscar Cuervo Ariza, student of Economics, asks for seriousness in the discussion of reform:
Mila tolo-kevitra matotra aho, resaka matotra mba hifanakalozana momba ilay fanavaozana ny lalàna 30, leo an'itony kabary mitaraindraina sy miloko politika loatra itony ||| I want serious proposals, serious speeches to discuss the reform of law 30, enough with these melancholic and politicized speeches
Tonizia: 2011 An-tsary Amin'ny Valantserasera ||| Tunisia: 2011 in Citizen Media Photos
Taona mahatalanjona ny taona 2011 ho an'i Tonizia - taona manan-tantara izay hiraikitra ao an-tsain'ny Toniziana rehetra. ||| The year 2011 has been an extraordinary year for Tunisia - a historic year that will be engraved into the memory of every Tunisian.
Izay nanomboka tamin'ny fipoahana tampoka noho ny fahadisoam-panantenana tao amin'ny faritra Sidi Bouzid izay noadinoina sy natao an-kilabao no nivadika fikomiam-bahoaka ho fanadiovana ny firenena, sy hanonganana ny fitondran'i Zeine el Abidine Ben Ali naharitra nandritra ny 23 taona, ary nanova ny faritra iray manontolo rehefa naka tahaka ny hafanam-pon'ny revolisiona ny tany an-kafa. ||| What started as a spontaneous act of despair in the forgotten and marginalised region of Sidi Bouzid, turned into a popular uprising that would sweep the country, topple the 23-year rule of Zeine el Abidine Ben Ali, and change the face of the entire region as one Arab country after the other picked up the revolution fervour.
Rà mandrika no niseho tamin'ny fiandohan'ny taona ||| A bloody beginning of the year
Tovolahy Toniziana namoy ny ainy tao Tala (afovoany andrefana Tonizia), tamin'ny 10 Janoary 2011. ||| Dead young Tunisian man in Tala (central-west of Tunisia), January 10, 2011.
Rà mandrika sy herisetra no niseho raha vao niatomboka ny taona. ||| The year had a bloody and violent beginning.
Nofaizin'ny manam-pahefana tamin'ny alalan'ny fitifirana amin'ny bala tena izy, sy baomba mandatsa-dranomaso ireo mpanao fihetsiketsehana mitaky "asa, fahalalahana, ary hambompo-pirenena", maherin'ny 300 ireo mpanao fihetsiketsehana namoy ny ainy ary marobe ihany koa ireo naratra. ||| Authorities responded to the protesters' demands of "employment, freedom, and national dignity" with live bullets, and tear gas, killing more than 300 protesters and injuring many more.
Ny andro nandosiran'ny filoha teo aloha tany Arabia Saodita ||| The day the former president fled to Saudi Arabia
Tamin'ny 14 Janoary 2011, mpanao fihetsiketsehana an-jatony no nitangorona teo ivelan'ny tranoben'ny minisiteran'ny Atitany ao an-drenivohitr'i Tonizia. ||| On January 14, 2011, thousands of protesters gathered outside the building of the Interior Ministry in the capital Tunis.
Niantsoantso ireo mpanao fihetsiketsehana hoe "Minisitera mpampihorohoro ny Minisiteran'ny Atitany", sy hoe 'Mialà Ben Ali." ||| The protesters were chanting "Interior Ministry is a Terrorist Ministry", and "Ben Ali Get Out."
Niafara tamin'ny fampiasan-kerin'ny polisy nanaparitaka ireo mpanao fihetsiketsehana anefa ny hetsika izay natomboka tao anatin'ny filaminana. ||| The demonstration which started peaceful, ended up with police violently dispersing protesters.
Ny harivan'iny andro iny ihany, dia nandositra any Jeddah, ao Arabia Saodita i Ben Ali. ||| Later on the same day, Ben Ali fled to Jeddah, Saudi Arabia.
Polisy mampiasa baomba mandatsa-dranomaso hanaparitahana ireo mpanao fihetsiketsehana manoloana ny Minisiteran'ny Atitany tamin'ny 14 Janoary. ||| Police use tear gas to disperse protesters outside the Interior Ministry on January 14.
Lasa ny mpanao didy jadona, fa manao ahoana kosa ny fitondrana jadona? ||| The dictator is gone, but what about dictatorship?
Hetsi-panoherana ny governemanta vonjimaika tarihin'i Mohamed Ghannouchi, namana akaiky an'i Ben Ali ihany, tamin'ny 25 Febroary. ||| Protest against interim government presided by Mohamed Ghannouchi, a close ally of Ben Ali, on February 25.
Iray andro taty aoriana, nametra-pialàna i Ghannouchi. ||| One day later, Ghannouchi resigned.
Nanapa-kevitra ny hanadino ny lasa rehetra ny Toniziana, ary tsy nitsahatra ny tolona ho amin'ny demokrasia raha tsy nitsoaka tao amin'ny firenena i Ben Ali. ||| Tunisians were keen to cut all ties with the past, and the battle for democracy in Tunisia, did not stop with Ben Ali fleeing the country.
Kianjan'i Kasbah, toerana misy ny minisitera, nanjary ivon-toerana fanaovana fihetsiketsehana sy sit-in, nampiasaina ho fandrodànana ny fitondrana teo aloha izay nankahalaina tanteraka (izay efa nihongana ankehitriny), ny RCD (amin'ny fanalavana azy amin'ny teny frantsay hoe Le Rassemblement Constitutionnel Démocratique, Fivondronann'ny mpiaro ny lalampanorenana Demokratika), izay voarohirohy tamin'ny resaka kolikoly sy ny fanararaotana (tsindry hazo lena). ||| Kasbah square, where the Cabinet building is located, became an epicenter of sit-ins and protests, which sought to overthrow the so hated former ruling party (now dissolved), the RCD (from its French acronym Le Rassemblement Constitutionnel Démocratique, Constitutional Democratic Rally in English), which was associated with corruption and oppression.
Fifidianana demokratika voalohany ||| First democratic election
Mpifidy milahatra handatsa-bato. ||| Voters lining up to vote.
Tamin'ny 23 Oktobra 2011, no kihon-dalana ho an'i Tonizia. ||| October 23, 2011, was a turning point for Tunisia.
Niandry ora maro ireo mpifidy handatsa-bato, nandritra ny fifidianana malalaka sy madio voalohany tamin'ilay antsoina hoe Lohataona Arabo. ||| Voters waited for hours to elect their representatives, in the first free and fair election of the so called Arab Spring.
Firoboroboan'ny Islamista ||| Rise of Islamists
Sora-baventy misoratra hoe: "Fitoviana sy Fahamarinana ho an'ny Toniziana rehetra". ||| Banner reads: "Equality and justice for all Tunisians".
Tamin'ny 21 Novambra 2011, hetsika teo anoloan'ny antenimieram-pirenena. ||| November 21, 2011, in a protest outside the assembly.
Salan'isa 41 isan-jato no vato azon'ny antoko Islamista Ennahdha, ary nahazo seza 89 tamin'ireo 217 tao amin'ny antenimieran-dalampanorenana koa izy. ||| The Islamist party Ennahdha won 41 per cent of the votes, and gained 89 out of 217 seats at the constituent assembly.
Ho an'ny liberaly kosa, matahotra ny firoboroboan'ny Islamista ao Tonizia ny tanjaky ny laika ao amin'ny firenena, sy ny zon'ny vehivavy Toniziana, lazaina fa mandroso indrindra ao amin'ny faritra Arabo. ||| For liberals, the rise of Islamists in Tunisia, is a threat to the secular values of the state, and Tunisian women's rights, considered as the most advanced in the Arab region.
Moncef Marzouki - Filohan'ny Repoblika Vaovao ||| Moncef Marzouki - New President of the Republic
Moncef Marzouki, filoha vaovao ao Tonizia. ||| Moncef Marzouki, new president of Tunisia.
Tamin'ny 22 Desambra, nifidy ilay mpiaro ny zon'olombelona, Moncef Marzouki ny Antenimieran-dalampanorenana, efa nogadraina izy io, ary nalefa sesintany nandritra ny fitondran'i Ben Ali, toy ny filohan'ny Repoblika Toniziana vaovao. ||| On December 12, the national constituent assembly elected human rights activist Moncef Marzouki, who was imprisoned, and exiled under Ben Ali's regime, as the new President of the Republic of Tunisia.
Satria mifarana ny taona, mbola mitohy hatrany ny hetsika sy ny sit-in ho amin'ny demokrasia, ny asa, ary ny hambompo-pirenena ao Tonizia, toy ny adihevitra mafana mikasika ny Antenimieran-dalampanorenana, sy ny governemanta vonjimaika tarihin'i Hamadi Jebali (avy amin'ny antoko Ennahdha) mandray ny asany. ||| As the year comes to an end, protests and sit-ins for democracy, employment, and dignity continue in Tunisia, as heated debates sweep the national constituent assembly, and an interim government presided by Hamadi Jebali (from Ennahdha) takes up duties.
Araho hatrany ny fitantarana mikasika ny Tonizia amin'ny 2012. ||| Stay tuned for more Tunisia coverage in 2012.
Iran: Mitsikia, Mamaky Ny Mailakao Ny Fitondrana ||| Iran: Smile, the Regime is Reading Your Emails
Nitombo isa ireo mpamaham-bolongana Iraniana nanambara ny tebitebiny rehefa nandre fa ny fitoera-mailaka Gmail dia mety ho boky mivelatra hovakian'ny fitondrana Iraniana ary nokendreny tamin'izany ireo mpisintaka tato anatin'ny roa volana izay. ||| A growing number of Iranian bloggers expressed their anxieties after learning that their Gmail inboxes may have been an open book for the Iranian state to read and target dissidents for the last two months.
Fanamarinana SSL mpisovoka iray no ampanaovina "sonia" nomerika hidirana ao amin'ny HTTPS ny vohikala Google rehetra, ary noforonina orinasa Holandey antsoina hoe DigiNotar izy io tamin'ny 10 jolay. ||| The rogue SSL certificate is used to digitally "sign" HTTPS connections to any Google site and was issued by a Dutch company called DigiNotar on July 10.
Ireo mpisintaka ara-politika izay nametrka ny finoany tamin'ny rafitra Google noho ny fiarovana ananany no tratran'ity fitsofohana ity ||| In particular, political dissidents who put their trust in Google's systems for their security may have been targeted in the attack.
Google nihetsika tamin'ny 29 Aogositra: ||| Google reacted on August 29, 2011, saying:
Androany izahay nahazo tatitra fisian'ilay fanafihana MITM (Lehilahy eo Afovoany) amin'ny alalan'ny fampiasana fanamarinana SSL ny mpisera Google, ary avy amin'izany no iezahan'ny sasany miditra eo anelanelan'ny mpisera sy ny tolotra Google efa misy kaody. Voaaro amin'io fisovohana io ny mpisera amin'ny alalan'ny Google Chrome satria nahatratra ny fisian'ilay fanamarinana sandoka ny Chrome. ||| Today we received reports of attempted SSL man-in-the-middle (MITM) attacks against Google users, whereby someone tried to get between them and encrypted Google services... Google Chrome users were protected from this attack because Chrome was able to detect the fraudulent certificate.
Nampitandrina ny fikambanana miaro ny zon'olombelona Arseh Sevom fa nokendrena ihany koa ny Tor, Yahoo ary Mozilla. ||| Human rights organisation, Arseh Sevom warns that Tor, Yahoo and Mozilla are targets too.
Ity ny resaka nifanaovan'i Ali Borhani (mpianatra teknolojian'ny fifandraisana mipetraka any Iran) tamin'ny Google: ||| Here is Ali Borhani's (an Iran-based IT student) conversation with Google:
Mieritreritra aho fa na ny mpanome ny tolotra aterineto na ny governemanta no nanao io fanafihana io (satria mipetraka aty Irao aho ary mety efa renareo ny tantaran'ilay mpisovoka Comodo) ||| I think my ISP or my government did this attack (because I live in Iran and you may hear something about the story of Comodo hacker) !
Iran Online Security nanoratra fa mahita ilay fampitandremana ny mpisera aterineto rehefa mikasa ny hiditra amin'ny Google Docs. ||| Iran Online Security writes that internet users got the warning when they wanted to access their Google Docs.
Raha maro ny mpamaham-bolongana no nanolo-kevitra hahazoana misera milamina sy voaaro tahaka ny fampiasana proxies rehefa hiditra amin'ny imailakany, Nima Rashedan, manampahaizana manokana momba ny fiarovana amin'ny cyber kosa dia namoaka lahatsary manazava amin'ny mpisera Iraniana izay mitranga. ||| While several bloggers offered advice for secure internet use such as using proxies to login to their emails, Nima Rashedan, a cyber security expert, published a video explaining to Iranian users what happened.
Niteny tamiko tamin'ny alalan'ny imailaka i Nima Rashedan fa tsy mahalala ny hagoavan'ity fanafihana ity ny ankamaroan'ny fampitam-baovao Iraniana. ||| Nima Rashedan told me via email that most Iranian media ignored the importance of this attack.
Eo ameplatanan'ny Hackers (mpisovoka) ny tenimiafina, rakitra, tahiry ary indrisy fa tsy voafaritra ho amin'ny Google izany fa efa nokinendry ihany kosa ny Yahoo sy ny Firefox. ||| Hackers got their hands on passwords, files, archives and unfortunately it is not limited to Google, since Yahoo, Firefox were targeted too.
Mbola mangina hatrany ny Diginotar na dia efa tafiditry ny vondrona milaza ny tenany ho "Mpisovoka Iraniana" aza. ||| Diginotar still keeps silent although it was hacked by a group that called itself "Iranian hackers".
Niteny moa i Rashedan fa tsy voavisavisa ny fahapotehana ary tsy azo oharina tamin'ny Fisovohan'i Comodo. ||| Rashedan says the damage is beyond imagination and nothing to compare with Comodo hacking.
Nalefa indray ny fanentanana vaovao hiarovana ny mpisera Iraniana ka misy ahitanay teny toy izao: ||| A new campaign was launched to protect Iranian users where we read:
Ny fanentanana ataonay dia mikendry ny hanaitra ny toe-draharaha mahazo ny mpisera Iraniana, indrindra hatramin'ny nisian'ny raharaha Digitnotar ||| Our campaign is aimed at raising awareness for the dangerous situation for Iranian netizens, especially since the Diginotar scandal.
Filipina: Tsy Voasakan'ny Governemanta Ny 'Noynoying' ||| Philippines: Government Fails to Stop 'Noynoying'
Izay natomboka ho solon'ny fomba fihetsi-panoherana efa voarara planking (mihohoka sahala amin'ny hazofisaka) ankehitriny dia lasa manaitaitra tokoa any Philippines. ||| What started as a substitute to the now banned planking protests is now the latest hit sensation in the Philippines.
Amin'ny maha-paozim-panoherana azy, ny 'Noynoying' dia mipetraka manodidina fotsiny, mitsilailay amin'ny tany, na mivandravandra amin'ny toerana tsy misy na inona na inona sady tsy manao na inona na inona. ||| As a protest pose, 'Noynoying' simply involves sitting around, lying on the ground, or staring on empty space, and doing nothing.
Namorona ny 'Noynoying' ny mpikatroka tamin'ny voalohany hanazavana ny tsy fihetsehan'ny Filoha Noynoy Aquino amin'ny fahalafosan'ny menaka (solika), mbamin'ny sara sy ny fandaniana hafa momba ny fampianarana, ary ny fahalafosan'ny entam-barotra ilaina andavanandro sy ny servisy isan-karazany, fitomboan'ny elanelana sy ny fahantrana ankoatra ny hafa (tsy voatanisa). ||| Activists first coined 'Noynoying' to describe Philippine President Noynoy Aquino's inaction on the soaring prices of oil, tuition and other school fees, and other basic goods and services, rising inequality, and poverty, among others.
Tsy Voasakan'ny Governemanta Ny Noynoying ||| Government fails to stop Noynoying
Nandamòka avokoa ny ezaka rehetra nataon'ny Governemanta hanakanana ny lazan'ny 'Noynoying'. ||| Government efforts to stop the growing popularity of 'Noynoying' have all failed miserably.
Vao maika mihamalaza kokoa ny voambolana rehefa namoaka sary ahitana ny Filoha heverina ho "miasa" ny tao an-dapa entina hanoherana ny fiampangana ny 'Noynoying'. ||| The term became even more popular after the Palace released several photos showing the president supposedly "at work" to counteract the charges of 'Noynoying'.
Tonga dia be be ny nanao photoshop azy ireny ary nampakatra azy an-tserasera ho meme an'aterineto. ||| These were quickly photoshopped and uploaded online as Internet memes.
nalaza tamin'ny herintaona rehefa nanamboamboatra ny sarindry zareo ry zareo mba entina hanehoana hoe "miasa" eo amin'ny helodranon'i Manila ry zareo rehefa nopotehin'ny rivodoza. ||| The latest 'Noynoying' images showed the president together with Department of Public Works and Highways officials who also became notorious last year after they edited photos of themselves to make it appear that they were "working" on a Manila Bay wall destroyed by a typhoon.
Indreto ho ohatra sasantsasany amin'ny meme noynoying mivezivezy amin'ny aterineto: ||| Here are some samples of noynoying memes now circulating on the Internet:
Ny 'Noynoying' moa amin'izao fotoana izao dia manana fidirana manokana ao amin'ny Wikipedia, izay niainga tamin'ny andininy fohy ka nihalava nihalava lasa lohahevitra lehibe mamakafaka ny niavian'ny voambolana. ||| 'Noynoying' now has its own entry in Wikipedia, which has expanded from a simple one short paragraph description to a lengthy treatise on the origin of the term.
Mihamalaza ny Noynoying ||| On Noynoying's growing popularity
Noraisina avy amin'ny anaram-bositry ny Filoha Noynoy, noraisin'ny daholobe amin'ny ankapobeny ho tsy fanaovana na inona na inona manoloana ny zavatra mila atao haingana ny voambolana 'noynoying'. ||| Taken from the president's nickname Noynoy, 'Noynoying' has been widely embraced by the public to mean doing nothing in the face of pressing matters that need action.
Efa nifampiresaka tamin'ny antony nampalaza ny 'Noynoying' amin'izao fotoana ny mpiserasera Filipino. ||| Filipino netizens have been discussing why 'Noynoying' gained its present popularity.
Ny mpikambana ao amin'ny governemantan'i Aquino miantso ny noynoying ho doka (fanaratsiana) kely "annoying" na mahasorena ataon'ny mpitsikera ny fitondrana. ||| A member of the Aquino regime's cabinet called Noynoying an "annoying" publicity gimmick by government critics:
Karazana fampielezan-kevitra fanohizana ny fanaratsiana ambadika ataon'ny fahavalo ara-politikan'ny fitondrana io. ||| It is a sub-plot to a more prolonged campaign against the government by its political enemies.
Satria sahirana amin'ny famelezana ny politikan'ny governemanta ry zareo dia enjehina manokana ny Prezidà Noy, milaza ny toe-tsainy ny fidinanana ambany dia ambany toy izany. ||| Because these people are having a hard time attacking government policies, they resort to ad hominem attacks on President Noy, stooping so low as to question his mental condition.
Bilaogera Teo Marasigan mamaly fa tsy asana mpikatroka vitsivitsy monja io fiakaran-dazan'ny noynoying io. ||| Blogger Teo Marasigan replies that the rise of Noynoying is not just the work of a few activists:
Malaza ny Noynoying satria izay no mamehy ny fahatsapan'ny olona momba ny filoha. ||| Noynoying became popular because it summed up the sentiments of the people about the president.
Ao ambadiky ny tsiky sy ny fampanantenana mamy ataon'ny filoha dia ny faharatsian'ny fahantrana sy ny hanoanana no tsapan'ny olona kokoa. ||| Behind the happy smiles and sweet promises of the president, the worsening poverty and hunger are felt by the people.
John Marcel Ragaza mandritra izany fotoana izany mamahana bolongana fa mety mahasorena (annoying) ny filoha sy ny manampahefana miaraka aminy ny 'Noynoying' fa tsy vitavitan'ny hoe fanenjehana manokana ny filoha. ||| John Marcel Ragaza meanwhile blogs that Noynoying, annoying as it maybe for the president and his officials, is not just an attack on the president's person.
Mari-panoherana mihoatra noho ny fitsikerana ny toetran'ny filoha ny noynoying. ||| Noynoying is a symbolic protest that goes beyond criticism of the president's character.
Tsy tokony ho diso fandray (fandika) ny noynoying, na izay fomba fanoherana miforona mitovitovy amin'izany, ho famelezana manokana ny tenan'i Aquino na ny olona eny fa na Malacanang aza. ||| The public and even Malacanang should not misconstrue Noynoying, and any act of creative protest for that matter, as a plain assault to person of Aquino.
Ompa amin'ny fomba fitondrana tsy nataon'i Aquino irery fa nataon'ireo teo alohany ihany koa, (ompa) amin'ny fitondran'ny vato nasondrotry ny tany nanjakazaka nandritra ny fotoana maharitra, amin'ny fomba fitarihana ny izay manampy trotraka ny fijalian'ny Filipino natao anjorombala ho fiarovana ny tombontsoan'ny vato nasondrotry ny tany. ||| Rather, it is an insult directed at the kind of governance that is being espoused not only by Aquino but even by his predecessors, to the elite rule that has long dominated the country, to a leadership that sadly contributes to the suffering of marginalized Filipinos through the protection of elite interests.
matoanteny manintona ny noynoying, fa manindrona sy manohina satria manambara zavatra marina. ||| Noynoying is just a catchy verb, but it nevertheless pierces and offends because it is truthful.
Any amin'ny andalana ambany indrindra amin'ny fifikiran'ny 'Noynoying', araka ny tsikaritr'i Like a Rolling Stone, ny tsy iraharahian'ny fitondrana Aquino ny raharaha manahirana ny vahoaka. ||| The bottom line for the endurance of Noynoying, Like a Rolling Stone observes, is the Aquino government's willful disregard for people's issues:
Hita ho miaina any amin'ny tontolo hafa i Aquino sy ny manampahefana miaraka aminy, any amin'ny toerana izay tsy ahitana afa-tsy olona faly mpandeha eny amin'ny tranombarotra, tsara ny mariky ny tsenam-bola ary betsaka ny toerana an-dalampananganana zavatra goavana izay mampiseho ny fitomboan-karena. ||| It is Aquino and his officials who appear to be living in a different world, a place where there are only happy mall-goers, rosy stock market indices and busy construction sites that point to economic growth.
Ao amin'io tontolo io, tsy olana ny vidin'ny menaka (solika) na dia lafo sahala amin'inona aza. ||| In this world, oil prices are not a problem no matter how high they get.
Foronina izany tsy fisian'asa izany ary toe-tsaina ny fahantrana. ||| Poverty is just a state of mind and unemployment is fiction.
Farany indrindra, mpitarika mpikatroka tanora Vencer Crisostomo namoaka lisitra ny dingana mivaingana azon'ny fitondrana Aquino atao, ankoatra ny famoahana sary sy fandavana isan-karazany hampiatoana ny fiampangana ho manao noynoying: ||| Lastly, youth activist leader Vencer Crisostomo lists down some concrete steps that the Aquino regime can do, instead of mere photo releases and denials, to stop accusations of Noynoying:
Mampitsahatra ny fiakaran'ny menaka (solika?), mametraka fanaovaozana ny fizakan-tany tena izy, mampakatra mazava ny karama, mampiato ny fiakaran'ny saram-pianarana sy ny fandaniana mifandraika aminy, mampitsahatra ny fandikàna ny zon'olombelona, manohitra ny fitsabahan'i Etazonia, ary mamarana ny fandrobàna sy ny fitrandrahana ataon'ny vahiny amin'ny harena voajanahary, ankoatra izay tsy voatanisa. ||| Stopping oil price hikes, implementing genuine land reform, significantly raising wages, imposing a moratorium on tuition and other school fee increases, ending impunity and human rights abuses, standing up against US intervention, and ending foreign plunder and mining of the country's natural resources, among many others.

Ireo Palestiniana Mpihazakazaky ny Fahafahana ||| Palestinian Freedom Riders
Naka tàhaka ireo hazakazaka ho an'ny fahafahana tamin'ny 1963 tany Etazonia izay nanoherana ny fanavakavahana ara-bolon-koditra io hetsika io. ||| The movement was modeled following the 1963 freedom rides in the United States against racial segregation.

Etazonia: Miverina Indray Occupy Wall Street Na Bodoy Wall Street ||| United States: Occupy Wall Street Returns
Maro ny olona no mifanontany amin'ny ho avin'ny Occupy Wall Street na Bodoy Wall Street taorian'ny nanesorana an-dry zareo tao amin'ny Zuccotti Park sy ny faharatsian'ny andro tsy ahafahan'ny mpibodo hilasy eny ivelany tamin'ny ririnina teo. ||| Many people were questioning Occupy Wall Street's future after the eviction from Zuccotti Park and the harsh weather conditions which prevented the occupiers from camping out last winter.
Saingy lazain'ny mpibodo fa tsy nanjavona mihitsy ny hetsika ary tapa-kevitra hibodo ny toera-malalaka manerana ny firenena, tahaka ny efa ataon-dry zareo eo amin'ny Union Square (Kianjan'ny Sendikà?) ao New York City. ||| However, according to the occupiers themselves, the movement never disappeared and they are now determined to occupy public spaces around the country, just as they have done already in Union Square in New York City.

Natsangana tamin'ny 15 Febroary ny blaogy bitika antsoina hoe 99% Spring, izay anasan'ny fikambanana eo ho eo amin'ny 40 naka aingam-panahy avy amin'ny Occupy nanasa olona manodidina ny 100.000 amin'izao faraparan'ny fotoan-ketra any Etazonia izao hiresaka "ny tantaran'ny toekarentsika" manomboka ny 9 ka hatramin'ny 15 Avrily. ||| On February 15, 2012, a microblog titled 99% Spring was set up, in which approximately 40 organizations inspired by Occupy invited around 100,000 people on the eve of the tax period in the United States to tell "the story of our economy" from April 9-15.
Efa niantso hanaovana diabe niainga avy teny afovoan'i Manhattan ho any amin'ny Wall Street ihany koa ny mpibodo tamin'ny 1 mey. ||| The occupiers have also called for a march from the centre of Manhattan to Wall Street on May 1.
Nirodorodo tokoa ny fipoiran'ny hetsika Bodoy indray ka nandresy tamin'ny firotsaha-kofidiana tao amin'ny Kongresy ny iray tamin'ny mpikambana amin'izy ireo tany Philadelphia. ||| The resurgence of the Occupy movement has been so impressive that one of its members in Philadelphia almost won a candidature for Congress.
Nahatsikaritra ny fipoirana indray ny tontolom-bolongana. ||| The blogosphere has noticed the resurgence.
Mametraka ny bolongana Indignant Feminists fa nihanatanjaka kokoa ny hetsika Bodoy tamin'ny alalan'ny fandraisana anjaran'ny vehivavy: ||| The blog Indignant Feminists states that the Occupy movement has become stronger through the participation of women:
Aty amin'ny ilabolantany avaratra, ohatra, navitrika ny vehivavy tamin'ny fandraisana anjara hanombohana ny hetsika Bodoy. ||| Here in the Northern Hemisphere, for example, women were active participants in starting the Ocuppy movement.
Saingy, tahaka ny tsikaritra ho ny lehilahy no tena betsaka ao amin'ity hetsika ity (ary tanora sy fotsy hoditra ny ao Etazonia) - sy ny tsy dia firaharahiana loatra ny zavamisy marina hoe tsy afa-miova ny kapitalisma raha tsy ny fototra ao aminy no donina: fanjakazakan'ny ray, izay miankina amin'ny fanaraha-maso sy ny fampiasana ny vehivavy. ||| However, this movement has given the impression of being predominantly masculine (and in the United States, young and white) - as well as indifferent to the fact that capitalism cannot simply be transformed without challenging its foundations: patriarchy, which depends upon the control and exploitation of women.
Ary ny vehivavy no mandrafitra ny 51% amin'ny 99% (ary 0% amin'ny 1%). ||| And women, by the way, make up 51% of that 99% (and 0% of the 1%).
Nasongadin'ny bolongana Maestroviejo fa natsangana teo amin'ny fiafaran'ny taona 2011 sy fanombohan'ny taona 2012 tany Minneapolis ny hetsika Bodoy: ||| Maestroviejo points out that the Occupy movement was also launched in Minneapolis towards the end of 2011 and the beginning of 2012:
Nandritra ny mihitsan-dravina sy ny ririnina, nanao hetsika tany amin'ny toerana samihafa tao Minneapolis tamin'ny alalan'ny fananganana tranolay ny mpanao fihetsiketsehana. ||| During the autumn and winter, the protestors made protests in various parts of the city of Minneapolis by pitching their tents.
Tohin'ireny hetsika ireny, niezaka ny handrara ny fidirana ao amin'ny toby amin'ny alina ny polisim-panjakana amin'ny alina ary manaisotra ny tranolain'ny mpandray anjara. ||| Following these protests, the State police forces stepped up their efforts to restrict entry to the camp at night and to remove the participants' tents.
Mitsipaka ny filazan-kevitra hoe nandamoka Hetsika Bodoy ny mpisera tsy nitonona anarana iray ao amin'ny Twitter: ||| On Twitter, Anonymous refutes the idea that the Occupy movement has failed:
Eritrereto ho tsy nahomby hoe ity Occupy ity? ||| Think Occupy has failed?
niova tanteraka ankehitriny ny fomba fiteny sy ny lantom-peo iresahana ny toekarena sy ny WallStreet noho IO hetsika IO ||| The entire rhetoric and tone used to discuss the economy and Wall Street are now different because of THAT movement.
Namoaka kapila ho fanomezam-boninahitra ny hetsika Occupy i Daltonicum: ||| Daltonicum notes that there is even a discographic production in honour of the Occupy movement:
Namoaka kapila mangilatra mitondra ny lohateny hoe "Occupy this Album" niarahana nanantontosa tamin'ny tarika tahaka an'i Mogwai ny hetsika "Occupy Wall Street" ||| The "Occupy Wall Street" movement has recorded a CD titled "Occupy this Album" with the collaboration of bands such as Mogwai
Jason Brickley nanoso-kevitra fa hiroborobo indray ny hetsika: ||| Jason Brickley suggests that the movement is flourishing once again:
Fifohazana Lohataona: mitady ny hahatanora ny hetsika indray ny Occupy Wall Street ||| Spring Revival: Occupy Wall Street Seeks to Rejuvenate Movement
Nalaina avy amin'ny hetsika Occupy tao New York City ireto manaraka ireto (nalain'ny mpanoratra daholo izy ireto): ||| The following images are of the Occupy movement in New York City (all photos were taken by the author):
Brezila: fahatsiarovana an'i Ayrton Senna, Tompondaka F1 tsy nety resy ||| Brazil: Remembering Ayrton Senna, the unbeatable F1 champion
Velona tsy mety resy, maty tsy misy mahasolo voasolo", hoy ny iray amin'ireo vohikala maro mahatsiaro ilay intelo tompondaka erantany tamin'ny Formule 1, ary nanohina an'i Brezila sy izao tontolo izao ny fahafatesany tamin'ny voalohan'ny volana mey 1994. ||| In life unbeatable, in death irreplaceable", says one of the many websites paying homage to the three-time Formula One world champion whose death, on May 1st 1994, shocked Brazil and the world.
Nitari-dalana nandritra ny Grand Prix de San Marino 1994, tsy nahafehy ny fiara nentiny i Senna ka nampisosa azy teo amin'ny fiolahan'i Tamburello. ||| Leading the 1994 San Marino Grand Prix, Senna lost control of his car and left the track at the Tamburello curve.
Niteraka alahelo lehibe teo amin'ny mpankafy azy ny fahafatesany,raha vao 34 taona monja izy ka mbola isaonany hatrany 15 taona aty aoriana. ||| His death, at just 34-years-old, has been mourned by fans throughout the country 15 years on.
"Raha sanatria tratran'ny lozam-piarakodia mety hiantraika amin'ny aiko aho, iriko raha tonga dia maty aho. ||| "If I ever happen to have an accident that eventually costs me my life, I hope it is in one go.
Tsy tiako ny hotarihina amin'ny seza misy kodiarana. ||| I would not like to be in a wheelchair.
Tsy tiako ny hijalijaly any amin'ny hopitaly amin'ny karazan-dratra na voina rehetra. ||| I would not like to be in a hospital suffering from whatever injury it was.
Raha mbola miaina aho, dia aleoko miaina izany manontolo, feno sy mavitrika, satria olona mavitrika aho. ||| If I'm going to live, I want to live fully, very intensely, because I am an intense person.
Manimba ny fiainako raha miaina tapatapany aho." ||| It would ruin my life if I had to live partially".
Ny anaran'i Ayrton Senna amin'izao fotoana izao no anisan'ny be mpametraka indrindra ao amin'ny Andavanandro breziliana ao amin'ny Twitter. ||| Ayrton Senna's name was among the most popular tags today on the Brazilian timeline on Twitter.
Biellebrunner ohatra namoaka sary iray mampiseho ny famangiana nataony teo amin'ny tsangambato teo amin'ny toerana nahafatesan'i Senna, teo amin'ny fiolahan'i Tamburello. ||| Biellebrunner publishes a photo of a visit she had paid to the monument built on the spot Senna died, on the the Tamburello curve.
Vinicius Cordeiro tamin'ny fiandohan'ny herinandro no iray tamin'ny nahatsiaro ny fahafatesany voalohany tamn'ity taona ity. ||| At the beginning of the week, Vinicius Cordeiro was one of the first people to remember the sad anniversary this year.
Feno ny foko isaky ny manatona ny voalohan'ny volana mey: taona iray hafa tsy misy an'i Ayrton Senna indray... nanatrika ny hazakazaka aho tamin'iny fotoana iny. ||| Every time we get close to May 1st my hearts sinks: another year without Ayrton Senna... I was watching that race.
Tsy irery i Cordeiro mijery fahitalavitra indray alahady izay maizina indrindra teo amin'ny tantaran'i Brezila. ||| Cordeiro was not alone in front of the television on the Sunday that became known in Brazil as the blackest race in history.
Nahita ny fahafatesan'ilay Aotrishiana Roland Ratzenberger i Imola iray andro monja mialoha ny loza nahazo an'i Senna. ||| Imola also saw the death of Austrian race driver Roland Ratzenberger just a day before Senna's accident.
Tsy misy very ao amin'ny fahatsiarovan'ny olona maro ny sary, ny fialan'aina, ny hirifiry niainana. ||| The images, the anguish, the pain are still fresh in many people's memories.
Hoy i Guilherme Tsubota mahatsiahy ity andro mahory ity: ||| Guilherme Tsubota recalls that fatal day:
Andro ratsy indrindra tamin'ny fiainako ny fahafatesany, izay indrisy nifanandrify indrindra tamin'ny vaninandro ahatsiarovana ny nahaterahan'ny reniko. ||| The day of his death, which was also my mother's birthday by an unfortunate coincidence, was one of the worst days I have lived.
Tsaroako ny fahataitairana sy ny fitokisana fa amin'ity Loka lehiben'i Imola ity, dia hahasongona ilay "Rainiboto" i Ayrton, ary araka ny mahazatra dia nifoha maraina aho hijery ny fifaninanana. ||| I remember the excitement and the certainty that from that Imola Grand Prix on, Ayrton would turn the tables on the "German", and as usual I woke up early to watch the race.
nipetraka teo amin'ny sezalava aho nandritra ny tontolo andro, nanaraka ny sombim-baovao rehetra tamim-pahagagana. ||| I sat on the couch and stayed there the rest of the day, following astonishingly every piece of news.
Aniveriseran'ny vahiny? ||| The birthday guests?
Tsy nahare izay fahatongavana na fahalasanan'ny hafa aho, tsy tadidiko akory ho niresaka taman'olona aza aho. ||| I didn't see anyone coming or leaving, I don't recall having spoken to anybody.
Ny hany tsaroako dia ny sary sy ny tantara navoakan'ny Globo TV broadcast momba ny loza nahazo an'i Senna. ||| I just remember the images and stories that Globo TV broadcast about Senna's accident.
Niditra ho tantara ny andro manaraka, ary nahatsiaro izay rehetra niaina tamin'iny fotoana iny, indrindra ny avy any São Paulo, hoe tahaka ny ahoana ny niatoan'ny tanàna ho fanajana azy. ||| The following days entered into history, and anyone from that generation, especially those from São Paulo, remember how the town stopped to honor him.
Tena nahavariana, zavatra tsy mbola hitako mihitsy nialoha io fotoana io. ||| It was impressive, something I had never seen before.
"Any andro iray, mandritra ny toe-javatra iray, mieritreritra ianao fa manam-petra. ||| "On a given day, a given circumstance, you think you have a limit.
Ary dia manatratra io fetra io ianao ka tratranao izany, dia hoy ianao, 'Okay, hatreto ny fetra. ||| And you then go for this limit and you touch this limit, and you think, 'Okay, this is the limit.
raha vao tratranao io fetra io, dia misy zava-mitranga ary dia mbola afa-mihoatra kely tampoka ianao. ||| As soon as you touch this limit, something happens and you suddenly can go a little bit further.
Miaraka amin'ny herintsainao, fikirizanao, herimponao sy ny traikefanao mazava loatra, dia afa-misidina avo ianao" ||| With your mind power, your determination, your instinct, and the experience as well, you can fly very high"
Nanararaotra nahatsiaro ny rainy izay fan(ina) an'i Senna sady misy fifanandrifian-javatra mahagaga mampanakaiky ny rainy amin'ny maherifony i Eduardo P.L. ||| Eduardo P.L takes the opportunity to remember his father, who was a fan of Senna and whose faith, in another series of amazing coincidences, brought him very close to his hero.
Ho an'ity mpamaham-bolongana ity dia kamban'alahelo no iainany: ||| For the blogger, this is a time of double sadness:
Indray Asabotsy, 15 taona lasa izay, teo ampisakafoanana tao amin'ny restaurant iray no naharay antso nilaza fa maty ny raiko! ||| On a Saturday, 15 years ago, I was having lunch in a restaurant when I received a phone call telling me that my dad had died!
Nankany an-tokatranon'ny ray aman-dreniko aho, dia nandevina an'i dokotera Santo izaho sy ny reniko, ny mpiray tampo amiko, namana sy olompantatra vitsivitsy. ||| I went to my parents' flat, and with my mother, siblings, a few friends and relatives, we buried Dr. Santo.
Tonga ny alahady, izany hoe andro iray taty aoriana, maty i Senna. ||| On Sunday, so a day later, Senna died.
Raha heverina, fifanandrifian-javatra mampalahelo. ||| So far, only a sad coincidence.
Herinandro taty aoriana dia tonga teto Brezila ny razana, ary taorian'ny fiandrasam-paty dia nalevina teo anilan'ny fasan-draiko izy, miray tokotanim-pasana ry zareo. ||| A week after the body arrived in Brazil, and after the vigil he was buried besides my father's grave in the same cemetery.
Na aiza na aiza misy azy ireo, miara-dalana izy ireo tahaka izay notadiavin'ny raiko. ||| Wherever they are, they are together as my father would like it to be.
Ricardo Vieira no manazava ny tsy fahafaha-mionon'ny olona anarivoarivony teo ampahalasanan'i Senna: ||| Ricardo Vieira explains how Senna's death has left millions disconsolate:
Namela olona an'arivoarivony, ary anisany aho, ho kamboty ny fifaliany, ny ohatry ny fiainany, ny asany sy ny fahazotoany ary ny ngeza indrindra tamin'ny hatsarany dia ny fanetretenany i Senna tamin'ity alahady tsy azo nivalozana ity. ||| On that fateful Sunday, Senna left millions of people including me orphaned of his joys, of his example of life, his work and professional determination and of the greatest of his qualities: his humility.
15 taona no lasa, fa nasehon'ny Birao Breziliana misahana ny antotanisa sy ny fitsapana ny hevitry ny olona fa i Ayrton Senna hatrany no be mpankafy indrindra eny fa na dia ho an'ireo taranaka taty aoriana tsy nahalala azy fahavelony sy nanaraka ny asany aza: manakaiky ny 400 ny tanora anelanelan'ny 15 ka hatramin'ny 19 taona no saiky niteny avokoa fa i Senna no mpanao fanatanjahantena ankafiziny indrindra. ||| Fifteen years on, a recent poll by the Brazilian Institute of Public Opinion and Statistics shows that Ayrton Senna is still the biggest idol even for a younger generation that did not get to know him alive or follow his career: among nearly 400 people aged between 15 and 19, most said Senna was their biggest sporting idol.
Tahaka an'i Pele, dia nanome faharisihana ny Breziliana hanana fanajana eo amin'ny sehatra iraisam-pirenena i Senna. ||| Like Pele, Senna made Brazilians feel they could achieve international respect.
Eo anatrehan'izany dia mino i Alan Ferraz fa ny lova tsara indrindra napetrak'i Senna dia ny nahafahan'ny Breziliana mirehareha. ||| Considering this, Alan Ferraz believes Senna's greatest legacy was the way he made Brazilians proud of themselves.
Mihetsi-po izy eo am-pahatsiarovana azy: ||| He feels moved to remember him:
Tsy tanako ny ranomasoko eto ampanoratana, na dia 15 taona aty aoriana aza. ||| While writing this post I could not hold the tears back, even after 15 years.
Mino aho fa ho tahaka izany avokoa ny fahatsapan'ireo tia Formula 1 sy ankona (toy ny voatsatok'antsy) tamin'ny fahalasanan'ilay tompondakanay mandrakizay. ||| I believe that this feeling happens to all those who love Formula 1 and were stabbed by destiny with the departure of our eternal champion.
Ho fahatsiarovana mipetraka mandrakizay ao an-tsain'ny rehetra tsy nahenoana ny hira manakoako manao hoe: "Ayrton, Ayrton, AYRTON SENNA DO BRASIL" intsony ny ampitso ny voalohan'ny volana mey 1994. ||| May 1st 1994 will be forever in the minds of everyone who after that day could no longer hear the chanting: Ayrton, Ayrton, AYRTON SENNA DO BRASIL.
"Ao anatin'ny rako ny mifaninana mihazakazaka (fiarakodia). ||| "Racing, competing, is in my blood.
Anisan'ny tenako, anisan'ny fiainako; io hatrany no ataoko mandritra ny fiainako. ||| It's part of me, it's part of my life; I've been doing it all my life.
Ary io no voalohandaharana mialoha ny zavatra hafa rehetra" ||| And it stands up before anything else"
Asehon'ny gazety ho miavonavona sy mpihatakataka, mirona kokoa ho amin'ny fandresena fa tsy amin'ny fiaraha-mientan'ny mpitia fanatanjahantena, nampiady hevitra ihany koa ity mpanamory ity teo anatrehan'ny mpijery. ||| Often portrayed in the press as being cold and aloof, and much more interested in winning than in sportsmanship, the driver was also a quite controversial figure in the eyes of the public.
Nefa samy nahatsapa ny rehetra, ary tafiditra amin'izany ny tsy mpankasitraka azy loatra tahaka an'i Wilton Sturm, fa tsy mbola nisy aloha ny tahaka an'i Senna: ||| But, even those who were not big fans, like Wilton Sturm, say there will never be anyone quite like Senna:
Afa-mirehareha aho raha milaza fa nanatrika ny fandresena rehetra nahatratra 41 nataony. ||| I am proud to say that I watched all 41 of his victories.
Tahaka ny tsapa fa efa nanomboka nanala azy ihany izy, efa niditra tamin'ny fankafizana fahafinaretana ankoatra ny fanapoahana champagne aorian'ny fandresena, dia lasa i Ayrton Senna. ||| It gave the impression that when he finally started to relax a bit, permitting himself to enjoy the pleasure of other things than just the champagne after winnings, Ayrton Senna passed away.
Ankehitriny, banga ny fisiany ary malahelo azy aho. ||| Today, I miss him and regret his absence.
Miezaka aho ny tsy hitsara ny nataony fa hahatsiaro kosa ny zavatra tsara tontosany. ||| I make an effort not to judge his attitude but to remember his beautiful performances.
Tsy tena "Sennist" loatra aho hatramin'izay saingy, tiako kosa ny milaza, fa mandritra ny fifaninanana Formula 1 iray, dia i Ayrton Senna no mahery indrindra tamin'izay hitako hatramin'izay! ||| I was never a super "Sennist" but I like to say that on the track, that's to say, during a Formula 1 race, Ayrton Senna was the best I have ever seen!
Te-hamangy ny fasany aho indray andro any fa tsy fantatro aloha izay fihetseham-poko, fa angamba aho hiteny hoe "misaotra" tamin'ireny fifaninanana goavana ireny, ny fandresena mahafinaritra nasehony ahy! ||| I want to visit his grave one day and I do not know what my reaction will be, but I will probably say "thanks" for the big races, the great overtaking, the great victories he gave me to watch!
Namoaka andian-dahatsoratra manokana ho fahatsiarovana an'i Senna ao anatin'ity voatsonga ity i Ricardo César: ||| wraps up a series of special posts dedicated to Senna with the following quote:
15 taona katroka izay ny fahatsapana fa nilaozana na dia ho an'ireo izay tsy niankim-po taminy aza. ||| There are exactly 15 years since the loss felt even by those who did not root for him.
Misy ny fahatsiarovan'ny olona, tahaka ahy, izay nanaraka ny hazakazaka nataony hatramin'ny fahafolo taonako. ||| There are memories of people who, like me, followed his F1 career from the age of 10.
Sarin'ny fifanandrinana sy fandresena, isa-maraina, isa-tolakandro na isan-kariva. ||| Images of battles and conquests, on mornings, afternoons or late nights.
Fahatsiarovana olona iray izay nitsahatra indray andro tamin'ny fisiana ho olombelona, fa teraka kosa ho angano, angamba ny olomanga efa teraka sahady tao amin'ny firenena iray mitady olona mahery fo. ||| Remembering the one who one day ceased to exist as a man to be reborn as a myth, perhaps the greatest idol already born in a country in need of heroes.
Antsoin'ny hafa hoe 'da Silva' izay tsy kivy mihitsy, tahaka ny Breziliana maro. ||| Another one named 'da Silva' who, as many Brazilians, never give up.
Ho tompondakanay izy mandrakizay. ||| He will forever be our champion.
Misaotra anao Ayrton Senna. ||| Thank you, Ayrton Senna.
Namoaka lahatsarin'ny fotoana tsara indrindra tamin'ny nataon'i Ayrton Senna ny mpampiasa YouTube DONIARIANO, ary nampiarahany tamin'ny hira izay nanakoako isaky ny alahady maraina tany Brezila. ||| YouTube user DONIARIANO has posted the video above highlighting the best moments of Ayrton Senna's career, with the song that was the soundtrack of many Sunday mornings in Brazil.
Mpampiasa hafa koa i MisterLotus1994 namoaka ny lahatsarin'ny Loka Lehibe Belza 1985 izay no tantarain'i Senna tenany tamin'ny teny anglisy. ||| Another user, MisterLotus1994 posts a video about the 1985 Belgian G.P commented on in English by Senna himself.
Ny sary kosa dia nalaina tao amin'ny vohikala AytonSenna.net sady efa azon'ny rehetra isintonana atontankevitra. ||| The photos used in this post were taken from a website which is no longer available.
Rosia: Miady Hevitra Momba ny Teknolojia sy ny Mangarahara ireo Mpitoraka Blaogin'ny Governemanta ao amin'ny Aterineto ||| Russia: E-Gov Blogger Discusses Technology and Transparency
Yekaterina Aksyonova, mpamorona ny gov-gov.ru, iray amin'ireo blaogy mpanome vaovao lehibe indrindra momba ny governemanta amin'ny aterineto any Rosia, dia nihaona vao haingana tamin'ny Global Voices tao amin'ny BarCamp an'i Azia afovoany, ary namaly fanontaniana maromaro momba ny anjara asan'ny teknolojia sy ny fangaraharàna. ||| Yekaterina Aksyonova, creator of gov-gov.ru, one of the most informative blogs about e-government in Russia, met with Global Voices at Central Asian BarCamp recently and answered several questions on the role of technology and transparency.
Aksyonova dia mpandraharaha ho an'ny governemanta ary mpamorona vohikala maro ho an'ny governemanta federaly. ||| Aksyonova is a government contractor and the creator of number of websites for the federal government.
Milazalaza tahaka izao izy momba ny blaoginy sy ny fomba fijeriny ny fangaraharàn'ny governemanta: ||| She describes her blog and her vision of government transparency the following way:
Nuremberg (tanàna Medieval any Baviera, Alemana) dia nanana fomban-drazana mahomby: ny mpikambana rehetra tao amin'ny filankevitry ny tanàna dia nandeha an-tongotra namonjy ny fivorian'ny filankevitra, amin'izay ny olona tsirairay dia afaka mandefa antso manokana ho azy ireo na maneho hevitra momba ny fanapahan-kevitry ny filankevitry ny tanàna. ||| Medieval Nuremberg (a city in Bavaria, Germany) had a useful tradition: all members of the city council were supposed go to the council meetings by foot, so that any citizen could personally pass them an appeal or express an opinion about the city council's decisions.
Ankoatr'izay dia fomba tsara mahasalàma ireo manampahefan'ny tanàna izany. ||| Beside, this tradition was a good way to keep city's officials in shape.
Raha amiko, tokony hiverina hijery ny lalàn'ny tanàna malalak'i Nuremberg ireo vohikalan'ny governemanta. ||| To my mind, government websites should be somewhat returned to the rules of the free city of Nuremberg.
Tsy eritreretiko ho voarain'ny solombavambahoaka sy ny manampahefana ny fanangonan-tsonia rehefa handeha hiasa izy, nefa satria ry zareo koa ao amin'ny aterineto dia mitovy "taranja" amin'ny olom-pireneny ihany izy izay. ||| I doubt whether the deputies and officials would receive petitions while going to work, but since they're on the Internet they are (virtually) on the same "street" as their citizens.
Manamora asa maro ny vohikala tsara ananan'ny governemanta, amin'ny fanomezany eo noho eo ny fanampim-panazavàna ilaina ary manamora ny fanaovana antontan-taratasy isan-karazany aza. ||| Good government websites make a lot of tasks easier, instantly providing much-needed information and even facilitating the execution of various papers.
Ny vohikala ratsy ananan'ny governemanta kosa, na toa inona na toa inona tranga, dia manabaribary ny marina mahamenatra momba ny andrim-panjakana. ||| Bad government websites, at all events, disclose the merciless truth about their institutions.
Rakotra kolikoly ny governemanta Rosiana. ||| Russian government is extremely corrupt.
Araka ny Lisitry ny fahitàna ny kolikoly 2010, fitaovana fampitahàna andaharana ireo firenena araka ny fahitàna kolikoly any amin'ny asam-panjakana, any amin'ny laharana 154 amin'ny 178 no misy an'i Rosia, eo anelanelan'ny Papua New Guinea sy Tajikistan. ||| According to the Corruption Perception Index 2010, a comparative tool to rank countries according to perception of corruption in the public sector, Russia ranks 154 out of 178, standing between Papua New Guinea and Tajikistan.
Naneho ezaka lehibe ireo Rosiana mpampiasa aterineto tamin'ny alalan'ny tetikasa lasitra maro momba ny fangaraharana amin'ny aterineto. ||| Russian netizens have shown a great deal of effort through a number of 'grass-roots' online transparency initiatives.
Vao tsy ela izay ny Rospil.info, vohikala Rosiana miady amin'ny kolikoly, dia nahazo ny loka "Blaogy tsara indrindra" taona 2011 tao amin'ny sokajy "Fampiasana tsara indrindra ny Teknolojia hanatsarana ny fiaraha-monina". ||| Recently Rospil.info, a Russian anti-corruption portal, received the 2011 Best of the Blogs award in the category "Best Use of Technology for Social Good".
Tamin'ny 22 Aprily 2011 dia natomboka koa ny Ny Herin'ny Fianakaviana, tetikasa iray hafa natokana ho an'ny fijerena tavan'olona sy ny kolikoly ao amin'ny governemanta Rosiana. ||| On April 22, 2011, The Power of the Families, another project dedicated to nepotism and corruption in the Russian government was also launched.
